BG-6 Platform
35

Document Purpose: This is the definitive, component-by-component specification for building the MVL Group ERP. Every module, page, tab, button, field, workflow, API integration, and UI element is described in detail. This document serves as the single source of truth for any AI agent, developer, or designer tasked with implementing any part of this system.

Core Philosophy: This ERP does NOT replace Microsoft 365 tools. It works alongside M365 by leveraging every M365 capability through Azure App Registrations and Microsoft Graph API. SharePoint is the document backend. Teams is the collaboration layer. Outlook handles notifications. Power Platform extends functionality. All within the FedRAMP/GCC High security boundary.

§1. System Overview & Architecture

1.1 Platform Identity

  • Name: MVL Group ERP
  • Type: DoD Prime Contractor Enterprise Resource Planning Platform
  • Architecture: All-In-One — 36 Native Capability Engines, No External Dependencies (Replaces Freshservice, Procore, Deltek CostPoint, Oracle Primavera P6, RIB CANDY, PlanSwift, RSMeans, Oracle Aconex, DocuSign, Bluebeam Revu, GovWin IQ, Rippling, Gordian/eGordian)
  • Compliance: CMMC V2 Level 2, NIST 800-171 Rev. 2, FedRAMP Authorization
  • Security Boundary: Single FedRAMP boundary — all data stays within M365 GCC High / Azure Government

1.2 Architecture Principles

  1. Unified Data Model — One source of truth for all modules. No sync conflicts, no mapping tables, no reconciliation between systems. Real-time data across every function.
  2. Single Security Boundary — Single set of NIST 800-171 controls applies everywhere. No gaps from third-party tools lacking FedRAMP authorization or CMMC compliance.
  3. Internal Integration — No external dependencies. Every capability previously served by external tools is built natively. This eliminates integration complexity, reduces security surface area, ensures FedRAMP boundary consistency, and provides a unified user experience.
  4. M365 Symbiosis — Deep native integration with M365 GCC High: actionable email notifications, auto-provisioned Teams channels per project, SharePoint document backend with CUI protection, ERP conversational bot, meeting automation, and M365 Copilot context integration.

1.3 System Architecture Diagram — Layers

BLOCK2179873a50fae9cba2bb4a5cfa8e9719_

1.4 Data Security Zones

Zone Description Examples
Zone 1 — Public Non-CUI / Public Data General HR data, published policies, public vendor information
Zone 2 — Internal Internal business data Database, internal services, admin tools
Zone 3 — CUI/Controlled Controlled Unclassified Information Sensitive project data, financial records, CUI-marked documents
Zone 4 — Perimeter Internet-facing services Internet-facing portal, public APIs

§3. M365 Integration Strategy

Principle: Every M365 service is consumed via Azure App Registrations with appropriate Graph API permissions. The ERP is a first-class M365 citizen, not a replacement.

3.1 App Registration Architecture

BLOCK5e644fbd6c494dd066fc612747d6a8c7_

3.2 Integration Points by M365 Service

Microsoft Outlook (via Graph API)

  • Actionable email notifications with Approve/Reject buttons via Graph API
  • AI Email Classifier extracts structured data from emails
  • Outlook Calendar integration for project milestones and deadlines
  • Email drafting, document summarization, Q&A

Microsoft Teams (via Bot Framework + Graph API)

  • Auto-provisioned Teams team per project with standard channels
  • Real-time alert cards in Teams channels (P1 incidents, budget breaches)
  • ERP conversational bot in Teams (query project status, submit timesheets)
  • Teams Chat & Collaboration integration
  • Meeting automation (CAB agenda, proposal reviews, action item extraction)
  • AI Meeting Secretary transcribes and extracts action items
  • AI Channel Activity Monitor flags inactive critical channels

SharePoint Online (via Graph API)

  • SharePoint as document backend with Purview sensitivity labels for CUI
  • Document transmittal with acknowledgment tracking
  • Version control and document lifecycle management
  • Project Document Repository per project
  • Auto-watermarking: DRAFT, CUI, CONFIDENTIAL, entity logo

OneDrive for Business

  • OneDrive offline sync for field teams with conflict resolution
  • Personal document storage with ERP integration

Power Platform

  • Power BI — Embedded dashboards per role within ERP
  • Power Apps — Custom mobile forms (site safety inspections, visitor registration, warehouse receiving quick-entry)
  • Power Automate — Automated process flows, workflow triggers, RPA
  • Dataverse — Data platform for Power Platform data

Microsoft 365 Copilot

  • AI assistant integrated in M365 apps
  • M365 Copilot context integration for NL queries across ERP data
  • M365 Copilot integration via Graph connectors for NL ERP queries
  • AI Copilot Context Engine enriches responses with ERP data

Microsoft Purview

  • Data classification and sensitivity labels
  • CUI content scanning and auto-labeling
  • DLP policies enforcement

§4. Security & Compliance Framework

14 Core Domains, 110 Practices (CMMC V2.0 Level 2 = NIST SP 800-171 Rev. 2) — All compliant and implemented:

AT Awareness & Training AT.L2-3.2.1, AT.L2-3.2.2, AT.L2-3.2.3
AU Audit & Accountability AU.L2-3.3.1 – 3.3.9

4.2 NIST SP 800-171 Rev. 2 — 14 Security Control Families (110 Requirements)

All 14 families implemented: - Access Control - Awareness & Training - Audit & Accountability - Configuration Management - Identification & Authentication - Incident Response - Maintenance - Media Protection - Personnel Security - Physical Protection - Risk Assessment - Security Assessment - System & Communications Protection - System & Information Integrity

4.3 Security Architecture Components

Component Implementation
Identity Azure AD with MFA, RBAC, PAM
Authentication Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA), Conditional Access Policies
Authorization Role-Based Access Control (RBAC), Segregation of Duties
SSO Single Sign-On via Azure AD / Entra ID
Encryption at Rest AES-256, Transparent Data Encryption (TDE)
Encryption in Transit TLS 1.3
Network Firewalls, DLP, Network Segmentation, WAF
Threat Detection Azure Sentinel (GCC High), Log Analytics workspace, KQL queries
Auto-Response Azure Logic Apps for auto-response
Key Management Azure Key Vault, HSM storage for private keys
Audit Immutable audit storage, 90+ day retention

4.4 FedRAMP Security Boundary

All data stays within the M365 GCC High / Azure Government FedRAMP boundary. No CUI data crosses to non-authorized external systems.

Security Advantages of All-Native Architecture: - Single set of NIST 800-171 controls applies everywhere - No gaps from third-party tools lacking FedRAMP authorization - Reduced security surface area - Unified audit trail across all modules - Consistent CUI handling and DLP enforcement

4.5 Data Classification & Retention Registry

Authority: This registry is the single authoritative reference for data classification and retention across all 26 ERP modules. Every module implementation MUST consult this table to correctly classify record types, apply the appropriate CUI/FCI/PII labels, enforce retention timers, and execute compliant disposition. Regulations enforced: FAR 4.703, NIST SP 800-171 Rev. 2 (AU-11), DFARS 252.204-7012, ITAR (22 CFR 122.5), CMMC V2 Level 2.

4.5.2 Classification Tier Definitions

Tier Label Description Handling Requirement
PUBLIC Public No restriction; sharable externally None
INTERNAL Internal Use Only MVL staff only; no external sharing Access control; no external email
FCI Federal Contract Information Info provided by/generated for the federal government under a contract CUI program basic safeguarding (FAR 52.204-21)
CUI Controlled Unclassified Information Information the government requires to be safeguarded per law/regulation NIST 800-171 full compliance; banner marking required
CUI-PRVCY CUI — Privacy CUI containing personally identifiable information CUI + privacy impact assessment; PII masking in displays
CUI-SP-OPSEC CUI — Specified, OPSEC Security-sensitive CUI requiring strict need-to-know Dual-person rule for access; CISO approval for export
ITAR International Traffic in Arms Regulations Export-controlled technical data or defense articles No foreign national access; export license required; ITAR log
PII Personally Identifiable Information Data that can identify a person GDPR/CCPA compliance; not combinable with non-PII exports

4.5.3 Classification Labeling Automation Rules

  1. CUI Banner Auto-Application: Any record or document tagged CUI/FCI automatically receives: - Top and bottom page banner: CONTROLLED UNCLASSIFIED INFORMATION // Category // Module // MVL GROUP - Microsoft Purview sensitivity label applied to the SharePoint file - Email subject line prepended with CUI when attached to outgoing email

  2. ITAR Auto-Controls: Any record tagged ITAR automatically: - Blocks access by accounts with ForeignNational = true in Azure AD profile - Requires ITAR license number entry before export - Logs every access event to ITAR access log (CISO-only view) - Prepends EXPORT CONTROLLED — ITAR to all generated PDFs

  3. PII Auto-Masking: Any field tagged PII: - Displayed as masked in data tables (e.g., ***-**-1234 for SSN) - Full value accessible only to record owner + HR Admin + CISO - Excluded from all bulk data exports unless explicitly authorized - Subject to right-to-erasure workflow (GDPR Article 17)

  4. Retention Timer Start: Retention period begins at record.CompletedDate or record.ClosedDate. If neither set, record.ModifiedDate of final status change is used.

  5. Legal Hold Freeze: Any record linked to an active eDiscovery hold (set in Compliance module §28) is frozen — no deletion, modification, or disposition until hold is lifted by CISO + Legal.

§5. Module 1: Finance & Accounting

Purpose: Comprehensive financial management: GL, AP, AR, cash, assets, expenses, tax, FX, budgeting, intercompany, and reporting.

M365 Excel Online for budget entry flowing into ERP budget module. Power BI embedded dashboards. Outlook actionable notifications for invoice approvals. SharePoint for financial document storage.

Key Personas: CFO / Finance Director, AP/AR Clerks, Budget Analysts, Tax Specialists, Treasury Managers

5.1 Tab 1: General Ledger & Chart of Accounts

Description: Core financial accounting platform with CoA and journal entry management.

Page: Chart of Accounts Design & Hierarchy

  • Fields Account Code, Account Name, Account Type (Asset/Liability/Equity/Revenue/Expense), Parent Account, Currency, Entity, Cost Center, Status (Active/Inactive)
  • Buttons Add Account Edit Account Deactivate Account Import CoA Export CoA View Hierarchy
  • Features:
  • Multi-level account hierarchy with drag-and-drop reordering
  • Account grouping by type, entity, and department
  • Account mapping to reporting standards (GAAP/IFRS)
  • Lock accounts during period close
  • Currency assignment per account (multi-currency support)
  • M365 Export CoA to Excel Online for review; Power BI account balance visualization

Page: Journal Entry Processing & Approval

  • Fields Journal ID (auto-generated), Date, Period, Entity, Description, Debit Account, Credit Account, Amount, Currency, FX Rate, Reference, Attachments, Approval Status
  • Buttons Create Entry Save Draft Submit for Approval Approve Reject Reverse Post Attach Document
  • Features:
  • Automated Journal Entry Creation based on sub-module triggers (AP, AR, Payroll, Assets)
  • Journal Entry Template Configuration — reusable templates for recurring entries
  • Dual-entry validation (debits must equal credits)
  • Multi-currency journal entries with auto FX conversion
  • Approval workflow (configurable by amount threshold)
  • Reversal capability with audit trail
  • Inter-entity journals for intercompany transactions
  • M365 Approval notifications via Outlook with Approve/Reject buttons; Journal attachments stored in SharePoint

Page: Period Close Checklist & Procedures

  • Fields Period (Month/Quarter/Year), Entity, Checklist Item, Assigned To, Status (Pending/In Progress/Complete), Due Date, Sign-off
  • Buttons Start Period Close Mark Complete Sign Off Reopen Period Generate Close Report
  • Features:
  • Configurable close checklist per entity
  • Task assignment and deadline tracking
  • Dependency management between close tasks
  • Period lock after sign-off (prevents post-close modifications)
  • Period Close Reporting & Sign-off with digital signatures

Page: Financial Statement Design (P&L, Balance Sheet, CF)

  • Fields Statement Type, Period, Entity, Consolidation Level, Currency, Format Template
  • Buttons Generate P&L Generate Balance Sheet Generate Cash Flow Customize Layout Export to PDF Export to Excel Schedule Auto-Generation
  • Features:
  • Configurable financial statement templates
  • Multi-entity consolidation
  • Comparative periods (current vs prior year/quarter)
  • Management Commentary & Narratives section
  • Auto-generate from GL data in real-time
  • M365 Power BI financial statement dashboards; Export to Excel Online for board review; PDF generation via native PDF engine

5.2 Tab 2: Accounts Payable

Description: Vendor invoice and payment processing.

Page: Vendor Master Setup & Maintenance

  • Fields Vendor ID, Legal Name, Trade Name, Tax ID, Address, Country, Payment Terms, Currency, Bank Details (encrypted), Category, Status, Risk Score, Compliance Status
  • Buttons Add Vendor Edit Deactivate View History Run Risk Assessment Export
  • Features:
  • Vendor Qualification & Onboarding workflow
  • Vendor Scorecard Management with performance tracking
  • Vendor Risk Assessment (financial, compliance, delivery)
  • Duplicate detection
  • Bank account verification
  • M365 Vendor onboarding form via Power Apps; Vendor documents in SharePoint

Page: Invoice Receipt & Matching (3-way)

  • Fields Invoice Number, Vendor, PO Number, GRN Number, Invoice Date, Due Date, Amount, Tax, Currency, Line Items, Match Status, Discrepancy Notes
  • Buttons Upload Invoice OCR Scan Auto-Match Manual Match Flag Discrepancy Approve Reject Put on Hold
  • Features:
  • Auto-extract PO numbers, amounts, vendor data via OCR (Azure Document Intelligence)
  • 3-way matching: Invoice vs PO vs Goods Receipt
  • Auto-categorize expenses to correct GL accounts
  • Discount Tracking & Management (early payment discounts)
  • Receipt Management & OCR for paper invoices
  • AI AI auto-categorizes expenses; Payment fraud detection (behavioral model per vendor)

Page: Invoice Approval Workflows

  • Fields Invoice ID, Amount, Approver(s), Approval Level, Status, Comments, Approval Date
  • Buttons Approve Reject Delegate Escalate View Audit Trail
  • Features:
  • Multi-level approval based on amount thresholds
  • Delegation and out-of-office routing
  • SLA tracking for approval turnaround
  • Batch approval capability
  • M365 Actionable email notifications with Approve/Reject buttons via Graph API; AI Smart Digest learns approval patterns and batches routine items

Page: Payment Processing & Scheduling

  • Fields Payment Batch ID, Vendor, Invoice(s), Amount, Currency, Payment Method (EFT/Check/Wire), Bank Account, Payment Date, Status
  • Buttons Create Payment Batch Schedule Payment Process Payment Cancel Generate Remittance Export Payment File
  • Features:
  • Dual-authorization payment batch processing (Maker-Checker)
  • Check & EFT Processing
  • SWIFT H2H Banking integration
  • MT101 payment file generation (ISO 20022 compliant)
  • Payment scheduling based on cash flow optimization
  • M365 Payment approval via Teams; Payment status notifications via Outlook

Page: AP Aging & Analysis

  • Fields Vendor, Invoice, Amount, Due Date, Days Overdue, Aging Bucket (Current/30/60/90/120+), Entity
  • Buttons Refresh Aging Filter by Entity Filter by Vendor Export Report Schedule Auto-Report
  • Features:
  • AP Aging & Accruals dashboard
  • Aging buckets with drill-down to individual invoices
  • Accrual calculation for uninvoiced receipts
  • Vendor payment history analysis
  • M365 Power BI AP aging dashboard; Automated aging report email via Outlook

5.3 Tab 3: Accounts Receivable

Description: Customer billing and collections management.

Page: Customer Master Setup & Classification

  • Fields Customer ID, Name, Contract Type, Billing Terms, Credit Limit, Currency, Tax Exempt Status, Address, Contact, Payment Terms
  • Buttons Add Customer Edit Deactivate View Payment History Set Credit Limit
  • Features:

Physical Asset Management → §23 EAM

Physical condition assessment, maintenance scheduling, work order management, and operational asset tracking are managed in the Enterprise Asset Management module §23. The Finance Fixed Asset Register (this tab) is the accounting/GL source of truth; §23 EAM is the physical/operational source of truth. The two are linked by Asset ID — depreciation schedules and net book value flow from here to §23; physical condition and maintenance history flow from §23 back here for impairment assessment.

→ Condition assessment, maintenance scheduling, work order creation, equipment history: §23 Enterprise Asset Management

5.12 Tab 12: Government Contract Accounting & DCAA Compliance (Replaces Deltek CostPoint)

Native government contract accounting engine replicating Deltek CostPoint's full DCAA-compliant capabilities. Supports FAR Part 31 cost allowability, CAS compliance, indirect rate management, incurred cost submissions, contract billing (SF1034/SF1035, WAWF/iRAPT), and audit trail requirements.

Description: Full DCAA-compliant accounting system for DoD Prime Contractor operations.

Page: Indirect Rate Management & Cost Pool Configuration

  • Fields Rate Structure ID, Fiscal Year, Rate Type (Fringe/Overhead/G&A/B&O/Material Handling/IR&D/B&P), Cost Pool Name, Base Type (Direct Labor $, Direct Labor Hours, Total Cost Input, Value Added, Direct Material $), Provisional Rate (%), Final Rate (%), Forward Pricing Rate (%), Ceiling Rate (%), Status (Provisional/Final/Audited)
  • Buttons Configure Rate Structure Add Cost Pool Edit Pool Set Base Calculate Rates Set Provisional Rate Submit Final Rates Generate Rate Proposal View Rate History Compare Years Lock Rates Simulate Rate Changes
  • Features:
  • Indirect Rate Structure Configuration:
    • Fringe Benefits Rate: Pool (health, pension, vacation, FICA, SUI, training) / Base (direct labor $)
    • Overhead Rate: Pool (indirect labor, facility costs, depreciation, utilities) / Base (direct labor $ + fringe)
    • G&A Rate: Pool (executive, accounting, HR, legal, corporate) / Base (total cost input or value added)
    • B&O Rate (if applicable): Bid & Proposal costs
    • Material Handling Rate: Pool (purchasing, receiving, warehousing) / Base (direct material $)
    • IR&D/B&P Rate: Independent R&D and Bid & Proposal
  • Rate Calculations:
    • Provisional billing rates (used for interim billing, adjusted at year-end)
    • Forward pricing rates (used for proposals and estimates, negotiated with DCMA)
    • Final rates (actual rates after fiscal year close, submitted to DCAA)
    • Rate simulation (what-if analysis: impact of new hire, facility move, etc.)
  • Cost Pool Management:
    • Automatic cost accumulation into pools from GL transactions
    • Cost pool validation (no unallowable costs in pools)
    • Pool-to-base allocation waterfall
    • Multi-segment rate structures (different rates for different business segments)
  • Fiscal year rate trending (5-year history)
  • Rate comparison: Provisional vs Final vs Forward Pricing

Page: FAR Part 31 Cost Allowability Engine

  • Fields Cost Type, FAR Reference, Allowable (Yes/No/Conditional), Conditions, GL Account(s), Screening Rule, Override Approval
  • Buttons Configure Allowability Rules Add Rule Edit Rule Run Screening Review Flagged Costs Override with Justification Generate Allowability Report View FAR Reference
  • Features:
  • Automated Cost Allowability Screening (FAR 31.205):
    • Automatically screen every transaction against FAR Part 31 cost principles
    • Unallowable cost categories (auto-flagged):
    • Alcoholic beverages (FAR 31.205-51)
    • Bad debts (FAR 31.205-3)
    • Contributions & donations (FAR 31.205-8)
    • Entertainment costs (FAR 31.205-14)
    • Fines & penalties (FAR 31.205-15)
    • Goodwill (FAR 31.205-49)
    • Interest (FAR 31.205-20, with exceptions)
    • Lobbying costs (FAR 31.205-22)
    • Organization costs (FAR 31.205-27)
    • Conditionally allowable costs (require documentation):
    • Travel (FAR 31.205-46): Must comply with FTR/JTR
    • Compensation (FAR 31.205-6): Reasonableness test
    • Professional services (FAR 31.205-33)
    • Training (FAR 31.205-44)
    • GL account mapping to allowability categories
    • Transaction-level allowability flag with audit trail
    • Override capability with documented justification and approval
  • Cost allowability report for DCAA auditors

Page: Cost Accounting Standards (CAS) Compliance

  • Fields CAS Number (CAS 401-420), Standard Title, Applicability (Full/Modified/Exempt), Disclosure Statement Reference, Compliance Status, Evidence/Documentation, Last Audit Date, Findings

Page: Government Contract Billing

  • Fields Contract, CLIN/SLIN, Billing Type (Cost-Plus/FFP/T&M/Progress/Milestone), Period, Direct Costs, Indirect Costs (applied at provisional rates), Fee/Profit, Total Billed, Cumulative Billed, Funded Amount, Ceiling Amount, Available Funding, Invoice Format (SF1034/SF1035/Commercial), Submission Method (WAWF/iRAPT/Email), Status
  • Buttons Generate Invoice Preview Validate Against Funding Submit via WAWF Submit via iRAPT Track Payment Apply Adjustment Generate Public Voucher View Billing History Reconcile to GL
  • Features:

    • Progress Payment: % of completion × contract price
    • Performance-Based Payment: Objective completion criteria

    • LOC (Limitation of Cost) clause compliance
    • Automatic stop-work notification when approaching funding ceiling
  • CLIN/SLIN Management:
    • Contract Line Item Number structure
    • Sub-Line Item tracking
    • CLIN type (priced, unpriced, informational, option)
    • ACRN (Accounting Classification Reference Number) mapping
    • LOA (Line of Accounting) assignment

  • Final billing rate adjustment vouchers
  • Contract closeout billing

Page: Contract Financial Management

  • Fields Contract Number, Contract Type (FFP/CPFF/CPAF/CPIF/T&M/IDIQ/BPA/BOA), Prime/Sub, Customer (DCMA ACO), Contracting Officer, DCMA Admin, Period of Performance (Start/End), Options (list with exercise dates), Total Contract Value, Funded Value, Billed Value, Cost Incurred, Fee Earned, At-Risk Amount, UB (Undefinitized), Status
  • Buttons Setup Contract Edit Add Modification Add Option Exercise Option Track Funding View Financial Summary Reconcile Generate Contract Status Report Close Contract
  • Features:
  • Contract Type Support:
    • Firm Fixed Price (FFP): Revenue recognition per ASC 606
    • Cost Plus Fixed Fee (CPFF): Cost reimbursement + fixed fee
    • Cost Plus Award Fee (CPAF): Cost + base fee + award fee based on evaluation
    • Cost Plus Incentive Fee (CPIF): Cost + fee adjusted by cost performance
    • Time & Materials (T&M): Labor rates × hours + materials
    • IDIQ (Indefinite Delivery/Indefinite Quantity): Task order management
    • BPA (Blanket Purchase Agreement): Call/order tracking
    • BOA (Basic Ordering Agreement): Order management under BOA
  • Contract Modifications:
    • Bilateral modifications (mutual agreement)
    • Unilateral modifications (government directed)
    • Administrative modifications (no cost/scope change)
    • Modification tracking with cost/schedule impact
    • Authorization of work before definitization (UCA tracking)
  • Contract Financial Tracking:
    • Contract value tracking (original + modifications = current)
    • Funding increment tracking (incremental funding)
    • Fee/profit tracking (earned, billed, received)
    • Contract-level P&L statement
    • Revenue recognition per ASC 606 / percentage of completion
    • Contract completion forecast
  • Revenue Recognition Engine (22+ Formulas — Replaces Deltek CostPoint Revenue Processing):
    • Cost-Based Formulas:
    • Cost Plus Fee on Cost — Fee percentage applied to allowable incurred costs
    • Cost Incurred Using EAC (Contract Value) — % complete = ITD Cost / EAC × Contract Value
    • Cost Incurred Using EAC (Funded Value) — % complete based on funded value
    • Cost Incurred Using ETC — % complete = ITD Cost / (ETC + ITD Cost)
    • Contract Value × Percent Complete — contract value multiplied by project % complete
    • Contract Value × Percent Complete vs. Rate Schedule — lower of two methods
    • Contract Value Less Backlog — contract value minus manually entered backlog
    • Time & Materials Formulas:
    • Loaded Labor Rate — Hours × billing rates from rate table
    • Loaded Labor Rate + Costs Incurred on Non-Labor — labor rates + ODC costs
    • Loaded Labor + Non-Labor + Burden on Non-Labor — includes burden allocation
    • Loaded Labor + Non-Labor w/Burden w/Fee — includes fee on non-labor+burden
    • Loaded Labor w/Fee + Non-Labor w/Burden w/Fee — fee on both labor and non-labor
    • Rate Schedule × Multiplier + Non-Labor × Multiplier — multiplier-based retroactive
    • Multiplier-Based Formulas:
    • Labor Cost × Multiplier + Non-Labor × Multiplier — multiplier rates on cost types
    • Billing-Based Formulas:
    • Equal to Project Ledger Sales — revenue equals costs from project summary
    • Equal to Billings Before Retainage — Amount Billed + Amount Retained
    • Equal to Billings After Retainage — Amount Billed only
    • Equal to Deliveries — Delivery Amount from billing summary
    • Fixed Amount Formulas:
    • Fixed Amount Month to Date — fixed monthly recognition
    • Fixed Amount Year to Date — fixed annual recognition
    • Fixed Amount Contract to Date — fixed contract-life recognition
    • Unit-Based Formulas:
    • Unit Revenue — CLIN-based unit pricing (fixed or incremental by date/quantity range)
    • Revenue Processing Features:
    • Ceiling enforcement (contract value ceiling, funded value ceiling)
    • Over-ceiling posting options (revenue only or revenue and billing)
    • Multiplier application (labor/non-labor from rate table and overrides)
    • Fee override hierarchy (lowest-rate precedence)
    • Prior-year revenue integration
    • Period-by-period allowable cost basis
    • Revenue compute → redistribute → post workflow
    • Revenue journal entry auto-generation

§6. Module 2: Human Resources — Full Rippling-Style Unified HR + IT + Finance Platform

Purpose: Unified employee lifecycle platform combining HR, IT, and spend management in a single system of record. Replicates the complete Rippling platform natively — providing workforce management (recruitment, onboarding, payroll, benefits, performance, learning), IT management (device management/MDM, identity/access management, app provisioning), and spend management (corporate cards, expense management, bill pay) from a single employee graph. This module eliminates the need for external HR platforms (Rippling, Workday, BambooHR, ADP) and standalone IT identity tools (Okta, JumpCloud) by providing automatic provisioning/deprovisioning, policy-based automation, and compound triggers that fire across HR, IT, and Finance simultaneously.

M365 Azure AD/Entra ID for identity management and SSO. Teams channels for onboarding. Outlook for offer letters, contract distribution, and automated notifications. SharePoint for personnel files and policy documents. Power Apps for leave requests and self-service. Power BI for HR analytics dashboards. Intune for device management co-management. Power Automate for workflow automation and compound triggers.

Key Personas: HR Director, HRIS Administrator, Recruiters, Payroll Administrators, Department Managers, IT Administrators, Security Officers, Finance/AP Team, Employees (self-service), Executives (analytics)

Tech Azure AD/Entra ID Graph API for identity management, SCIM 2.0 for app provisioning, MDM via Intune co-management, Azure Functions for payroll calculations and automation triggers, Azure SQL for employee graph database, React 18 for self-service portal, Azure Key Vault for encrypted PII, Azure OpenAI for AI features

6.1 Tab 1: Employee Master Data & Unified Employee Graph

Description: Core employee information and organizational management with Rippling-style unified employee graph — every change to an employee record cascades across HR, IT, and Finance systems automatically.

Page: Employee Master Data Setup

  • Fields Employee ID (auto-generated), First Name, Middle Name, Last Name, Preferred Name, Date of Birth, National ID (encrypted), Passport Number (encrypted), Passport Expiry, Nationality, Gender, Pronoun Preference, Marital Status, Contact Email (Personal), Work Email (auto-generated), Phone (Personal), Phone (Work), Emergency Contact (Name/Relationship/Phone/Email), Photo, Entity, Department, Division, Cost Center, Job Title, Job Level/Grade, Manager (direct), Dotted-Line Manager, Employment Type (Full-time/Part-time/Contract/Intern/Temp), Work Location (Office/Remote/Hybrid), Office Location, Desk/Seat Number, Start Date, End Date, Probation End Date, Status (Active/Inactive/Terminated/On Leave/Suspended), Work Authorization (Country-specific), Visa Type, Visa Expiry, Security Clearance (None/Secret/TS/TS-SCI), Clearance Expiry, FLSA Status (Exempt/Non-Exempt), EEO Category, Veteran Status, Disability Status
  • Buttons Add Employee Edit Deactivate View History Print ID Card Export Profile View All Systems View Device Inventory View App Access View Spend Organization Chart Audit Log
  • Features:
  • Unified Employee Graph (Rippling Core):
    • Single source of truth for all employee data
    • Every field change triggers automatic cascading updates:
    • Department change → updates cost center → updates GL coding → updates Teams channel membership → updates app access → updates SharePoint permissions → updates device policies
    • Title change → updates org chart → updates email signature → updates badge → updates reporting hierarchy → triggers compensation review workflow
    • Location change → updates payroll tax jurisdiction → updates benefits eligibility → updates device shipping → updates time zone → updates holiday calendar
    • Termination → revokes all app access → locks device → archives email → disables badge → triggers final pay → initiates equipment return
    • Employee timeline view (every lifecycle event chronologically)
    • Change audit trail with before/after values for every field
  • Organizational hierarchy with reporting lines and org chart visualization
  • Multi-entity employee management (UAE, US, Japan, Greece, Italy operations)
  • Custom fields builder (add unlimited custom fields with validation rules)
  • Employee groups (dynamic groups based on rules: e.g., "All US employees in Engineering with TS clearance")
  • Headcount tracking with approved positions vs. filled
  • M365 Azure AD/Entra ID sync (employee → Azure AD user auto-creation/update/disable); SharePoint personnel files; Teams org chart integration

Page: Employee Self-Service Portal

  • Fields Personal details (read/edit), Bank details (encrypted), Tax declarations, Emergency contacts, Certifications, Work preferences, Notification settings
  • Buttons Update Personal Info Update Bank Details View Payslips Submit Request View Leave Balance View Benefits View My Devices View My Apps View My Expenses View My Training Request Equipment Request App Access
  • Features:
  • Unified Self-Service Hub:
    • Single portal for all HR, IT, and Finance self-service
    • Request time off, view payslips, update personal info
    • Request new device, report device issue, request app access
    • Submit expenses, view corporate card transactions
    • View and complete assigned training
    • View company directory and org chart
    • Mobile-first responsive design (PWA)
    • Notification center (all alerts in one place)
  • Employee directory with search (name, department, skills, location)
  • Document center (access contracts, policies, tax forms, certificates)
  • AI-powered HR chatbot for FAQ answers (policy questions, leave balance, benefits info)
  • M365 Power Apps self-service portal; OneDrive for personal documents; Teams integration for quick requests

6.4 Tab 4: Payroll

Description: Built-in payroll calculation engine for UAE (WPS), US (federal/state tax, SCA/DBA), Japan, Greece, and Italy. Handles tax calculations, statutory deductions, multi-currency pay, payslip generation, and GL posting — no external payroll provider needed. Enhanced with Rippling-style automatic payroll that runs itself.

Page: Payroll Configuration & Setup

  • Fields Entity, Country, Pay Frequency (Monthly/Bi-weekly/Weekly), Pay Calendar, Currency, Tax Rules, Social Security Rules, GL Mapping, Cost Center Default, Auto-Run Schedule
  • Buttons Configure Entity Set Pay Calendar Import Tax Tables Test Calculation Set GL Mapping Configure Auto-Run
  • Features:
  • Multi-Country Payroll Setup
  • Calendar & working-day management per country/entity
  • Multi-Country Payroll Engine
  • Automatic Payroll (Rippling Payroll):
    • Auto-calculate payroll on schedule (no manual trigger needed)
    • Auto-incorporate: approved timesheets, overtime, leave deductions, new hires, terminations, salary changes, garnishments, bonuses
    • Exception-based review (only review flagged items, not every calculation)
    • Auto-file payroll taxes per jurisdiction
    • Auto-generate and distribute payslips

Page: Payroll Tax Rules & Deductions

  • Fields Country, Tax Type, Rate/Formula, Effective Date, Employee Category, Exemptions, Jurisdiction (Federal/State/Local)
  • Buttons Add Rule Edit Deactivate Import Updated Rates Verify Compliance
  • Country-specific implementations:
  • UAE: WPS (Wage Protection System) compliance, End of Service Benefit calculation (UAE Labour Law), MOHRE reporting
  • US: Federal/State/Local tax, Social Security, Medicare, 401(k), W-2, W-4, SCA/DBA prevailing wage, state unemployment (SUTA), workers' compensation
  • Japan: Employment insurance, health insurance, pension, resident tax, semi-annual bonus, year-end adjustment
  • Greece: IKA/EFKA contributions, income tax, solidarity levy, 14-month salary, employer contributions
  • Italy: INPS contributions, IRPEF tax, TFR severance, 13th/14th month salary, regional/municipal tax
  • Features:
  • Auto-update tax tables when government rates change
  • Multi-jurisdiction tax calculations (employee in State A, employer in State B)
  • Reciprocal tax agreements handling
  • Tax notice management (respond to tax agency inquiries)
  • Tech Azure Functions for tax calculation, country-specific tax rule engines, encrypted payroll database

Page: Payroll Processing & Execution

  • Fields Pay Period, Entity, Employee Count, Gross Pay Total, Deductions Total, Net Pay Total, Employer Taxes Total, Status (Draft/Calculated/Reviewed/Approved/Posted/Paid), Exceptions Count, Variance from Previous (%)
  • Buttons Calculate Payroll Preview Review Exceptions Approve Post to GL Generate Payslips Generate Payment File Rollback View Audit Trail
  • Features:
  • Wage/Salary Management
  • Deductions & Compliance
  • Garnishment & Levy Processing (child support, tax liens, creditor garnishments with priority rules)
  • Loan and salary advance management with auto-deduction
  • Loan Management & Deductions
  • Payroll-to-GL integration mapped by entity, cost center, project
  • Batch PDF generation and email distribution (payslips on 28th)
  • SWIFT MT101 payment file generation
  • Exception Dashboard: Flag unusual items (large variance from prior period, new hire missing tax forms, overtime exceeding threshold, negative net pay)
  • Off-cycle payment processing (bonuses, corrections, final pay)
  • Payroll preview with line-by-line comparison to prior period
  • M365 Payslips distributed via Outlook (encrypted PDF); Power BI payroll analytics; Teams notification to HR on payroll completion

Page: Payroll Compliance Reporting

  • Fields Report Type, Period, Jurisdiction, Filing Deadline, Status (Pending/Filed/Accepted/Rejected), Filing Method
  • Buttons Generate Report File View History Export Verify Filing Re-file
  • Features:
  • Year-end tax reporting per jurisdiction (W-2, 1099, etc.)
  • Quarterly tax filings (941, state unemployment)
  • Statutory filing support per country
  • Incentive & Bonus Management
  • New hire reporting (state-mandated)
  • ACA (Affordable Care Act) compliance reporting (1095-C)
  • EEO-1 report generation
  • Workers' compensation reporting
  • Filing deadline calendar with automated reminders

  • M365 Power BI learning dashboards; Training certificates stored in SharePoint; Teams notifications for training reminders

    • Location-based access (block access from unapproved countries)

  • Access Reviews & Compliance:

6.14 Tab 14: Workflow Automation Engine (Rippling Workflow Automation)

Description: Rippling-style compound trigger automation that fires across HR, IT, and Finance systems from a single event.

Page: Workflow Builder

  • Fields Workflow Name, Trigger Event, Conditions (list), Actions (list), Status (Active/Paused/Draft), Created By, Last Modified, Execution Count, Last Executed
  • Buttons Create Workflow Edit Clone Activate Pause Delete Test View Execution Log View Templates
  • Features:
  • Compound Trigger Automation:
    • Trigger Events: Employee hired, terminated, promoted, transferred, department changed, location changed, role changed, clearance changed, leave started, leave ended, training completed, probation ended, anniversary date, birthday, benefits eligible, performance review due, certification expiring, device refresh due, expense submitted, custom date field
    • Conditions (If/Then Logic):
    • If department = "Engineering" AND location = "US" AND clearance = "TS"
    • If employment type = "Full-time" AND tenure > 90 days
    • If salary > $150,000 AND role change
    • Any combination of employee fields with AND/OR/NOT logic
    • Actions (What Happens):
    • HR: Change benefits eligibility, update payroll, assign training, create review, update org chart
    • IT: Provision/deprovision app access, assign device, change security group, update permissions, reset MFA
    • Finance: Issue/cancel corporate card, update spending limit, change cost center coding, update GL mapping
    • Communication: Send email notification, post Teams message, send Outlook calendar invite, trigger in-app notification
    • Approval: Route to manager for approval, escalate if overdue, auto-approve if criteria met
    • Document: Generate document from template, request e-signature, file to SharePoint
    • Pre-Built Workflow Templates:
    • New Hire Onboarding (complete HR + IT + Facilities provisioning)
    • Department Transfer (update access, groups, cost center, training)
    • Promotion (update title, salary, access level, notify stakeholders)
    • Termination (full deprovisioning across all systems)
    • Clearance Change (add/remove classified system access)
    • Location Change (update payroll tax, benefits, time policy)
    • Annual Compliance (assign annual training, certifications renewal)
    • Device Refresh (order new device, configure, ship, retire old)
  • Visual workflow builder (flowchart-style with drag-and-drop)
  • Workflow execution log with full audit trail
  • Error handling (retry logic, failure notifications, manual override)
  • Workflow testing (dry run without executing actions)
  • Workflow analytics (execution count, success rate, average duration)

Tech React Gantt component, Azure SQL temporal tables, WebSocket real-time updates, Azure Functions for EVM calculations

Native enterprise scheduling engine replicating ALL Oracle Primavera P6 EPPM capabilities. Supports CPM scheduling, resource management, cost loading, earned value, risk analysis, multi-project scheduling, baseline management, and all P6 professional features. Additionally provides bi-directional P6 XER/XML import/export for interoperability with external stakeholders.

Page: Enterprise Project Structure (EPS) & Portfolio

  • Fields EPS Node ID, Node Name, Parent Node, OBS (Organizational Breakdown Structure), Responsible Manager, Project Count, Status Summary, Budget Summary
  • Buttons Add EPS Node Edit Delete Move Expand All Collapse All View Project List Assign OBS View Portfolio Dashboard
  • Features:
  • Enterprise Project Structure (EPS):
    • Hierarchical project grouping (Company → Division → Program → Project)
    • Unlimited nesting levels
    • Portfolio-level roll-up of schedule/cost data
    • EPS-level security and access control
  • Organizational Breakdown Structure (OBS):
    • Organizational hierarchy mapping
    • OBS-based security profiles (users see only their OBS projects)
    • OBS-to-EPS assignment (responsibility matrix)

Page: Activity Management & Scheduling

  • Fields Activity ID (auto or custom format), Activity Name, WBS Element, Activity Type (Task Dependent/Resource Dependent/Level of Effort/Start Milestone/Finish Milestone/WBS Summary), Original Duration, Remaining Duration, Actual Duration, % Complete Type (Duration/Physical/Units), Planned Start, Planned Finish, Actual Start, Actual Finish, Expected Finish, Early Start, Early Finish, Late Start, Late Finish, Total Float, Free Float, Calendar, Constraint Type, Constraint Date, Primary Resource, Activity Codes (up to 20 user-defined), Activity Steps, Notebook Topics, Status (Not Started/In Progress/Completed), Suspend Date, Resume Date, Driving Flag
  • Buttons Add Activity Edit Delete Indent Outdent Move Up Move Down Link Activities Unlink Assign Resources Assign Codes Add Steps Add Notes Add Relationships Schedule (F9) Level Resources Set Constraint View Log Dissolve Import from P6 XER Export to P6 XER
  • Features:
  • Activity Types:
    • Task Dependent: Duration drives, resources follow
    • Resource Dependent: Resource availability drives duration
    • Level of Effort: Duration spans from predecessor start to successor finish
    • Start Milestone: Zero-duration start marker
    • Finish Milestone: Zero-duration completion marker
    • WBS Summary: Roll-up activity for WBS level
  • Activity Relationships (PDM):
    • Finish-to-Start (FS) with positive/negative lag
    • Finish-to-Finish (FF) with lag
    • Start-to-Start (SS) with lag
    • Start-to-Finish (SF) with lag
    • Driving vs non-driving relationship identification
    • Relationship float calculation
    • Inter-project relationships (cross-project dependencies)
  • Constraint Types:
    • As Soon As Possible (ASAP)
    • As Late As Possible (ALAP)
    • Start On
    • Finish On
    • Start On or Before / Start On or After
    • Finish On or Before / Finish On or After
    • Mandatory Start / Mandatory Finish
    • Expected Finish (soft constraint for forecasting)
  • Activity Codes (User-Defined):
    • Up to 20 code categories per project (Area, Phase, Responsibility, Trade, Priority, etc.)
    • Global codes (shared across all projects) and project-specific codes
    • Code-based grouping, sorting, and filtering
    • Color-coding by code value on Gantt chart
  • Activity Steps:
    • Sub-tasks within an activity (weighted %)
    • Step completion drives activity % complete
    • Step descriptions and assignments
    • Step weight-based % calculation
  • Activity Notebook:
    • Multiple notebook topics per activity (Description, Assumptions, Risks, Notes)
    • Rich text formatting
    • Notebook search across project
  • Percent Complete Types:
    • Duration %: Based on elapsed duration vs original duration
    • Physical %: Manual entry based on physical progress
    • Units %: Based on resource units consumed vs planned
  • Suspend & Resume:
    • Suspend an activity (pauses schedule calculation)
    • Resume with new remaining duration
    • Split activities with gaps
  • Auto-Compute Actuals:
    • Option to auto-update actual start/finish from resource actuals
    • Option to calculate remaining duration from % complete

Page: CPM Scheduling Engine

  • Fields Schedule Options (Retained Logic/Progress Override/Actual Dates), Data Date, Project Must Finish By Date, Schedule Log (warnings/errors), Total Float Calculation Method, Multiple Float Path Settings
  • Buttons Schedule (F9) Set Data Date View Schedule Log Retained Logic Mode Progress Override Mode Calculate Multiple Float Paths View Longest Path View Near-Critical Export Schedule Log
  • Features:
  • Critical Path Method (CPM) Engine:
    • Forward pass calculation (Early Start/Early Finish)
    • Backward pass calculation (Late Start/Late Finish)
    • Total Float = Late Finish - Early Finish
    • Free Float = Successor Early Start - Activity Early Finish - Lag
    • Critical Path identification (Total Float ≤ 0)
    • Longest Path calculation (true driving path through the network)
    • Multiple Float Paths analysis (identify parallel near-critical paths)
  • Scheduling Options:
    • Retained Logic: Honors original logic sequence even when out-of-sequence progress occurs
    • Progress Override: Allows out-of-sequence progress to override remaining relationships
    • Actual Dates: Uses actual dates as-is without re-scheduling
  • Data Date Management:
    • Data date (status date) for schedule calculation reference
    • Progress Spotlight: Highlights activities that should have progressed between two dates
    • Auto-advance data date
  • Schedule Health Checks:
    • DCMA 14-point schedule health assessment: 1. Logic (% activities with predecessors AND successors) 2. Leads (number of negative lags) 3. Lags (excessive positive lags) 4. Relationship Types (% FS vs others) 5. Hard Constraints (% with constraints) 6. High Float (activities with excessive float) 7. Negative Float (activities with negative float) 8. High Duration (activities > threshold) 9. Invalid Dates (actual dates after data date) 10. Resources (% activities with resources assigned) 11. Missed Tasks (% past due) 12. Critical Path Test (longest path integrity) 13. Critical Path Length Index (CPLI) 14. Baseline Execution Index (BEI)
    • Schedule quality score (composite metric)
    • Automated schedule health report generation
  • Schedule Log:
    • Detailed scheduling log with warnings, errors, and circularity detection
    • Out-of-sequence activity identification
    • Constraint-driven date identification
    • Open-ended activity warnings

Page: Gantt Chart & Visualizations

  • Fields Visual Gantt display, Timeline Scale (Hour/Day/Week/Month/Quarter/Year), Grouping, Sorting, Filtering, Bar Colors, Baseline Bars, Critical Path Highlight
  • Buttons Expand All Collapse All Zoom In Zoom Out Show Critical Path Show Float Show Baselines Group By Sort By Filter Color By Code Show Relationships Show Progress Print Export PDF Save Layout Load Layout
  • Features:
  • Gantt Chart (Activity Table + Bar Chart):
    • Interactive Gantt with drag-and-drop duration adjustment
    • Activity bars with progress fill, remaining duration, critical path highlighting
    • Baseline bars overlay (up to 3 baselines simultaneously)
    • Relationship lines (driving relationships in solid, non-driving in dashed)
    • Float bars (total float and free float display)
    • Milestone diamonds with labels
    • Summary bars for WBS and group headers
    • Timescale customization (dual timescale: month/week, quarter/month)
    • Activity bar coloring by code, criticality, status, or custom rule
  • Resource Usage Profile/Spreadsheet:
    • Resource histogram (stacked bar chart by resource/trade)
    • Resource spreadsheet (tabular view of resource loading by period)
    • Over-allocation highlighting (red when demand > availability)
    • Cumulative resource curve
  • Activity Network Diagram (PDM):
    • Visual network diagram showing activity boxes and relationship arrows
    • Critical path highlighting
    • Customizable box content (ID, name, dates, duration, float)
    • Zoom and pan navigation
  • Trace Logic:
    • Trace driving relationships forward/backward from selected activity
    • Visual path highlighting through the network
    • Identify what drives the activity and what the activity drives
  • Earned Value Charts:
    • S-Curve: BCWS, BCWP, ACWP curves with time axis
    • CPI/SPI trend chart
    • Variance analysis charts
    • EAC projection overlay

Page: Resource Management

  • Fields Resource ID, Resource Name, Resource Type (Labor/Non-Labor/Material), Trade/Skill, Calendar, Max Availability (units/hour), Default Units/Time, Price/Unit, Cost Account, Role Assignment, Resource Code Categories
  • Buttons Add Resource Edit Delete Assign to Activity Set Availability Set Rate View Loading Level Resources Auto-Assign by Role Import Resource Pool Export
  • Features:
  • Resource Dictionary:
    • Global resource pool shared across all projects
    • Resource types: Labor, Non-Labor (equipment), Material
    • Resource codes for grouping/filtering (Skill, Department, Location, Trade)
    • Resource calendars (individual availability calendars)
    • Multiple rate profiles per resource (standard, overtime, shift differential)
  • Resource Assignment:
    • Assign resources to activities with units/time or total units
    • Role-based assignment (assign role, later fill with named resource)
    • Resource lag (resource starts after activity starts)
    • Resource curves for non-linear loading:
    • Uniform (default)
    • Front-loaded (bell curve shifted left)
    • Back-loaded (bell curve shifted right)
    • Triangle (peak in middle)
    • Trapezoidal (ramp up, plateau, ramp down)
    • Custom curve (user-defined distribution)
    • Resource bucket planning (rough cut by role/skill)
  • Resource Leveling:
    • Automatic resource leveling (delays activities to resolve over-allocations)
    • Level within total float (don't extend project)
    • Level with priority-based rules (activity priority, total float, early start)
    • Level across projects in portfolio
    • What-if leveling (preview results before applying)
    • Leveling log with explanations
  • Resource Analysis:
    • Resource utilization dashboard (% utilized vs available)
    • Demand vs availability charts by period
    • Resource conflict identification across projects
    • Resource sharing analysis (which projects compete for same resources)
    • Staffing plan generation from schedule

Page: Calendar Management

    • Global Calendar: Default calendar for all projects

  • Multiple shifts per day with different hours
  • Holiday lists by country/entity (UAE, US, Japan, Greece, Italy)
  • Exception days (planned shutdowns, client-mandated non-work days)
  • Calendar export/import for sharing

Page: Baseline Management

  • Fields Baseline Number (BL-0 through BL-49), Baseline Name, Type (Project Baseline/Initial/Current/Monthly Snapshot), Save Date, Saved By, Description, Activities Count, Total Duration, Total Cost

Page: Schedule Analysis & Reporting

  • Fields Analysis Type, Parameters, Results, Score, Recommendations
  • Buttons Run DCMA 14-Point Check Run Critical Path Analysis Run Float Analysis Run Multiple Float Paths Generate Schedule Narrative Run Claim Digger Run Monte Carlo Simulation Generate IPMR/IPMDAR Export CPR Format 1-5
  • Features:
  • Schedule Claim Digger (Change Detection):
    • Compare two schedule versions and identify ALL changes:
    • Added activities
    • Deleted activities
    • Modified dates (start, finish, duration)
    • Modified relationships (added, deleted, changed logic)
    • Modified constraints
    • Modified calendars
    • Modified resources
    • Detailed change report with categorized findings
  • Monte Carlo Simulation:
    • Probabilistic schedule analysis
    • Three-point duration estimates (optimistic, most likely, pessimistic)
    • Risk distribution types (triangular, beta, uniform, normal)
    • 1,000+ simulation iterations
    • Confidence level results (P10, P50, P80, P90 completion dates)
    • Criticality index (% of iterations where activity is on critical path)
    • Sensitivity analysis (which activities most impact project completion)
    • Tornado chart (risk drivers ranked by impact)
  • Thresholds & Issues:
    • Configurable threshold parameters (float, duration, cost, dates)
    • Automatic threshold monitoring against data date
    • Issue generation when thresholds are exceeded
    • Issue tracking with resolution workflow
  • Global Change Engine:
    • Batch update activities based on conditional rules
    • Examples: "If Activity Code Area = Building A, add 5 days to remaining duration"
    • Preview changes before applying
    • Undo capability
    • Change log for audit trail
  • Reports & Layouts:
    • User-defined layouts (column selections, grouping, sorting, filtering)
    • Layout categories: Global, Project, User
    • Custom columns (calculated fields using formulas)
    • User Defined Fields (UDFs): Text, Number, Date, Cost, Integer, Indicator
    • Report Wizard for custom report creation
    • Standard schedule reports (Activity List, Schedule Summary, Resource Loading, Milestone Report)
    • Look-ahead reports (2-week, 4-week, 6-week, 90-day)
  • Schedule Narrative AI:
    • Auto-generates schedule analysis narrative from variance data
    • Identifies key drivers, delays, and recovery opportunities
    • Executive-friendly language with technical detail available
  • AI
  • AI Schedule Optimizer — Analyzes the schedule and recommends optimization opportunities (parallel activities, fast-tracking, crashing)
  • AI Delay Predictor — Uses weather forecasts, supply chain data, and historical patterns to predict potential delays
  • AI Resource Balancer — Recommends optimal resource distribution across portfolio to minimize conflicts
  • AI Schedule Narrator — Generates professional schedule narrative reports from variance data

7.4 Tab 4: Earned Value Management (EVM) — Full EVMS (Replaces Deltek CostPoint EVM)

Native ANSI/EIA-748 compliant Earned Value Management System replicating Deltek CostPoint's full EVM capabilities. Supports DCMA surveillance, IPMR/IPMDAR reporting (replacing CPR Format 1-5), baseline management, Management Reserve (MR), Undistributed Budget (UB), Over Target Baseline (OTB), and complete DoD EVM compliance.

Page: Performance Measurement Baseline (PMB) Setup

  • Fields Contract, WBS Element, Control Account (CA), Work Package (WP), Planning Package (PP), OBS Assignment (Control Account Manager), Budget at Completion (BAC), Budget Distribution Method (manual/spread curve), Time-Phased Budget (by period), Management Reserve (MR), Undistributed Budget (UB), Contract Budget Base (CBB), Total Allocated Budget (TAB), Authorized Unpriced Work (AUW), Contract Target Cost, Contract Target Price, Over Target Baseline (OTB) Flag, Negotiated Contract Cost (NCC)
  • Buttons Build PMB Set Baseline Distribute Budget Time-Phase Assign CA Manager Create Work Packages Create Planning Packages Convert PP to WP Set MR Set UB Lock Baseline Request OTB View RAM (Responsibility Assignment Matrix) Export PMB
  • Features:
  • EVM Hierarchy:
    • Contract → WBS → Control Account (CA) → Work Package (WP) / Planning Package (PP)
    • Control Account: Intersection of WBS element and OBS element (assigned to CA Manager)
    • Work Package: Lowest-level scheduled task with earned value
    • Planning Package: Future work not yet decomposed into work packages
    • Summary Level Planning Package (SLPP): Far-future work
  • Budget Structure:
    • Contract Budget Base (CBB) = Negotiated Contract Cost (NCC) + Authorized Unpriced Work (AUW)
    • Total Allocated Budget (TAB) = Performance Measurement Baseline (PMB) + Management Reserve (MR)
    • PMB = Distributed Budget + Undistributed Budget (UB)
    • Distributed Budget = Σ(Control Account Budgets)
    • Management Reserve: Withheld budget for unknown-unknowns, only released by PM authorization
  • Budget Distribution Methods:
    • Linear spread (equal per period)
    • Front-loaded / Back-loaded curves
    • Custom distribution (manual period-by-period entry)
    • Milestone-weighted distribution
    • Resource-loaded distribution (from schedule resource assignment)
  • Responsibility Assignment Matrix (RAM):
    • WBS × OBS matrix showing CA Manager assignments
    • Budget allocation at each intersection
    • Drill-down from RAM to work packages

Page: Earned Value Calculation & Techniques

  • Fields Work Package, EV Technique, Period, BCWS (Budgeted Cost of Work Scheduled / Planned Value), BCWP (Budgeted Cost of Work Performed / Earned Value), ACWP (Actual Cost of Work Performed / Actual Cost), BAC, % Complete, % Spent
  • Buttons Calculate EV Update Progress Apply EV Technique View by Period View Cumulative View by CA View by WP Reconcile with Finance Import Actuals Lock Period
  • Features:
  • Earned Value Techniques (per ANSI/EIA-748):
    • 0/100: 0% until complete, then 100% (short-duration tasks)
    • 50/50: 50% at start, 50% at completion
    • 25/75: 25% at start, 75% at completion
    • Percent Complete: Manual % complete × BAC (subjective assessment)
    • Milestone Weighted: Weighted milestones within work package
    • Units Complete: Physical units completed / total units × BAC
    • Apportioned Effort: EV tied proportionally to another work package
    • Level of Effort (LOE): EV = PV (for support/overhead activities)
  • Cost Element Breakdown:
    • Direct Labor (hours × rate)
    • Direct Material (quantities × unit cost)
    • Direct Equipment
    • Subcontractor Costs
    • Other Direct Costs (ODC): Travel, Consultants, etc.
    • Indirect Costs (Fringe, Overhead, G&A) — applied per Deltek CostPoint rates
  • Period Close Process:
    • EV data collection period alignment
    • Actuals import from Finance/GL module
    • % complete update from field/schedule
    • Period lock after verification
    • Reconciliation between EV system and financial books

Page: EVM Performance Analysis

  • Fields WBS/CA, Period, BAC, BCWS, BCWP, ACWP, CV (Cost Variance = BCWP-ACWP), SV (Schedule Variance = BCWP-BCWS), CPI (Cost Performance Index = BCWP/ACWP), SPI (Schedule Performance Index = BCWP/BCWS), EAC (multiple methods), ETC, VAC (Variance at Completion = BAC-EAC), TCPI (To-Complete Performance Index), IEAC (Independent EAC), Cumulative CPI/SPI, Current Period CPI/SPI
  • Buttons Calculate All Metrics View Trend Charts Drill Down by WBS Drill Down by OBS Generate Variance Narrative Run EAC Calculations Compare EAC Methods View S-Curve Generate IPMR Export View Thresholds
  • Features:
  • EAC Calculation Methods:
    • EAC = BAC / CPI (cumulative CPI-based)
    • EAC = ACWP + (BAC - BCWP) (remaining work at budget rate)
    • EAC = ACWP + (BAC - BCWP) / CPI (remaining at current efficiency)
    • EAC = ACWP + (BAC - BCWP) / (CPI × SPI) (composite index)
    • EAC = Manager's estimate (bottom-up re-estimate)
    • Independent EAC (IEAC) for government oversight comparison
  • TCPI (To-Complete Performance Index):
    • TCPI(BAC) = (BAC - BCWP) / (BAC - ACWP) — efficiency needed to meet budget
    • TCPI(EAC) = (BAC - BCWP) / (EAC - ACWP) — efficiency needed to meet EAC
  • S-Curve Generation:
    • Three-curve overlay: BCWS (blue), BCWP (green), ACWP (red)
    • Cumulative and current-period views
    • EAC projection line extending from ACWP
    • BAC reference line
    • Management Reserve line
    • Interactive time axis with period drill-down
  • Variance Analysis:
    • Cost Variance drill-down by WBS, CA, resource type, cost element
    • Schedule Variance drill-down
    • Variance threshold monitoring (configurable Yellow/Red thresholds)
    • Auto-generated Variance Analysis Report (VAR) narrative
    • Root cause categories for variances (Rate, Usage, Efficiency, Schedule, Scope)
  • Trend Analysis:
    • CPI trend chart (12-month rolling)
    • SPI trend chart (12-month rolling)
    • EAC trend chart (monthly EAC evolution)
    • TCPI trend chart
    • Cumulative vs current-period comparison
  • Multi-project portfolio view with aggregated SPI/CPI weighted by BAC

Page: IPMR / IPMDAR Reporting (Replaces CPR Format 1-5)

  • Fields Report Period, Contract, IPMR Format (1-7), Reporting Level (WBS Level 2/3/4), Submission Date, Status
  • Buttons Generate IPMR Format 1 Generate Format 2 Generate Format 3 Generate Format 4 Generate Format 5 Generate Format 6 Generate Format 7 Validate Data Submit to Customer View History Export Excel Export PDF
  • Features:
  • IPMR/IPMDAR Format 1 — Work Breakdown Structure (WBS):
    • WBS-oriented EV data (BCWS, BCWP, ACWP, BAC, EAC, VAC)
    • Cumulative and current-period values
    • Reporting at customer-required WBS level
    • MR, UB, TAB reconciliation
  • Format 2 — Organizational/Functional Categories:
    • OBS-oriented view of same EV data
    • Functional cost breakdown (Engineering, Manufacturing, T&E, Quality, PM, etc.)
    • Cross-tabulation of WBS × OBS
  • Format 3 — Baseline:
    • Time-phased PMB by period (monthly/quarterly)
    • Baseline changes log
    • MR changes log
    • Budget reconciliation
  • Format 4 — Staffing:
    • Time-phased staffing plan (headcount by functional area)
    • Actual vs planned staffing
    • Staffing forecast through completion
  • Format 5 — Explanations & Problem Analysis:
    • Narrative explanations for significant variances
    • Variance thresholds triggering mandatory explanation
    • Corrective action plans
    • Impact assessment
  • Format 6 — Integrated Master Schedule (IMS):
    • Schedule data export in IPMR Format 6
    • Activity-level detail with EV mapping
    • Critical/near-critical path identification
  • Format 7 — Historical (Trend Data):
    • 12-month rolling history of key EVM metrics
    • CPI, SPI, EAC trends

Page: EVM Progress Reporting & Metrics

  • Fields Report Period, Project, Status (Green/Amber/Red), Key Accomplishments, Issues, Risks, Next Period Plan, EVM Health Score
  • Buttons Generate PSR Generate CPR/IPMR Generate EVM Dashboard Submit Approve Export PDF Email Distribution Schedule Auto-Generation
  • Features:
  • Automated Project Status Report (PSR) generation

§9. Module 5: Proposal & Bid Management — Full GovWin IQ Intelligence Platform

Purpose: Enterprise business development, opportunity intelligence, capture management, and proposal lifecycle platform. Replicates the complete Deltek GovWin IQ intelligence ecosystem natively — providing pre-RFP intelligence, incumbent tracking, agency analysis, competitor intelligence, contract award data, and market analytics alongside full proposal development, review, submission, and award workflows. This module eliminates the need for external opportunity intelligence tools (GovWin IQ, Bloomberg Government, GovTribe, HigherGov) by building a comprehensive government contract intelligence engine with predictive analytics, teaming partner matching, and win strategy optimization.

M365 SAM.gov API and FPDS/USASpending.gov data feeds for contract intelligence. Teams for proposal review meetings, capture planning sessions, and BD strategy calls. SharePoint for proposal library, intel reports, and past performance database. Outlook for bid deadline notifications, agency alerts, opportunity tracking emails, and proposal distribution. Power BI for pipeline analytics, win rate dashboards, market share analysis, and agency spend trending. Power Automate for opportunity intake automation, deadline reminders, and review workflow triggers.

Key Personas: VP Business Development, Capture Managers, Proposal Managers, Technical Writers, BD Analysts, Competitive Intelligence Analysts, Pricing Analysts, Contract Specialists, Teaming/Partnerships Manager, Executive Leadership (pipeline reviews)

Tech SAM.gov API (opportunities, exclusions, entity validation), FPDS-NG data feeds (federal procurement data), USASpending.gov API (contract award data), Azure Cognitive Services for document analysis, Azure OpenAI for intelligence extraction and proposal generation, ML win/loss prediction model, Azure SQL for opportunity and intelligence database, SignalR for real-time pipeline updates, React 18 with advanced data visualization (D3.js for market maps)

9.1 Tab 1: Opportunity Intelligence & Pipeline (Replaces GovWin IQ Opportunities)

Page: Opportunity Discovery & Intake

  • Fields Opportunity ID (auto-generated), External ID (SAM.gov/FPDS/State Portal), Source (SAM.gov/FPDS/USASpending/State Portal/Agency Website/Industry Contact/Pre-RFP Intel/Sources Sought/RFI), Title, Description, Agency (Federal/State/Local), Sub-Agency/Office, NAICS Code(s), PSC Code(s) (Product Service Codes), Set-Aside Type (Full & Open/Small Business/WOSB/SDVOSB/8(a)/HUBZone/VOSB/Sole Source), Competition Type (Full Competition/Sole Source/Limited Sources/Set-Aside), Estimated Value (Low/High Range), Contract Type (FFP/T&M/CPFF/CPAF/CPIF/IDIQ/BPA/BOA), Period of Performance (Base + Options), Place of Performance (City/State/OCONUS), Due Date, Q&A Deadline, Pre-Bid Conference Date, Response Date, Classification (Unclassified/CUI/Secret/TS), Clearance Required (None/Secret/TS/TS-SCI), Status (Identified/Tracking/Pursuing/Bid/Submitted/Won/Lost/No-Bid/Cancelled), Priority (High/Medium/Low), Match Score (AI-calculated)
  • Buttons Add Opportunity Import from SAM.gov Import from FPDS Bulk Import Edit Archive Set Alert Auto-Scan Sources View Intel Package Assign to BD Quick Bid/No-Bid
  • Features:
  • Automated Opportunity Discovery:
    • SAM.gov continuous feed with configurable NAICS/PSC filters
    • Sources Sought / RFI / Draft RFP / Pre-solicitation notice tracking
    • State and local government opportunity portals aggregation
    • Industry day and pre-bid conference calendar
    • Keyword-based opportunity alerts (email + in-app notification)
    • Saved search profiles (e.g., "USACE Construction $1M-$50M SDVOSB")
    • De-duplication engine (merge opportunities from multiple sources)
  • Pre-RFP Intelligence (Replaces GovWin IQ Early Intel):
    • Track opportunities 12-24 months before RFP release
    • Budget line item tracking (link to agency budget requests and congressional appropriations)
    • Program intelligence (track program milestones, funding status, acquisition strategy)
    • Forecast calendar (predicted RFP release dates based on historical patterns and budget cycles)
    • Acquisition forecast notifications from agency published procurement forecasts
    • Pre-solicitation engagement tracking (industry days attended, meetings with contracting officers)
  • Opportunity Scoring & Matching:
    • AI-powered match scoring against MVL capabilities, past performance, clearances, and geographic presence
    • Match criteria: NAICS alignment, past performance relevance, key personnel availability, clearance match, set-aside eligibility, geographic proximity, contract type experience, agency relationship history
    • Configurable scoring weights per criteria
    • Threshold alerts (auto-notify when match score exceeds configurable threshold)
    • Recommendation engine: "Similar to opportunities you've won"
  • AI
  • AI Opportunity Matcher — Scores each opportunity against MVL capabilities with detailed factor breakdown; learns from win/loss history to improve scoring
  • AI RFP Analyzer — Extracts key requirements, evaluation criteria, and compliance items from RFP/SOW documents; generates structured requirement matrix
  • AI Budget Tracker — Monitors agency budget requests and congressional appropriations to predict upcoming opportunities

Page: Opportunity Pipeline & Tracking

  • Fields Opportunity, Stage (Pre-RFP/Identified/Tracking/Qualifying/Pursuing/Capture/Proposal/Submitted/Evaluation/Award/Post-Award), Probability (%), Weighted Value, Capture Manager, BD Owner, Next Action, Next Action Date, Decision Gate Date, Days in Stage, Pipeline Category (Must Win/Strategic/Opportunistic/Qualify Out)
  • Buttons Update Stage Set Probability Assign Capture Manager Add Notes View History Pipeline Review Stage Gate Review Advance Stage Move to No-Bid
  • Features:
  • Pipeline Management Dashboard:
    • Pipeline funnel visualization with stage counts and values
    • Weighted pipeline value (probability × estimated value)
    • Pipeline by: agency, NAICS, set-aside, contract type, capture manager, time horizon
    • Pipeline aging (opportunities stuck in stage too long)
    • Win probability trending over time
    • Pipeline velocity (average time per stage)
    • Revenue forecast (weighted pipeline value by expected award quarter)
  • Stage Gate Process:
    • Configurable stage gates with required approvals
    • Gate criteria checklist (e.g., must have customer intel before advancing to Capture)
    • Mandatory gate reviews with recorded decisions
    • Auto-advancement rules (if all criteria met, suggest next stage)
  • Opportunity Calendar:
    • Bid due dates with countdown
    • Pre-bid conferences and industry days
    • Q&A deadlines
    • Draft RFP / Final RFP expected dates
    • Award expected dates
    • Team resource availability overlay
  • Pipeline Analytics:
    • Win rate by: agency, NAICS, contract size, set-aside type, capture manager
    • Average pursuit cost vs. win value (ROI analysis)
    • Pipeline-to-booking conversion rate
    • Seasonal trending (government fiscal year patterns)
  • M365 Power BI pipeline dashboards; Outlook calendar sync for all bid deadlines; Teams channel for pipeline status updates; Power Automate for deadline reminder sequences

Page: Bid/No-Bid Analysis & Decision

  • Fields Opportunity, Evaluation Criteria (12 weighted factors), Score per Factor, Weighted Score, Total Score, Decision (Bid/No-Bid/Conditional Bid), Decision Authority, Rationale, Conditions (if conditional), Risk Assessment
  • Buttons Create Analysis Score Criteria Calculate Submit Decision Approve Reject Request Additional Intel View History Compare to Similar Bids Generate Decision Memo
  • Features:
  • Comprehensive Go/No-Go Evaluation (12 Factors):
    1. Technical Fit (do we have the capabilities?)
    2. Past Performance (do we have relevant experience?)
    3. Competitive Position (can we win against known competitors?)
    4. Price-to-Win (can we price competitively and maintain margin?)
    5. Key Personnel Availability (are the right people available?)
    6. Teaming/Partnerships (do we have the right team?)
    7. Customer Relationship (do we have agency access and insight?)
    8. Clearance/Compliance (do we meet all eligibility requirements?)
    9. Resource/Capacity (do we have B&P budget and capacity?)
    10. Strategic Value (does this align with growth strategy?)
    11. Risk Assessment (contract risk, performance risk, financial risk)
    12. Recompete/Incumbent Advantage (are we the incumbent or is there one?)
  • Configurable scoring scale (1-5, 1-10, Red/Yellow/Green) with weights
  • Historical comparison (how did similar scored opportunities perform?)
  • Multi-level approval (BD Manager → VP BD → CEO for high-value)
  • Decision memo auto-generation with AI
  • Go/No-Go decision dashboard (all pending decisions in one view)

9.2 Tab 2: Agency & Customer Intelligence (Replaces GovWin IQ Agency Intelligence)

Page: Agency Intelligence Dashboard

  • Fields Agency Name, Type (Federal/State/Local/DoD), Sub-Agency/Office, Annual Procurement Budget, Construction Budget, Top NAICS Codes, Primary PSC Codes, Key Contacts, Preferred Contract Types, Socioeconomic Goals, Small Business Goals (%), Historical Award Count, Average Award Size, MVL Relationship Score
  • Buttons Add Agency Edit View Spend Analysis View Award History View Contacts View Forecasts Set Alert Link Opportunities Export Profile
  • Features:
  • Agency Spend Analysis (Replaces GovWin Spend Analysis):
    • Total agency procurement spend by fiscal year (from FPDS/USASpending)
    • Spend breakdown by: NAICS, PSC, contract type, set-aside type, place of performance
    • Spend trending (year-over-year growth/decline by category)
    • Top contractors by agency (who wins the most work)
    • Small business achievement vs. goals (SB, WOSB, SDVOSB, 8(a), HUBZone)
    • Construction-specific spend filtering
    • Spend by sub-agency/office (drill down to contracting office level)
  • Agency Contact Management:
    • Key decision makers: Contracting Officers, CORs, Program Managers, Technical POCs
    • Contact relationship tracking (meeting history, correspondence, engagement level)
    • Org chart mapping (agency organizational structure)
    • Contact influence mapping (decision authority level)
    • Meeting notes and follow-up action tracking
    • Do-not-contact flags (procurement sensitivity periods)
  • Agency Procurement Forecast:
    • Published agency procurement forecasts imported and tracked
    • Budget request analysis (President's Budget, Congressional markups)
    • Program lifecycle tracking (R&D → Procurement → O&M → Disposal)
    • Continuing Resolution impact analysis
    • Sequestration/funding risk indicators
  • Agency Alerts:
    • New award notifications for tracked agencies
    • Budget change alerts
    • Leadership change notifications (new contracting officers, program managers)
    • Policy change alerts affecting procurement
    • Protest/challenge activity on agency contracts
  • AI
  • AI Agency Analyzer — Analyzes agency procurement patterns, predicts future spend, and identifies emerging opportunities
  • AI Relationship Mapper — Scores MVL relationship strength with each agency based on meeting frequency, past performance, and contract history

Page: Incumbent & Contract Intelligence

  • Fields Contract Number, Contractor Name (Incumbent), Agency, Contract Value, Period of Performance (Start/End/Options Remaining), Contract Type, Place of Performance, NAICS, PSC, Description, Recompete Date, Follow-On Expected, Incumbent Performance Rating (CPARS if available)
  • Buttons Search Contracts Import from FPDS Import from USASpending Track Recompete Set Alert View Contractor Profile View Subcontractors Analyze Competitive Landscape
  • Features:
  • Contract Award Database:
    • Complete federal contract award history (FPDS data)
    • Search by: contractor, agency, NAICS, PSC, value range, location, date range
    • Award details: value (base + options), period, modifications history
    • Sub-award data (major subcontractors on each prime contract)
    • Contract modification tracking (increases, decreases, extensions, novations)
  • Incumbent Tracking (Replaces GovWin Incumbent Data):
    • Identify current incumbents on target contracts
    • Recompete calendar (contracts expiring within 6/12/18/24 months)
    • Incumbent performance analysis (CPARS ratings, past performance references)
    • Incumbent vulnerability assessment (contract issues, protests, schedule delays)
    • Bridge contract tracking (when recompete is delayed)
    • Incumbent team analysis (known subcontractors, teaming partners)
  • FPDS Analytics:
    • Award data trending by agency, NAICS, contractor
    • Market share calculations (MVL vs. competitors by agency/NAICS)
    • Average award size by category
    • Set-aside utilization rates
    • Sole source vs. competitive award ratios
    • Geographic distribution of awards (map visualization)

9.3 Tab 3: Competitor Intelligence (Replaces GovWin IQ Competitor Tracking)

Page: Competitor Database & Profiling

  • Fields Company Name, DUNS/UEI Number, CAGE Code, Size Standard (Large/Small), Revenue (annual), Employee Count, Headquarters, Key Offices, NAICS Codes, Core Capabilities, Certifications (ISO/CMMI/8(a)/SDVOSB/etc.), Clearance Facility Level, Key Personnel, Website, Status (Active Competitor/Potential Partner/Watch List)
  • Buttons Add Competitor Edit Import from SAM.gov View Awards View Win/Loss Against View Teaming History Compare to MVL Set Alert SWOT Analysis Export Profile
  • Features:
  • Competitor Profiling:
    • Complete competitor profiles with capabilities, past performance, certifications
    • SAM.gov entity validation (verify small business status, certifications)
    • Competitor award history from FPDS (what they've won, where, how much)
    • Competitor revenue and employee trends (growth/decline indicators)
    • Key personnel tracking (who are their program managers, capture managers)
    • Competitor facility locations and clearance levels
    • Competitor certifications and compliance posture
  • Competitive Analysis:
    • Head-to-head win/loss record (MVL vs. specific competitor)
    • Competitor market share by agency, NAICS, geography
    • Competitor bid frequency (how often they bid in your markets)
    • Competitor pricing patterns (analysis of awarded contract values)
    • Competitor teaming patterns (who they team with)
    • Strength/Weakness/Opportunity/Threat (SWOT) analysis per competitor
  • Competitive Landscape Mapping:
    • Market map visualization: competitors positioned by market segment and market share
    • Bubble chart: competitors by revenue (bubble size), win rate (x-axis), market overlap with MVL (y-axis)
    • Competitor activity heatmap by agency and NAICS
    • Emerging competitor alerts (new entrants to MVL's core markets)
  • Competitor Alerts:
    • New contract awards to tracked competitors
    • Competitor merger/acquisition/partnership news
    • Competitor leadership changes
    • Competitor protest activity
    • Competitor size standard changes (graduation from small business)
  • AI
  • AI Competitive Analyzer — Predicts which competitors will bid on a specific opportunity based on historical patterns, agency relationships, and capability match
  • AI Price-to-Win Modeler — Estimates competitor pricing strategies based on their historical award data and current market conditions

Page: Teaming & Partnership Intelligence

  • Fields Partner Name, Partnership Type (Prime/Sub/JV/Mentor-Protégé), Capabilities Complementary to MVL, Past Teaming History, Contract References, Status (Active/Prospective/Inactive), Agreement Type (TA/NDA/JV/MP), Agreement Status, Expiry Date
  • Buttons Add Partner Search Potential Partners View Teaming History Create Agreement Evaluate Fit Compare Partners View Joint Capabilities
  • Features:
  • Teaming Partner Discovery:
    • Search potential partners by: capability gap, NAICS, set-aside eligibility, clearance level, geographic presence
    • Partner scoring (capability fit, past performance, reliability, pricing competitiveness)
    • Complementary capability matching (MVL gaps → partner strengths)
    • Small business partner database (for SB subcontracting plans and mentor-protégé)
  • Teaming Agreement Management:
    • Teaming Agreement (TA) template library
    • Non-Disclosure Agreement (NDA) tracking
    • Joint Venture agreement management
    • Mentor-Protégé agreement tracking
    • Agreement status and expiration alerts
    • Teaming history database (past performance of teaming arrangements)
  • Joint Bid Capability Matrix:
    • Combined team past performance
    • Combined team key personnel availability
    • Combined team clearance posture
    • Work share allocation planning
    • Cost/price allocation between team members
