  • Buttons Create Capture Plan Edit Update Strategy Assign Team Set B&P Budget Schedule Gate Review View Competitor Assessment Generate Capture Brief Submit for Approval
  • Features:
  • Capture Plan Template Library:
    • Pre-built capture plan templates by contract type (FFP construction, T&M services, IDIQ task order)
    • Capture plan sections: Executive Summary, Customer Profile, Competitive Assessment, Win Strategy, Technical Solution Outline, Management Approach, Past Performance Mapping, Pricing Strategy, Teaming Plan, Risk Mitigation, Action Plan
    • Capture plan version control with change tracking
  • Win Strategy Development:
    • Win theme articulation (3-5 discriminating themes)
    • Technical discriminator mapping (unique capabilities)
    • Ghost strategy (competitive counter-positioning)
    • Customer hot button alignment (match solution to evaluation criteria)
    • Proof point library (past performance evidence for each claim)
  • B&P (Bid & Proposal) Budget Management:
    • B&P budget allocation per opportunity
    • B&P spend tracking (hours and costs)
    • B&P budget vs. actual dashboard
    • B&P ROI analysis (B&P investment vs. win rate and contract value)
    • Annual B&P budget planning and forecasting
  • Capture Action Tracking:
    • Action items with owners, due dates, and status
    • Customer engagement activities (meetings, calls, emails logged)
    • Competitor intelligence gathering tasks
    • Technical solution development milestones
    • Teaming partner engagement timeline
  • M365 Capture plan documents in SharePoint; Teams channel per capture effort; Outlook for action item reminders; Power BI for B&P budget dashboards

Page: Bid Kick-off Meeting & Planning

  • Fields Opportunity, Meeting Type (Capture Kick-off/Proposal Kick-off/Color Team/Strategy Review), Meeting Date, Attendees, Agenda Items, Action Items, Assignments, Due Dates, Meeting Notes, Decisions
  • Buttons Schedule Meeting Send Invites via Teams Record Minutes Track Action Items Generate Meeting Summary Distribute Notes

9.5 Tab 5: Proposal Development

Page: Technical Proposal Development

  • Fields Section Number, Section Title, Volume (Tech/Mgmt/Past Performance/Cost), Author, Content (rich text editor), Status (Outline/Draft/Review/Final), Reviewer(s), Review Comments, Version, Page Count, Word Count, Compliance Requirement(s) Addressed, Graphics/Figures Count
  • Buttons Create Section Assign Author Import Content Block Submit for Review Approve Compile Volume Export PDF Version Compare Check Compliance Track Changes
  • Features:
  • Proposal Template Library:
    • Pre-built proposal templates by contract type and agency
    • Standard volume structures: Technical Approach, Management Approach, Past Performance, Cost/Price, Small Business Participation Plan
    • Section templates with placeholder guidance
    • Boilerplate content library (company overview, quality approach, safety program)
  • Content Reuse & Knowledge Base:
    • Searchable library of past proposal sections indexed by: topic, agency, NAICS, evaluation criteria, win/loss
    • Content blocks with quality ratings (from win/loss outcomes)
    • Version-controlled content blocks (update once, update everywhere)
    • Past performance narratives database with structured fields: contract name, agency, value, period, scope, relevance, reference contact
  • Collaborative Authoring:
    • Multi-author concurrent editing with section-level locking
    • Track changes with author attribution
    • In-line commenting and discussion threads
    • Version comparison (diff view between draft versions)
    • Content approval workflows (author → section lead → volume lead → proposal manager)
  • Proposal Formatting & Branding:
    • Corporate branding templates (fonts, colors, logos, headers/footers)
    • Agency-specific formatting requirements (page limits, font sizes, margin requirements)
    • Automated page/figure/table numbering
    • Cross-reference management (Figure 1-2, Table 3-1)
    • Graphics and figures management with numbered references
  • Proposal Outline & Planning:
    • Shred the RFP (decompose RFP sections into compliance requirements)
    • Compliance matrix generation from RFP analysis
    • Section assignments with due dates and word/page limits
    • Proposal schedule with milestone tracking (storyboards, first draft, color teams, final)
    • Daily page count tracking
  • AI
  • AI Proposal Writer — Auto-generates proposal sections from previous wins, capability statements, and capture plan
  • AI Compliance Checker — Cross-references proposal content against RFP requirements to identify gaps and non-compliance

Page: Cost/Price Proposal Development

  • Fields Cost Element, Labor Category, Hours (Base Year + Option Years), Labor Rate (Loaded/Unloaded), Material Cost, Subcontractor Cost, ODCs (Other Direct Costs), Overhead Rate (%), G&A Rate (%), FCCM (Facilities Capital Cost of Money), Profit/Fee (%), Total by CLIN, Grand Total, Price-to-Win Target, Variance from Target
  • Buttons Build Cost Model Import Rates from Finance Calculate What-If Scenario Apply Wrap Rates Price-to-Win Analysis Review Finalize Generate Cost Volume Export to Excel
  • Features:
  • Cost Build-Up Engine:
    • Bottom-up labor cost estimation (labor categories × hours × rates)
    • Material cost estimation linked to Estimation module (Section 10)
    • Subcontractor cost inclusion with proposal integration
    • ODC estimation (travel, equipment, supplies, other)
    • Indirect rate application (overhead, G&A, FCCM)
    • Fee/profit calculation with justification
    • Multi-year cost modeling (base year + option years with escalation)
    • CLIN-level cost roll-up
    • Cost comparison across what-if scenarios (side-by-side)
  • Price-to-Win Analysis:
    • Historical award data analysis (what prices won similar contracts?)
    • Competitor pricing estimation based on award history
    • Price sensitivity analysis (win probability at different price points)
    • Strategic pricing options (aggressive/competitive/premium)
    • Price-to-win target setting with margin analysis
  • Rate Reconciliation:
    • Import approved indirect rates from Finance module (Section 5)
    • Forward pricing rate proposal alignment
    • Rate comparison (proposed vs. approved vs. market)
    • Incurred cost rate vs. proposed rate variance analysis

Page: Proposal Quality Assurance & Color Team Reviews

  • Fields Review Type (Outline/Pink Team/Red Team/Gold Team/Final QC), Review Date, Reviewers (list), Section, Finding Category (Strengths/Weaknesses/Deficiencies/Suggestions), Finding, Severity (Critical/Major/Minor), Status (Open/In Work/Resolved/Accepted), Assigned To, Resolution
  • Buttons Schedule Review Assign Reviewers Start Review Record Finding Track Resolution Generate Review Report Approve for Next Stage Final Compliance Check
  • Features:
  • Color Team Review Process:
    • Outline Review — Validate approach and section assignments before writing begins
    • Pink Team — Review first drafts for approach, theme compliance, and content gaps
    • Red Team — Simulate government evaluation; score proposal using stated evaluation criteria
    • Gold Team — Executive review of final draft; approve pricing and win strategy
    • Final QC — Compliance verification, formatting, page count, cross-references
  • Review scoring using government evaluation factors (Outstanding/Good/Acceptable/Marginal/Unacceptable)
  • Finding tracking with required resolution before advancement
  • Review report generation with findings summary and action items
  • Compliance matrix verification (every RFP requirement addressed)
  • Cross-reference verification (figures, tables, section references)
  • Page/word count verification against RFP limits

    • Searchable lessons learned indexed by: agency, contract type, NAICS, evaluation factor
    • Lessons automatically fed back into capture planning and proposal development
    • Win theme effectiveness tracking (which themes correlate with wins)
    • Pricing strategy effectiveness analysis
    • Competitor strategy pattern recognition
  • AI
  • AI Win/Loss Analyzer — Builds predictive model from all historical bid data; identifies patterns that predict wins/losses; recommends strategy adjustments
  • AI Debrief Insight Extractor — Analyzes debrief notes to extract actionable insights and maps them to future capture strategies

    • CDRL list with delivery dates, formats, distribution, approval authority
    • CDRL status tracking (Draft/Submitted/Approved/Rejected/Resubmit)
    • CDRL calendar with deadline alerts
    • Link to EDMS (Section 12) for deliverable document management
  • Contract Modifications & Amendments:
    • Modification tracking (bilateral/unilateral, administrative, funding, scope change)
    • Modification impact analysis (cost, schedule, scope)
    • Amendment text diff comparison (original vs. modified language)
    • Modification approval workflow
    • Running contract value tracking (original + all modifications)
  • Past Performance Management:
    • CPARS (Contractor Performance Assessment Reporting System) tracking
    • Self-assessment preparation
    • PPIRS (Past Performance Information Retrieval System) monitoring
    • Past performance narrative maintenance for future proposals
  • AI
  • AI Amendment Analyzer — Classifies modification significance and drafts acknowledgment letters
  • AI CPARS Advisor — Prepares self-assessment narrative suggestions based on project performance data

9.8 Tab 8: Market Intelligence & Analytics (Replaces GovWin IQ Analytics)

Page: Government Market Intelligence Dashboard

  • Features:
  • Market Size & Trending:
    • Total addressable market (TAM) by NAICS/PSC
    • Market growth/decline trends (5-year history + 3-year forecast)
    • Government spend by agency relevant to MVL capabilities
    • Construction market segment analysis (federal, military, infrastructure)
    • Budget cycle analysis (impact of CRs, shutdowns, supplementals)
  • MVL Market Position Analysis:
    • MVL market share by agency, NAICS, geography
    • Market share trending (growing/stable/declining)
    • Revenue concentration risk (over-reliance on single agency/contract)
    • Competitive position mapping (leader/challenger/follower/niche)
  • Opportunity Forecast Modeling:
    • Predicted opportunity pipeline (based on budget data, recompete calendar, agency forecasts)
    • Revenue forecast (awarded + weighted pipeline + market growth)
    • Scenario modeling (optimistic/most likely/pessimistic)
    • Growth target gap analysis (forecast vs. strategic plan)
  • State & Local Government Intelligence:
    • State government procurement portals aggregation
    • State DOT construction spending analysis
    • Municipal bond-funded project tracking
    • P3 (Public-Private Partnership) opportunity monitoring
  • Custom Analytics & Reports:
    • Ad-hoc query builder (filter by any combination of fields)
    • Saved report templates (weekly pipeline review, monthly BD report, quarterly market analysis)
    • Scheduled report distribution (email to leadership team)
    • Export to Excel/PDF/Power BI
  • M365 Power BI dashboards embedded with full drill-through capability; Scheduled reports via Outlook; Executive pipeline review deck auto-generation

§10. Module 6: Estimation & Costing — Enterprise Estimation Platform

Purpose: Enterprise-grade construction cost estimation platform combining native cost database engine (replaces RSMeans dependency), digital takeoff (replaces PlanSwift 11 Pro), bill of quantities management (replaces RIB CANDY/CCS), and comprehensive estimate build-up. Features resource-based estimating, operational estimating, unit rate estimating, assemblies, location cost indexing, crew-based productivity calculations, and bi-directional feedback from completed projects. This module is the single source of truth for all pre-construction and estimation activities across every MVL project globally.

M365 Excel Online for estimate worksheets and rate data import. Power BI for estimation accuracy analytics, cost trending, and benchmark dashboards. SharePoint for rate library documents, specification storage, and drawing files. Teams for estimate review sessions and bid coordination. Outlook for estimate submission notifications and approval workflows.

Key Personas: Chief Estimator, Senior Estimators, Quantity Surveyors, Cost Engineers, Takeoff Specialists, Bid Managers, Pre-construction Directors

Tech React 18 canvas/WebGL for drawing rendering, PDF.js for plan viewing, Azure Computer Vision for drawing analysis, Azure SQL for cost database, Azure Blob for drawing storage, SignalR for real-time collaboration, Azure OpenAI for AI estimation features, Geometry calculation engine (area/linear/volume/count), Azure Functions for cost calculations

10.1 Tab 1: Native Cost Database Engine (Replaces RSMeans)

CRITICAL: This is a NATIVE cost database built WITHIN the ERP — NOT an API connection to RSMeans. The MVL ERP owns, maintains, and updates its own comprehensive construction cost data using the same methodology and data structure as RSMeans, but with full control, customization, and integration into all estimation workflows.

Page: Cost Data Administration & Configuration

  • Fields Database Version, Base Year, Current Year, Update Frequency (Quarterly/Annual), Data Region (US/International), Classification System (MasterFormat CSI), Active Divisions, Total Line Items Count, Last Update Date, Update Source (Internal Research/Market Survey/Vendor Quotes/Project Actuals), Data Quality Score
  • Buttons Configure Database Import Base Data Run Update Cycle Validate Data Integrity Publish New Version Archive Previous Version View Change Log Export Database Set Update Schedule Run Benchmark Comparison
  • Features:
  • MasterFormat CSI Classification System — Full 50-division structure:
    • Division 01: General Requirements (temporary facilities, project management, cleanup)
    • Division 02: Existing Conditions (demolition, site remediation, hazmat abatement)
    • Division 03: Concrete (formwork, reinforcing, cast-in-place, precast, grouting)
    • Division 04: Masonry (unit masonry, stone, CMU, brick, mortar, reinforcement)
    • Division 05: Metals (structural steel, metal joists, metal decking, fabrications, railings)
    • Division 06: Wood, Plastics, Composites (rough carpentry, finish carpentry, millwork)
    • Division 07: Thermal & Moisture Protection (waterproofing, insulation, roofing, sealants, fireproofing)
    • Division 08: Openings (doors, windows, curtain walls, hardware, glazing)
    • Division 09: Finishes (plaster, gypsum board, tiling, terrazzo, flooring, painting, wall coverings)
    • Division 10: Specialties (signage, toilet accessories, fire extinguishers, lockers, partitions)
    • Division 11: Equipment (kitchen, laundry, athletic, lab, loading dock)
    • Division 12: Furnishings (casework, window treatments, furniture, rugs)
    • Division 13: Special Construction (clean rooms, radiation protection, seismic isolation)
    • Division 14: Conveying Equipment (elevators, escalators, dumbwaiters, material handling)
    • Division 21: Fire Suppression (sprinkler systems, standpipes, fire pumps)
    • Division 22: Plumbing (fixtures, piping, pumps, water heaters, drainage)
    • Division 23: HVAC (ductwork, piping, equipment, controls, testing/balancing)
    • Division 25: Integrated Automation (BAS, lighting controls, HVAC controls)
    • Division 26: Electrical (power distribution, lighting, wiring, grounding, generators)
    • Division 27: Communications (structured cabling, data networks, AV, paging)
    • Division 28: Electronic Safety (fire alarm, detection, mass notification, security)
    • Division 31: Earthwork (grading, excavation, fill, dewatering, shoring)
    • Division 32: Exterior Improvements (paving, curbs, fences, landscaping, irrigation)
    • Division 33: Utilities (water, sanitary sewer, storm drainage, gas, electrical distribution)
    • Division 34: Transportation (roads, bridges, rail, airfield)
    • Division 35: Waterway and Marine (waterway structures, dredging, marine)
    • Division 40-49: Process Integration (process piping, equipment, instrumentation)
  • Cost Data Line Item Structure — Each line item contains:
    • Line Number (hierarchical: XX.XX.XX.XXXX)
    • Description (short + detailed)
    • Crew Code reference
    • Daily Output (units per day for the assigned crew)
    • Labor Hours per unit
    • Unit of Measure (SF, LF, CF, CY, EA, TON, LB, GAL, etc.)
    • Bare Costs: Material ($), Labor ($), Equipment ($), Total ($)
    • Total Including O&P: Material ($), Labor ($), Equipment ($), Total ($)
    • Productivity factors
    • Waste factors (%)
    • Notes/Specifications
  • Database versioning with full audit trail
  • Multi-region data support (US base + international locations)
  • Annual database refresh cycle with quarterly interim updates
  • Import capability from vendor price lists, supplier quotes, and project actuals
  • AI
  • AI Data Validator — Cross-references cost data against market indices, inflation rates, and historical trends; flags anomalies
  • AI Rate Predictor — Uses ML to predict future cost trends based on commodity prices, labor market data, and economic indicators

Page: Labor Rate Database

  • Fields Trade Code, Trade Name (e.g., Carpenter, Electrician, Plumber, Ironworker, Laborer, Operating Engineer, Pipefitter, Sheet Metal Worker, Painter, Roofer, Insulator, Glazier, Tile Setter, Cement Mason, Bricklayer), Rate Type (Union/Open Shop/Prevailing Wage/Davis-Bacon), Base Hourly Rate, Fringe Benefits (Health & Welfare, Pension, Vacation, Training, Annuity), Total Hourly Rate, Workers Comp Rate (%), State, Location/City, Effective Date, Expiry Date, Source (Union Agreement/DOL/Survey/Internal), Installing Contractor's O&P Markup (%)
  • Buttons Add Trade Edit Rate Import Union Rates Import Davis-Bacon Rates Compare Locations View Rate History Apply Annual Increase Clone to New Location Bulk Update Export Set Effective Date Range
  • Features:
  • Complete Trade Classification Library:
    • 60+ trade classifications with sub-specialties
    • Union rate tables by local/jurisdiction
    • Open shop rates by region
    • Davis-Bacon prevailing wage rates by county (DOL import)
    • International labor rates (UAE, Japan, Greece, Italy)
  • Rate Composition Breakdown:
    • Base Rate + Health & Welfare + Pension + Vacation + Training + Annuity + Dues = Total Bare Rate
    • Total Bare Rate + Workers Comp + Liability Insurance + Taxes = Total Cost to Employer
    • Total Cost + Contractor's O&P = Total Billing Rate
  • Rate comparison across locations/cities for same trade
  • Historical rate trending (5+ year history per trade)
  • Automatic Davis-Bacon rate import from SAM.gov/DOL Wage Determinations
  • Rate escalation modeling (annual % increase projections)
  • Overtime rate calculations (1.5x, 2x) by jurisdiction
  • Shift differential rates (swing shift, graveyard)
  • M365 Excel import/export for rate tables; Power BI rate comparison dashboards

Page: Crew Composition Database

  • Fields Crew Code (e.g., C-1, C-2, B-1, B-2, E-1, Q-1), Crew Name/Description, Crew Members (list of trades with quantity per trade), Equipment Included (list of equipment with quantity), Daily Crew Cost (sum of all labor + equipment), Hourly Crew Cost, Standard Daily Output (units per day), Unit of Measure, Productivity Factor, Notes
  • Buttons Add Crew Edit Crew Clone Crew Calculate Crew Cost Import Standard Crews View Crew Details Compare Crews Set Output Rates Export Library Link to Line Items
  • Features:
  • Standard Crew Library (200+ pre-defined crews):
    • Building trades crews (B-1 through B-90+): Bricklaying, concrete, carpentry, drywall, flooring
    • Civil/Earthwork crews (C-1 through C-35+): Excavation, grading, paving, utilities
    • Electrical crews (E-1 through E-20+): Power distribution, lighting, low-voltage
    • Plumbing crews (Q-1 through Q-15+): Piping, fixtures, drainage
    • HVAC crews (H-1 through H-15+): Ductwork, piping, equipment
    • Structural steel crews (S-1 through S-15+): Erection, welding, detailing
    • Roofing crews (R-1 through R-10+)
    • Painting crews (P-1 through P-10+)
    • Demolition crews (D-1 through D-10+)
  • Crew Cost Calculation Engine:
    • Crew Cost = Σ(Workers × Trade Rate) + Σ(Equipment × Equipment Rate)
    • Labor Cost Per Unit = (Crew Daily Labor Cost) / Daily Output
    • Equipment Cost Per Unit = (Crew Daily Equipment Cost) / Daily Output
    • Labor Hours Per Unit = (Total Crew Labor Hours) / Daily Output
  • Custom crew creation with drag-and-drop trade/equipment assignment
  • Crew productivity adjustment for conditions (weather, site access, height, complexity)
  • Crew comparison tool (output per dollar analysis)
  • Clone and modify crews for project-specific conditions

Page: Equipment Rate Database

  • Material substitution recommendations (equivalent specs, lower cost)
  • Automatic price refresh from vendor portals and commodity feeds
  • AI AI Price Tracker — Monitors commodity indexes (steel, copper, lumber, concrete) and auto-adjusts material costs; alerts estimators when prices shift significantly

Page: City Cost Index & Location Factors

  • Fields City/Region, State/Country, Zip/Postal Code, Material Factor, Installation Factor (Labor), Equipment Factor, Weighted Average Factor, Base City (national average = 1.00), Effective Date, Division-Specific Factors (per CSI Division)
  • Buttons Add Location Edit Factor Import Indexes Calculate Adjusted Cost Compare Locations View Map Generate Location Report Apply to Estimate Historical Trend Custom Factor
  • Features:
  • City Cost Index (CCI) Engine — 900+ locations:
    • US: All 50 states, 900+ cities/zip codes
    • International: UAE (Abu Dhabi, Dubai, Al Ain), Japan (Tokyo, Yokosuka, Okinawa), Greece (Athens, Souda Bay), Italy (Naples, Vicenza, Aviano)
    • Military installations (OCONUS adjustment factors for MILCON)
  • Location Factor Methodology:
    • Material Factor: Reflects local material pricing vs national average
    • Installation Factor: Reflects local labor rates vs national average (union/open shop)
    • Equipment Factor: Reflects local equipment costs vs national average
    • Weighted Average: Combined factor based on typical cost distribution (materials 40%, labor 45%, equipment 15%)
  • Division-specific factors (e.g., concrete labor may vary differently than electrical labor)
  • Historical index trending (year-over-year changes)
  • Cost adjustment calculation: Base Cost × Location Factor = Adjusted Local Cost
  • OCONUS adjustment factors for overseas military construction
  • GSA/USACE area cost factor integration
  • Custom location factor creation for unique project sites
  • AI AI Location Factor Predictor — Analyzes economic indicators, construction activity levels, and labor market data to predict future location factor changes

Page: Cost Index & Escalation Engine

  • Fields Index Type (30-City Average, Division-Specific, Trade-Specific, Material-Specific), Base Year, Current Year, Index Value, Annual Change (%), 5-Year CAGR, Source, Effective Date
  • Buttons View Index History Calculate Escalation Project Future Costs Compare Periods Apply to Estimate Import External Indexes Generate Trend Report
  • Features:
  • Historical Cost Indexes (20+ year history):
    • 30-city composite index
    • Per-division indexes (all 50 CSI divisions)
    • Per-trade indexes (labor-specific: carpenter, electrician, etc.)
    • Per-material indexes (concrete, steel, lumber, copper)
    • Regional composite indexes
  • Escalation Calculator:
    • Present-to-Future: Cost Today × (Future Index / Current Index) = Projected Cost
    • Past-to-Present: Historical Cost × (Current Index / Past Index) = Current Cost
    • Multi-year escalation with compounding
  • Forecasting Engine:
    • Linear, polynomial, and ML-based trend projection
    • Confidence intervals (P10, P50, P90)
    • What-if scenarios (economic downturn, boom, moderate growth)
  • Integration with ENR (Engineering News-Record) construction cost indexes
  • BLS Producer Price Index (PPI) data import for material categories
  • Custom escalation profiles for specific project types
  • AI AI Escalation Forecaster — Uses economic modeling, commodity futures, and labor market data to generate probabilistic cost escalation forecasts with confidence intervals

10.3 Tab 3: Bill of Quantities (BOQ) Management (Replaces RIB CANDY/CCS)

Native BOQ management engine replacing RIB CANDY/CCS capabilities — supports unit rate estimating, resource-based estimating, operational estimating, assemblies/composites, nested items, rate build-up, and comprehensive tender management.

Page: BOQ Creation & Management

  • Fields BOQ ID, Project, Client, Contract Reference, BOQ Type (Elemental/Trade/Operational), Version, Currency, Base Date, Location, Status (Draft/Priced/Reviewed/Submitted/Awarded), Created By, Last Modified
  • Buttons Create New BOQ Import BOQ Clone BOQ Edit Add Section Add Page Add Item Delete Reorder Renumber Calculate Totals Apply Location Factors Lock Unlock Submit Compare Versions Export Excel Export PDF Print
  • Features:
  • BOQ Structure (Hierarchical):
    • BOQ → Sections → Pages → Items → Sub-Items
    • Section: Major work category (e.g., Substructure, Superstructure, Finishes, Services)
    • Page: Sub-category within section (e.g., Concrete Work, Masonry, Structural Steel)
    • Item: Individual measured work item (e.g., "Reinforced concrete grade C30, 200mm thick slab")
    • Sub-Item: Resource breakdown or assembly components
  • Item Types:
    • Measured Items: Quantity × Rate = Amount
    • Provisional Sums: Defined/Undefined (per contract)
    • Prime Cost Items: Specialist items with attendant profit/markup
    • Daywork: Labor/material/plant at scheduled rates
    • Preliminaries: Time-related and fixed charges
    • Contingencies: Risk allowances (% or lump sum)
  • Measurement Rules Support:
    • SMM7 / NRM2 / CESMM4 / POMI
    • Custom measurement rules per client/contract
    • Dimension entry with formulas
    • Waste factor application per item
    • Conversion factor support
  • BOQ auto-generation from digital takeoff measurements
  • BOQ import from Excel (standard templates)
  • BOQ import from industry formats (CITE, BIM BOQ)
  • Version control with delta comparison between versions
  • Multi-currency BOQ with automatic conversion

Page: Resource-Based Estimating & Rate Build-Up

  • Fields BOQ Item, Estimation Method (Unit Rate/Resource-Based/Operational), Resources (Labor/Material/Equipment list), Quantity per unit, Resource Rate, Waste %, Productivity Factor, All-In Rate, Built-Up Rate, Markup %, Final Rate
  • Buttons Build Up Rate Add Resource Remove Resource Apply from Library Save to Library Calculate All-In Rate Compare Methods View Breakdown Apply Gang Rate Adjust Productivity Copy Rate Build-Up
  • Features:
  • Unit Rate Estimating:
    • Apply rate from cost database directly to BOQ item
    • Rate = Material + Labor + Equipment per unit
    • Adjust for location, conditions, access, complexity
  • Resource-Based Estimating (Bottom-Up):
    • Build rate from individual resources:
    • Labor: Trade × hours × rate = labor cost per unit
    • Material: Item × quantity × unit cost = material cost per unit (+ waste)
    • Equipment: Type × hours × rate = equipment cost per unit
    • Subcontractor: Lump sum or per unit
    • All-in rate = Σ(Resource Costs) + Overhead + Profit
  • Operational Estimating:
    • Method/Gang-based approach
    • Define operation (e.g., "Pour 200mm concrete slab")
    • Assign gang/crew with productivity rate
    • Calculate cost based on gang cost ÷ daily output
  • Gang/Crew Rate Calculation:
    • Gang = collection of tradespeople + equipment
    • Gang Daily Cost = Σ(workers × daily rate) + Σ(equipment × daily rate)
    • Cost per unit = Gang Daily Cost / Daily Output
  • Assembly/Composite Items:
    • Create composite items from multiple resources
    • Nested assemblies (assembly within assembly)
    • Standard assembly library (wall types, floor types, ceiling types, MEP systems)
    • Assembly modification preserves structure while updating rates
  • Productivity Factors:
    • Base productivity (ideal conditions)
    • Weather adjustment factor
    • Height adjustment factor (work above ground level)
    • Congestion/access factor
    • Learning curve factor (repetitive work efficiency gain)
    • Overtime productivity decline factor
  • Rate build-up audit trail (full breakdown visible at all times)
  • Rate comparison tool (compare built-up rate vs market rate vs historical actual)
  • Save rate build-ups to reusable library

Page: BOQ Pricing & Extension

  • Fields BOQ Item, Quantity, Unit, Material Rate, Labor Rate, Equipment Rate, Sub Rate, Total Rate, Extended Amount, Section Subtotal, BOQ Grand Total, Markup Summary
  • Buttons Price All Items Apply Rates from Library Apply Location Factors Calculate Extensions View Pricing Summary Apply Markups Adjust Rates Lock Pricing Generate Cash Flow What-If Scenario Compare to Budget
  • Features:
  • Pricing Engine:
    • Auto-price from cost database (match BOQ items to line items)
    • Manual rate entry with override capability
    • Blended rate calculation (weighted average of multiple sources)
    • Rate rounding rules (nearest cent, nearest dollar)
    • Currency conversion for multi-currency BOQs
  • Markup Management:
    • Overhead (site overhead + company overhead)
    • Profit margin (% or lump sum)
    • Bond cost (performance bond, payment bond)
    • Insurance (builder's risk, liability, workers comp)
    • Contingency (design contingency, construction contingency)
    • Escalation (inflation adjustment for project duration)
    • Fee (management fee for cost-plus contracts)
    • Tax (sales tax, use tax by jurisdiction)
    • Markup cascade: Base Cost → + Site OH → + Company OH → + Profit → + Bond → + Contingency = Sell Price
  • Markup by section (different margins for different trades)
  • What-if pricing scenarios (change material spec, change labor source, etc.)
  • Price comparison between estimates/versions

Page: Tender & Bid Management

  • Fields Tender ID, Project, Client, Due Date/Time, Tender Type (Open/Selective/Negotiated), Status (In Progress/Submitted/Awarded/Lost), Bid Amount, Competitor Analysis, Win Probability, Margin %, Notes
  • Buttons Create Tender Manage Subcontractor Quotes Level Bids Tabulate Bids Compare Bids Select Best Bid Generate Tender Summary Submit Tender Post-Tender Analysis
  • Features:
  • Subcontractor Quote Management:
    • Send bid packages to subcontractors (scope, drawings, specifications)
    • Receive and log subcontractor quotations
    • Quote comparison/leveling (normalize scope differences)
    • Bid tabulation matrix (all subs by trade, side-by-side)
    • Scope gap analysis (identify unpriced scope items)
    • Selected bid tracking with reason documentation
  • Bid Analysis:
    • Cost per SF analysis (compare to benchmarks)
    • Trade cost distribution analysis (% by trade)
    • Margin sensitivity analysis
    • Win probability scoring (based on historical data, competition, client relationship)
  • Post-award cost tracking (estimate vs actual)
  • Lessons learned capture for future estimates

Page: Cash Flow Forecasting

  • Buttons Generate Cash Flow Link to Schedule Adjust Timing View S-Curve Export Compare Scenarios Apply Payment Terms
  • Features:
  • Cash flow projection from BOQ quantities × schedule timing

  • Payment application forecast (progress claims)

  • Working capital requirement analysis
  • Multi-project portfolio cash flow consolidation
  • What-if scenarios (delay impact on cash flow)
  • AI AI Cash Flow Optimizer — Analyzes historical payment patterns by client and recommends optimal billing timing to maximize cash position

10.4 Tab 4: Estimate Build-Up & Review

Page: Estimate Creation & Configuration

  • Fields Estimate ID (auto-generated EST-YYYY-NNNN), Project, Client, Contract Type (FFP/CPFF/T&M/GMP/Unit Price/Design-Build), Estimate Type (Conceptual/Preliminary/Detailed/Final), Estimate Class (AACE Class 5/4/3/2/1), Version, WBS Alignment, Base Date, Location, Currency, Status (Draft/Under Review/Approved/Submitted/Locked)
  • Buttons Create Estimate Clone from Template Import BOQ Import Takeoff Link to Proposal Set WBS Configure Markups Set Basis of Estimate Submit for Review Lock Estimate
  • Features:
  • AACE Estimate Classification:
    • Class 5: Conceptual (order of magnitude, -50%/+100%)
    • Class 4: Feasibility (parametric, -30%/+50%)
    • Class 3: Budget/Authorization (semi-detailed, -20%/+30%)
    • Class 2: Control (detailed, -15%/+20%)
    • Class 1: Check/Bid (definitive, -10%/+15%)
  • Estimate from multiple sources: BOQ + Takeoff + Subcontractor Quotes + Historical Data
  • Estimate-to-schedule integration (cost loading the schedule)
  • Estimate basis documentation (assumptions, exclusions, qualifications)
  • Estimate template library by project type
  • Multi-currency estimate consolidation

  • Estimate version comparison (line-by-line delta with visual highlights)

10.7 Tab 7: Job Order Contracting (JOC) Engine (Replaces Gordian JOC / eGordian)

CRITICAL: This replicates the complete Gordian Job Order Contracting (JOC) platform natively — providing unit price book-based ordering, JOC proposal generation, task order management, and contractor performance tracking. JOC enables rapid procurement of renovation, repair, and minor construction work using pre-priced unit price books (UPBs) without individual competitive bidding for each task order.

Page: JOC Contract & Unit Price Book (UPB) Administration

  • Fields JOC Contract ID, Contract Name, Owner/Agency, Contract Value (Ceiling), Min/Max Task Order Value, Effective Date, Expiry Date, Option Periods, Coefficient (Multiplier), UPB Version (Year/Edition), UPB Line Item Count, Geographic Area, Status (Active/Expired/Pending), Contractor(s) Assigned
  • Buttons Create JOC Contract Import UPB Set Coefficient Configure Task Order Rules Assign Contractors View Capacity Renew Contract View Analytics Export
  • Features:
  • Unit Price Book (UPB) Management:
    • Import and manage Gordian Construction Task Catalog® (CTC) data or custom UPBs
    • UPB line items with pre-established unit prices (material + labor + equipment)
    • Coefficient/multiplier application (adjustment factor per contract — e.g., 0.95 for high-volume, 1.10 for remote locations)
    • UPB version management and annual updates
    • Custom line item additions (for items not in standard UPB)
    • UPB categories aligned with MasterFormat CSI divisions
    • Price adjustment mechanisms (annual escalation, fuel surcharge)
    • Non-pre-priced (NPP) item management (for items outside UPB scope)
  • JOC Contract Configuration:
    • Multi-contractor JOC contracts (rotate or compete between contractors)
    • Task order value limits (min/max per task order)
    • Annual capacity tracking (remaining contract value)
    • Contract type support: IDIQ/JOC, MATOC/JOC, SATOC/JOC
    • Geographic scope configuration (by installation, region, or nationwide)
    • Small business set-aside tracking and reporting

Page: JOC Task Order / Delivery Order Management

  • Fields Task Order (TO) Number, JOC Contract Reference, Project/Facility, Description of Work, Location (Building/Room/Area), Scope Category (Renovation/Repair/Maintenance/Minor Construction), Urgency (Routine/Urgent/Emergency), Requested By, JOC Manager, Assigned Contractor, Estimated Value, Coefficient-Adjusted Value, Status (Draft/Scoping/Priced/Review/Approved/In Progress/Complete/Closed), Start Date, Completion Date, NTE (Not to Exceed) Amount
  • Buttons Create Task Order Scope Work Build Price Proposal Submit for Review Approve Issue to Contractor Track Progress Process Payment Close Out Modify Cancel
  • Features:
  • JOC Proposal Development (Replaces eGordian Proposal):
    • Visual scope builder (select UPB line items for task order)
    • Quantity assignment per line item
    • Automatic price calculation (quantity × unit price × coefficient)
    • Line item grouping by phase, location, or trade
    • Non-pre-priced (NPP) item entry with supporting documentation
    • Proposal summary with total price breakdown
    • Independent Government Estimate (IGE) generation for comparison
    • Proposal-to-IGE variance analysis (flag if contractor proposal > 110% of IGE)
    • Multiple proposal revisions with comparison tracking
  • Task Order Workflow:
    • Request intake (facility manager submits work request)
    • Site visit scheduling and documentation
    • Scope development with UPB line item selection
    • Contractor proposal submission and review
    • Government/owner review and approval
    • Notice to Proceed (NTP) issuance
    • Progress tracking with milestone payments
    • Completion inspection and punch list
    • Final acceptance and closeout
    • Payment processing linked to Finance module (Section 5)
  • Task Order Dashboard:
    • Active task orders by status, contractor, facility, value
    • Task order aging (days in each status)
    • Capacity utilization (% of JOC contract ceiling used)
    • Monthly/quarterly spend trending
    • Average task order cycle time (request to completion)

Page: JOC Contractor Management & Performance

  • Fields Contractor Name, JOC Contract(s), Performance Rating (1-5), On-Time Completion %, Quality Score, Safety Record, Task Orders Completed, Total Value Completed, Average Cycle Time, Current Workload, Capacity Available
  • Buttons View Profile View Task Orders Rate Performance Generate Scorecard Compare Contractors Assign Task Order View History
  • Features:
  • Contractor performance scorecards (quality, timeliness, safety, responsiveness)
  • Contractor workload balancing (distribute task orders based on capacity)
  • Contractor prequalification tracking
  • Performance-based task order assignment (higher-rated contractors get priority)
  • Contractor compliance tracking (insurance, bonding, licensing, DBE goals)
  • AI
  • AI JOC Estimator — Auto-selects UPB line items from natural language scope descriptions; suggests quantities based on similar past task orders
  • AI Contractor Matcher — Recommends optimal contractor assignment based on workload, performance history, and scope expertise
  • AI Task Order Predictor — Forecasts upcoming task order volume based on facility age, condition data, and historical patterns

10.8 Tab 8: Facility Condition Assessment (FCA) Engine (Replaces Gordian FCA)

CRITICAL: This replicates the Gordian Facility Condition Assessment platform — providing systematic facility inspection, condition scoring, deficiency tracking, and capital planning for entire facility portfolios. FCA data drives preventive maintenance priorities, capital budget requests, and JOC task order generation.

Page: Facility Portfolio & Configuration

  • Fields Facility ID, Facility Name, Type (Office/Warehouse/Barracks/Hospital/Lab/Hangar/SCIF/School/Training Center/Maintenance Shop), Location (Installation/Base/Campus), Address, Gross Square Footage, Year Built, Year Last Renovated, Replacement Value (CRV — Current Replacement Value), Number of Floors, Number of Systems (HVAC/Electrical/Plumbing/Structural/Envelope/Interior/Site), Condition Index (FCI), Mission Dependency Index (MDI), Status (Active/Standby/Surplus/Scheduled for Demolition)
  • Buttons Add Facility Edit Import Portfolio Schedule Assessment View Condition Summary View Deficiencies Generate Capital Plan View History Export Portfolio Map View
  • Features:
  • Facility Portfolio Management:
    • Complete facility inventory with key attributes
    • Facility hierarchy (installation → building → floor → room → system)
    • Floor plan integration (linked to PDF/CAD drawings in EDMS Section 12)
    • Photo documentation per facility
    • Facility classification by type, mission criticality, and condition
    • Portfolio map view (GIS integration showing facility locations with color-coded condition)
    • Replacement value calculation engine (parametric cost per SF by building type)
  • Facility Condition Index (FCI) Calculation:
    • FCI = Deferred Maintenance Backlog / Current Replacement Value (CRV)
    • FCI Rating: Good (0-5%), Fair (5-10%), Poor (10-30%), Critical (>30%)
    • FCI trending over time (improving/stable/declining)
    • FCI benchmarks by facility type (compare against industry standards)
    • Portfolio-level FCI aggregation

Page: Facility Condition Assessment Execution

  • Fields Assessment ID, Facility, Assessment Type (Comprehensive/Focused/Rapid/Follow-Up), Assessor(s), Assessment Date, Systems Inspected (list), Deficiencies Found, Total Repair Cost, Assessment Status (Scheduled/In Progress/Draft Report/Final), Next Assessment Due
  • Buttons Create Assessment Assign Assessor Start Assessment Record Deficiency Add Photo Complete Assessment Generate Report Submit for Review Approve
  • Features:
  • Assessment Methodology (ASTM E2018 / BUILDER SMS):
    • Systematic inspection of all building systems:
    • Structural — Foundation, columns, beams, walls, slabs, load-bearing elements
    • Envelope/Exterior — Roof, exterior walls, windows, doors, waterproofing, caulking
    • Interior — Floors, ceilings, walls, doors, finishes, stairs, railings
    • HVAC — Heating, cooling, ventilation, controls, ductwork, piping
    • Plumbing — Piping, fixtures, water heaters, drainage, pumps
    • Electrical — Distribution, panels, wiring, lighting, emergency power, fire alarm
    • Conveying — Elevators, escalators, dumbwaiters
    • Life Safety — Fire suppression, fire detection, egress, emergency lighting
    • Site — Paving, sidewalks, landscaping, fencing, drainage, utilities
    • Condition rating per system/component (1-5 scale or Good/Fair/Poor/Critical)
    • Remaining useful life (RUL) estimation per component
    • Photo documentation linked to each deficiency
    • Voice-to-text field notes (transcribed by AI)
  • Mobile Assessment App (PWA):
    • Offline-capable inspection forms
    • Photo capture with auto-GPS tagging
    • Barcode/QR scan for equipment identification
    • Voice recording for notes
    • Sync when connectivity restored
    • Floor plan navigation with tap-to-locate deficiencies

Page: Deficiency Register & Prioritization

  • Fields Deficiency ID, Facility, System, Component, Location (Floor/Room), Description, Condition Rating, Photo(s), Estimated Repair Cost, Priority (Critical/High/Medium/Low), Urgency (Immediate/1 Year/2-3 Years/4-5 Years/6-10 Years), Category (Safety/Code Compliance/Operational/Aesthetic), Mission Impact (High/Medium/Low), Status (Identified/Planned/Funded/In Progress/Complete), Linked Task Order/Work Order
  • Buttons Add Deficiency Edit Prioritize Generate Work Order Generate JOC Task Order Link to Capital Plan Upload Photo View on Floor Plan Export Batch Update
  • Features:
  • Deficiency Prioritization Engine:
    • Multi-factor scoring: safety risk × code compliance × mission impact × cost × urgency
    • Configurable priority weighting by owner preferences
    • Auto-prioritization using scoring algorithm
    • Priority override with justification
    • Deficiency grouping (combine related deficiencies into single project)
  • Deficiency-to-Action Workflow:
    • Generate JOC Task Order directly from deficiency (auto-populate scope from deficiency description)
    • Generate EAM Work Order for maintenance items (linked to Section 23)
    • Link to Capital Plan for large-value items requiring budget approval
    • Track deficiency resolution through work completion
  • Deferred maintenance backlog calculation (total unresolved deficiency cost)
  • Deficiency trending (new vs. resolved over time)
  • Recurring deficiency detection (same issue in same location — indicates systemic problem)
  • AI
  • AI Deficiency Classifier — Auto-categorizes deficiencies by system, severity, and priority from description and photos
  • AI Repair Cost Estimator — Estimates repair cost from deficiency description using UPB/cost database data
  • AI Condition Forecaster — Predicts future condition deterioration based on age, environment, usage, and maintenance history

Page: Capital Planning & Deferred Maintenance (Replaces Gordian Capital Planning)

  • Fields Capital Plan Name, Planning Horizon (5-Year/10-Year/20-Year), Fiscal Year, Facility/Portfolio, Total Deferred Maintenance Backlog, Annual Funding Request, Funded Amount, Unfunded Gap, FCI Target, Priority Projects (list), Funding Source (O&M/MILCON/SRM/FSRM/Client Budget)
  • Buttons Create Capital Plan Import Deficiencies Prioritize Projects Set Funding Scenarios Generate Budget Request Submit for Approval View Scenario Comparison Export Plan Generate Briefing Deck
  • Features:
  • Capital Planning Engine:
    • Multi-year capital investment planning (5/10/20-year horizons)
    • Project prioritization using weighted scoring (FCI impact, mission dependency, safety, cost-effectiveness)
    • Funding scenario modeling (what if we get 100%/75%/50% of requested budget?)
    • FCI projection under each funding scenario (show facility condition trajectory)
    • Deferred maintenance backlog trending (growing/stable/shrinking)
    • Optimized project sequencing (maximize FCI improvement per dollar invested)
    • Capital vs. maintenance classification (repair vs. replace analysis)
  • Budget Request Generation:
    • Automated capital budget request package generation
    • Project justification sheets with deficiency data, photos, cost estimates
    • Priority ranking with scoring methodology documentation
    • DoD-specific formats: DD Form 1391 (Military Construction), FSRM (Facility Sustainment, Restoration, and Modernization)
    • State/local government capital improvement plan (CIP) format
  • Lifecycle Cost Analysis:
    • Repair vs. replace decision support (present value analysis)
    • Component lifecycle curves (expected useful life by system/component)
    • Maintenance cost impact on capital timing (deferring replacement increases annual maintenance cost)
    • Total cost of ownership modeling
  • Integration with Project Module (Section 7):
    • Approved capital projects auto-create project records
    • Project completion updates facility condition data
    • As-built information feeds back to facility records

§11. Module 7: Construction Field Management — Enterprise Field Platform (Replaces Procore)

Purpose: Enterprise construction field management platform replicating ALL Procore capabilities — daily logs, observations, RFIs, submittals, punch lists, photos, drawings, correspondence, closeout, and complete field productivity tracking. Fully integrated with Project Management, Estimation, QMS, HSE, and Finance modules for seamless data flow.

M365 Power Apps for mobile field forms. OneDrive offline sync for field teams. Teams for field communications and project channels. SharePoint for photo storage, daily reports, and specification library. Power BI for field analytics, labor productivity, and project dashboards. Outlook for RFI/submittal notifications with actionable buttons.

Key Personas: Site Superintendents, Field Engineers, QC Inspectors, Safety Officers, Project Engineers, Foremen, Subcontractor PMs

Tech React Native PWA for mobile, offline-first with IndexedDB, Azure Blob Storage for photos, SignalR for real-time sync, Azure Computer Vision for photo analysis, GPS/geolocation API

  • Buttons Create Submittal Upload Documents Submit to Reviewer Review Approve Approve as Noted Revise & Resubmit Reject Forward Return Resubmit Close View Log Export Report Batch Submit Transmit via EDMS
  • Features:

§12. Module 8: Enterprise Document Management System (EDMS) — Full Aconex-Style Platform

Purpose: Enterprise-grade document management, correspondence control, transmittal management, and collaborative review platform replicating the full capabilities of Oracle Aconex natively within the MVL ERP. Serves as the central Common Data Environment (CDE) connecting ALL modules, ALL project participants, and ALL organizations. Every document, drawing, correspondence, and decision is captured in an unalterable audit trail. This module is the backbone of information flow across all 36 ERP modules — every module communicates through this centralized document platform.

Core Philosophy: Unique data ownership model — each organization controls their workspace data. Documents remain private until explicitly shared via transmittal. Strict version control ensures everyone works from the latest revision. Complete audit trail of every action and decision.

M365 SharePoint as primary document backend (Sites.ReadWrite.All). Purview for classification and sensitivity labels. OneDrive for personal docs. Power Automate for document workflows and transmittal automation. Outlook for mail/correspondence notifications (Mail.Send). Teams for document review collaboration channels (ChannelMessage.Send). Power BI for document analytics dashboards. Azure Blob Storage for archival tier.

12.1 Tab 1: Document Register & Lifecycle

Page: Enterprise Document Register (Aconex-Style)

  • Fields Document Number (auto-generated or manual), Revision (A/B/C/0/1/2), Title, Document Type (Drawing/Specification/Report/Procedure/Certificate/Correspondence/Submittal/RFI Response/O&M Manual/As-Built/Method Statement/ITP/Test Report/Datasheet/Schedule/Minutes/Contract/Variation/Claim/Photo/Model), Category, Discipline (Architectural/Structural/Mechanical/Electrical/Plumbing/Civil/Geotechnical/Landscape/Fire Protection/IT/General), Sub-Discipline, Status (Work in Progress/For Review/For Approval/For Construction/For Information/Approved/Approved as Noted/Superseded/Obsolete/Final/As-Built), Revision Date, Author, Organization, Originator, Project, Package, Confidential (Y/N), File Size, File Format, Pages, Scale, Classification Level (Public/Internal/CUI/Confidential/ITAR), Retention Date, Tags, Custom Fields 1-10
  • Buttons Upload Document Upload Multiple Bulk Upload via Spreadsheet New Revision Supersede Check Out Check In Download View Markup Compare Revisions Transmit Start Workflow Add to Package Set Status Edit Metadata View History View Audit Trail Print Export Register Advanced Search Save Search Share Link
  • Features:
  • Document Auto-Numbering Engine (Aconex-Style):
    • Configurable numbering schemes using document fields and project fields
    • Available fields: Organization Code, Project Code, Discipline Code, Category Code, Sequence Number, Select Lists 1-10, VDR Number
    • Configurable separators (hyphen, underscore, dot, slash, none)
    • Multiple schemes per project (different schemes for different document types)
    • Basic auto-numbering fallback: Type Code + Sequential Number (e.g., DWG-000001, RPT-000045)
    • Read-only Document Number field when auto-numbering is active
    • Skip pre-existing numbers when enabling on existing projects
  • Version Control & Revision Management:
    • Full revision history with all previous versions retained
    • Revision numbering: Alpha (A, B, C...) for preliminary, Numeric (0, 1, 2...) for issued
    • Supersede workflow: new revision auto-supersedes previous, notification sent to all holders
    • Check-out/check-in locking (prevents concurrent edits)
    • Revision comparison with visual diff (overlay, side-by-side, redline)
    • Metadata auto-populated from filename on upload
    • Bulk supersede with metadata spreadsheet
  • Document Status Workflow:
    • Configurable status lifecycle per document type
    • Status codes with color coding (green=approved, yellow=review, red=rejected, grey=superseded)
    • Status transition rules (e.g., "For Review" can only move to "Approved" or "Revise & Resubmit")
    • Industry-standard status codes: A (Approved), B (Approved with Comments), C (Revise & Resubmit), D (Rejected), E (For Information Only)
  • Data Ownership Model (Aconex-Style):
    • Each organization owns their workspace documents
    • Documents invisible to other organizations until explicitly transmitted
    • Organization-level document registers (filtered view of project register)
    • Cross-organization visibility controlled via transmittals
  • Search & Retrieval:
    • Full-text search across all document content (OCR for scanned documents)
    • Metadata-based filtering (type, discipline, status, date range, organization, author)
    • Saved searches with custom columns and sort order
    • Recent documents, favorites, and bookmarks
    • Advanced boolean search (AND/OR/NOT operators)
  • File Format Support: PDF, DWG, DXF, DWF, DWFX, IFC, RVT, NWD, E57, DOC/DOCX, XLS/XLSX, PPT/PPTX, TIF/TIFF, JPG/PNG/BMP/GIF, MP4, ZIP, MSG, EML, XML, JSON, CSV
  • Bulk Processing: Upload/supersede hundreds of documents via metadata spreadsheet template
  • Placeholder Documents (Aconex-Style):
    • Reserve document numbers before actual files are ready
    • Contain metadata (discipline, type, location) without an uploaded file
    • Can be transmitted to subcontractors who then upload actual files and transmit back
    • Tracked in register as "Placeholder" status until file attached
  • Online Viewer & Markup Engine (Aconex-Style):
    • Browser-based document viewing (no software installation required)
    • Supports 2D drawings, 3D models, PDF, Office, images, CAD
    • Pan, zoom, rotate navigation
    • Measurement tools: Distance, Perimeter, Area
    • 17 Markup Tools: Sticky Note, Callout, Text, Text Highlight, Text Underline, Text Squiggly, Text Strikeout, Square, Rectangle, Arrow, Cloud (revision cloud), Polygon, Freehand, Signature, Rubber Stamp, Image Stamp, Dynamic Stamp
    • Dynamic Stamps (3 levels): Level 1 (Name + Date), Level 2 (Name + Organization + Review Outcome), Level 3 (Name + Organization + Outcome + Logo + Disclaimer)
    • Markup style presets auto-saved per user
    • Bulk Annotate for batch markup operations
    • Flatten markups to permanently embed into document
    • Publish markups to share with other reviewers in same workflow step
    • Third-party markup compatibility (Adobe, Bluebeam XFDF format)
    • Side-by-side revision comparison (additions in green, deletions in red)
  • Aconex for Outlook Integration:
    • Create and send project correspondence directly from Outlook
    • Reply to and forward project mail from Outlook
    • Attach documents from EDMS Document Register or local drive
    • Register existing Outlook emails into EDMS correspondence record
    • Aconex Mail folder appears in Outlook sidebar with project sub-folders
    • Synchronized with EDMS project mail register
    • Confidential mail support (preserves confidentiality on reply/forward)
  • M365 SharePoint document libraries as backend storage; Purview sensitivity labels auto-applied; Version history via SharePoint versioning; OneDrive for personal workspace drafts; Outlook plugin for email-to-correspondence registration

Page: Document Access & Permissions

  • Fields Document/Folder, Access Level (No Access/View Only/Download/Edit/Approve/Full Control/Admin), Users/Groups/Roles/Organizations, Expiry Date, Confidential Flag, Classification Level, Inherit from Parent (Y/N)
  • Buttons Set Permissions Bulk Set Permissions Share via Link Revoke Access View Access Log Copy Permissions Inherit from Folder Break Inheritance
  • Features:
  • Role-based document access (RBAC) aligned with ERP roles
  • Organization-level access control (Aconex-style)
  • Document-level confidentiality override
  • Folder-level permission inheritance with break capability
  • Time-limited access (auto-expire for external parties)
  • Access audit log (who accessed what, when, from where)
  • Watermark enforcement for view-only users
  • Download restriction for sensitive documents
  • IP-based access restrictions for classified content

Page: Document Security & Classification

  • Fields Document, Classification Level (Public/Internal/CUI/Confidential/ITAR/Secret), Handling Instructions, Sensitivity Labels, Marking Requirements, Distribution Restrictions, Declassification Date
  • Buttons Classify Auto-Classify Apply Label Redact View Classification History Bulk Classify Generate Cover Sheet
  • Features:
  • Auto-watermarking: DRAFT, CUI, CONFIDENTIAL, ITAR, entity logo, user name, date
  • Dynamic watermarking (user-specific watermark on view/download/print)
  • CUI content scanning and auto-labeling (AI-powered)
  • ITAR/EAR export control document flagging
  • Redaction tool (permanent removal of sensitive content from PDF)
  • Classification inheritance (child documents inherit parent classification)
  • Security cover sheet generation (DD Form 254 reference)
  • AI AI Auto-Classifier reads documents and assigns type/metadata; AI CUI Content Scanner detects CUI indicators and auto-applies labels
  • M365 SharePoint/Purview sensitivity labels; Microsoft Information Protection (MIP); DLP policies; Azure RMS encryption

12.2 Tab 2: Transmittal Management (Aconex-Style)

Page: Create & Send Transmittal

  • Fields Transmittal Number (auto-generated TRN-NNNN), Project, From Organization, To Organization(s), Date, Subject, Reason for Issue (For Review/For Approval/For Construction/For Information/For Comment/For Record/As-Built/For Tender/Preliminary/Final/Superseded Issue), Priority (Urgent/Normal/Low), Response Required (Y/N), Response Due Date, Cover Letter/Notes, Distribution List, Documents (selected from register), Confidential (Y/N)
  • Buttons Create Transmittal Add Documents from Register Select Distribution List Preview Send Transmittal Save as Draft Use Template View Transmittal Print Cover Sheet Acknowledge Receipt Track Responses Export
  • Features:
  • Transmittal = Document + Distribution (Aconex-style): Transmitting a document automatically shares it to the recipient's document register with all metadata (revision, revision date, status, etc.)
  • Transmittal Templates: Pre-configured templates for common transmittal types (design review, construction issue, tender, closeout)
  • Distribution Lists: Pre-defined lists by role, discipline, or organization (e.g., "All Structural Engineers", "Design Team", "Client Representatives")
  • Reason for Issue Codes: Configurable per project — standard codes: For Review (FR), For Approval (FA), For Construction (FC), For Information (FI), For Comment (FCM), For Record (FRE), As-Built (AB), For Tender (FT)
  • Transmittal Register: Complete log of all transmittals sent/received with status tracking
  • Acknowledgment Tracking: Track who has acknowledged receipt (date/time stamped)
  • Response Tracking: Track review responses against due dates, overdue alerts
  • Unalterable Record: Once sent, transmittals cannot be edited, recalled, or deleted — permanent project record
  • Bulk Transmittal: Send multiple documents to multiple organizations in single transmittal
  • Auto-Numbering: Sequential transmittal numbering per project (TRN-001, TRN-002, etc.)
  • Cover Sheet PDF: Auto-generated transmittal cover sheet with document list, reason for issue, and signatures
  • Re-transmit: Create new transmittal referencing previous transmittal (for resubmission after review)
  • Auto-Transmit: Automatically transmit documents to pre-configured recipients when a document reaches a specific status (e.g., all drawings reaching "For Construction" status auto-transmit to the Site Team distribution list); configure triggers per document type, discipline, and status — no manual transmittal required
  • Workflow Transmittal (Return): Upon workflow completion, the system automatically generates a return transmittal from the workflow completer back to the originator containing the reviewed documents with final review outcomes, markups attached, and completion certificate — providing a complete documented record of the entire review cycle
  • Transmittal-to-Workflow Link: Automatically start a review workflow when transmittal is received
  • M365 Outlook notification to all recipients with transmittal summary; SharePoint document links in email body; Teams channel posting for project transmittals

Page: Transmittal Register & Tracking

  • Fields Transmittal Number, Date Sent, From, To, Subject, Document Count, Reason for Issue, Response Status (Pending/Acknowledged/Reviewed/Overdue), Response Due Date, Days Overdue, Acknowledged By, Acknowledged Date
  • Buttons Search Transmittals Filter by Status Filter by Organization Filter by Date Range Export to Excel Print Register View Overdue Send Reminder Bulk Acknowledge
  • Features:
  • Real-time transmittal status dashboard
  • Overdue transmittal alerts with automatic reminders
  • Transmittal analytics (volume by organization, response times, overdue trends)
  • Ball-in-court tracking (which organization holds the next action)
  • Transmittal chain tracking (original → review response → resubmission → final approval)

    • Restricted fields visible only to specific organizations/roles
    • Form templates per mail type with mandatory/optional field configuration
  • Mail Type Rules: Auto-set distribution, response requirements, and due dates per mail type
  • Mail Threading: Automatic threading of related correspondence (reply chains maintained as permanent record)
  • Ball-in-Court Tracking: Shows which organization/person holds the next action
  • Overdue Management: Automatic overdue flagging, reminder emails, escalation to managers
  • Unalterable Record: All mail is permanently retained — cannot be erased, deleted, or modified after sending
  • Confidential Mail: Restricted visibility — only sender, recipients, and CC can see
  • Document Register Attachment: Attach controlled documents from the register (maintains version link)
  • Response Tracking Dashboard: Open/responded/closed/overdue counts by mail type and organization
  • Correspondence Search: Full-text search across all project correspondence with advanced filters
  • Export: Export mail register to Excel/CSV/PDF with customizable columns
  • Cross-Module Links:

  • Site Instructions link to → Field Management (11.7), QMS (13.3)
  • Variations link to → Contract Lifecycle (27.3), Finance (5.12)
  • NCRs link to → QMS (13.3), Field Management (11.8)
  • Progress Claims link to → Finance (5.3), Project Management (7.5)
  • CDRLs link to → DoD Compliance (31.6)
  • Meeting Minutes link to → Project Management (7.1)
  • M365 Outlook email import (drag email into ERP to create correspondence record); Teams notification for new correspondence; Power Automate for overdue escalation; SharePoint for attachment storage

12.4 Tab 4: Review & Approval Workflows (Aconex Workflow Engine)

Page: Workflow Template Manager

  • Fields Workflow Template Name, Description, Document Types (applicable), Organization, Steps (ordered list), Step Type (Sequential/Parallel), Reviewers per Step (users/roles/organizations), Review Status Set (configurable labels), Completion Rule (All Must Review/Majority/Lead Reviewer Only/First Response), Rejection Action (Return to Originator/Return to Previous Step/Terminate), Due Date Calculation (fixed days/business days/calendar days), Escalation Rules, SLA Days, Active (Y/N)
  • Buttons Create Template Edit Template Clone Template Activate Deactivate Delete Test Workflow View Usage Export
  • Features:
  • Configurable Multi-Step Workflows (Aconex-Style):
    • Drag-and-drop workflow template designer
    • Sequential steps (one after another)
    • Parallel steps (simultaneous review by multiple parties)
    • Mixed sequential + parallel (e.g., Step 1: internal review parallel → Step 2: client approval sequential)
    • Unlimited steps per workflow
    • Unlimited reviewers per step
  • Review Status Labels (Configurable per Project):
    • Up to 6 review status labels per project, ordered by influence (least to greatest)
    • Standard labels: Approved (A), Approved with Comments (B), Revise & Resubmit (C), Rejected (D), For Information Only (E), Not Reviewed (F)
    • Custom labels supported (project-configurable)
    • Color-coded status indicators
  • Completion Rules:
    • "Final step outcome" — lead reviewer's final review determines outcome
    • "Lowest of all step outcomes" — worst outcome from any reviewer becomes the overall outcome
    • "Majority vote" — most common outcome wins
    • "First response" — first reviewer's response applies
  • Delegation & Subworkflows (Aconex-Style):
    • Delegate review to another person (full delegation transfer)
    • Start a subworkflow from within a step (get additional input before completing your review)
    • Subworkflow results roll up to parent workflow step
  • Escalation: Auto-escalate overdue reviews to manager/project director
  • SLA Management: Per-step SLA with automatic tracking and breach notification
  • Workflow Analytics: Average review time, overdue rate, rejection rate per reviewer/organization

Page: Active Workflow Dashboard

  • Fields Workflow Instance ID, Document(s), Template Used, Initiated By, Initiated Date, Current Step, Current Reviewer(s), Status (In Progress/Completed/Terminated/Overdue), Due Date, Days Remaining/Overdue, Final Outcome
  • Buttons View Workflow View Document Remind Reviewer Reassign Delegate Terminate Skip Step Add Comment View History Export Active Workflows Filter by Status/Organization/Template
  • Features:
  • Real-time workflow progress visualization (step-by-step progress bar)
  • Overdue workflow highlighting with automatic reminder capability
  • Bulk workflow actions (remind all overdue, reassign, terminate)
  • My Reviews queue (documents assigned to current user for review)
  • Review history (all past reviews with comments and markups)

Page: Document Review Interface

  • Fields Document being reviewed, Workflow step, Review Status (select from configured labels), Review Comments, Markup/Annotations, Conditions of Approval, Reviewer Name, Review Date
  • Buttons Approve (A) Approve with Comments (B) Revise & Resubmit (C) Reject (D) For Info Only (E) Save Draft Review Submit Review Delegate Start Subworkflow Add Markup View Previous Reviews Download for Offline Review Compare to Previous Revision
  • Features:
  • In-browser document viewer with markup tools (highlight, text note, arrow, rectangle, circle, strikethrough, cloud, stamp)
  • Review stamp application: APPROVED / APPROVED AS NOTED / REVISE & RESUBMIT / REJECTED / REVIEWED / FOR INFORMATION
  • Side-by-side revision comparison during review
  • Review comment threading (per-page comments)
  • Offline review: download, review offline, upload marked-up version
  • Review consolidation: all reviewer comments merged into single document
  • Automatic notification to originator when review complete

  • Buttons Create Supplier Package Activate Package Request Documents View Submissions Review Submission Approve Reject Request Resubmission Close Package Export to Excel View History
  • Features:
  • Supplier Document Request Workflow (Aconex-Style):
    1. Create Package — define required documents and metadata
    2. Activate Package — send formal request to supplier (once activated, cannot be deactivated)
    3. Request Documents — formal document request sent to supplier organization
    4. Supplier Submission — supplier uploads documents and submits for review
    5. Review Cycle — receiving organization reviews (approve/reject with comments)
    6. Resubmission — if rejected, supplier resubmits revised documents
    7. Completion — package marked complete when all documents approved
  • Submission status monitoring with milestone and due date tracking
  • Submission history per document (all previous submissions retained)
  • Percentage completion tracking per supplier package
  • Configurable review statuses (separate from workflow review labels)
  • Auto-complete when all required documents reach approved status
  • Supplier document register (filtered view showing supplier-submitted documents)
  • Cross-Module Links:
  • Supplier Packages link to → Procurement (8.5 Goods Receipt & Inspection) for vendor documentation requirements
  • Supplier reviews link to → QMS (13.5 Supplier Quality) for supplier quality tracking

12.11 Tab 11: Audit Trail & Compliance

    • Cryptographic hash verification for audit integrity

  • Legal Discovery: Search and export audit trail for legal proceedings, disputes, and claims support
  • Retention Compliance: Track document retention policy adherence, alert on approaching retention dates
  • Print/Download Tracking: Log every print and download for information security compliance

12.12 Tab 12: Document Retention & Archival

Page: Retention Policy Manager

  • Fields Policy Name, Document Type(s), Retention Period (years/months), Trigger Event (Project Closeout/Contract End/Document Approval/Custom Date), Action at Expiry (Archive/Review/Destroy), Legal Hold Override, Regulation Reference (FAR, DFARS, State Law, Custom), Active (Y/N)
  • Buttons Create Policy Edit Apply to Documents Bulk Apply View Affected Documents Generate Retention Schedule Place Legal Hold Release Legal Hold Run Expiry Check Export
  • Features:
  • Configurable retention policies per document type and project type
  • Automatic retention schedule enforcement (countdown from trigger event)
  • Legal hold capability (suspend all retention actions during litigation)
  • Secure disposal per NIST SP 800-88 guidelines (overwrite, degauss, destroy)
  • Government contract retention: FAR 4.703 (3-year minimum), DFARS (6-year for CUI), project-specific requirements
  • Archive tiers: Online (hot — instant access), Archive (cool — minutes), Deep Archive (cold — hours)
  • Retention dashboard: documents approaching expiry, documents under legal hold, destruction queue
  • Destruction certificate generation (proof of secure disposal)
  • M365 SharePoint retention labels and policies; Azure Blob archival storage tier (hot/cool/archive); Purview records management; eDiscovery for legal hold

Page: Project Archive (Read-Only Completed Project)

  • Fields Project Name, Archive Status (Active/Pending Archive/Archived), Archive Request Date, Requested By, Total Documents, Total Mail Items, Total Transmittals, Total Workflows, Total Packages, Archive Region/Data Center, Legal Hold Status, Archive Size (GB)
  • Buttons Request Archive View Archived Project Search Archive Download Archive Index Generate Archive Report Place Legal Hold Release Legal Hold Request Destruction Export Document List
  • Features:
  • Complete Read-Only Archive: Upon project completion, all project data frozen into a permanent read-only archive accessible to all original participants
  • Archive Contents: Full Document Register (all versions/revisions), complete Mail/Correspondence history (all threads and attachments), all Workflow records and outcomes with markups, complete Transmittal register and acknowledgment histories, all Package contents and review outcomes, Audit Trail/event logs, Project Directory/user data snapshot, project configuration settings
  • Archive Search & Retrieval: Full search capability within archived data — search by document number, title, type, discipline, date range, organization, mail type, correspondence subject; same filtering capabilities as active project
  • Legal Hold on Archive: Place or release legal hold on archived projects — suspends any destruction or modification actions for litigation support
  • Data Retention Compliance: Archived data retained per regional legal requirements (FAR 4.703 minimum 3 years, DFARS CUI 6 years, project-specific requirements enforced)
  • Archive Access for Original Participants: All organizations that participated in the project retain read-only access for the duration of the retention period without needing active licenses
  • Destruction Authorization: Secure destruction of archive upon retention period expiry requires dual authorization; generates legally admissible destruction certificate per NIST SP 800-88
  • Archive Index Report: Complete report of total data size, document count, mail count, and archive contents for legal and records management purposes
  • M365 Azure Blob Cold Storage tier for archive; Purview Compliance Manager for retention tracking; eDiscovery for legal discovery across archived projects

  • Fields Smart Manual Name, Project, Asset Number/Tag, Description, Level/Area/Zone/Room, Manufacturer, Model, Discipline, Document Category (Specification/Technical Data Sheet/Maintenance Procedure/Commissioning Report/Warranty Certificate/O&M Manual/Drawing/Operational Procedure), "Required for Handover" Flag (Y/N), Asset Reference, Completion Status
  • Buttons Create Smart Manual Import Asset Register (Excel) Add Asset Generate TOC Preview Manual Validate Completeness View Gap Report Package for Handover Transmit to Owner Export Smart Manual PDF View Placeholder Documents
  • Features:
  • Smart Manual Concept: Compile complete, structured, graphically navigable O&M manuals directly from the EDMS Document Register — assembled up to 80% faster than manual compilation; software installed on recipient's computer for offline access
  • Click-Through Navigation: Graphical navigation structure determined by project configuration (Buildings → Levels → Systems → Equipment → Documents); users click through a logical equipment hierarchy to reach relevant documentation
  • Asset Register Integration (linked to §23 EAM):
    • Import supplier-provided Asset Registers in standardized Excel format (Asset Number in Column A must not be blank)

    • Consolidate all supplier asset data into master project asset register
