  • Placeholder Strategy for Handover Docs: Reserve document numbers before actual files are ready — transmit placeholder numbers to subcontractors; subcontractors upload files and transmit back to complete the record; tracked in register as "Placeholder" until file attached
  • Handover Completeness Validator: Automatically checks all assets have required document types attached; generates gap report identifying missing document categories per asset and per discipline
  • File Format Compliance Enforcement: System flags non-compliant uploads (requires text-based searchable PDF, not scanned/rasterized; DWG requires TrueType fonts, 1.000 width factor, no multi-page drawings)
  • Auto-Generated Table of Contents: O&M manual TOC auto-generated from discipline/system/equipment hierarchy with live hyperlinks
  • Supplier Guide Distribution: Automatically distribute supplier guidance documents (naming conventions, metadata requirements, quality standards, submission deadlines) through EDMS transmittals
  • Dual Acceptance Acknowledgment: Digital owner acceptance signature confirms handover completeness — integrated with §21 E-Signature module
  • Up to 50% Pre-Assembly: O&M manuals can be started up to 50% complete before construction ends using available equipment specifications and design data
  • Cross-Module Links:
  • Asset data links to → EAM (23.1 Enterprise Asset Register) — exported handover asset register becomes the live operating asset register
  • Warranty records link to → EAM (23.2 Asset Lifecycle Management) for warranty tracking and expiry alerts
  • O&M Manuals link to → Facilities (30.5 Space & Equipment Records) for ongoing maintenance reference

  • Handover signatures link to → E-Signature (21.1)

  • Cross-Module Links:

  • Closeout links to → Field Management (11.6 Punch List & Closeout)
  • Handover links to → EAM (23.1 Asset Register) for asset commissioning records
  • O&M Manuals link to → Facilities Management (30.5)
  • Certificates link to → Digital Signatures (21.1)
  • Government property link to → DoD Compliance (31.1 Government Property Management)

12.15 Cross-Module Document Communication Hub

Every module in the MVL ERP communicates through the EDMS. The following matrix defines how each module interacts with the document management system, ensuring seamless information flow, version control, and audit trail across the entire platform.

# Module Documents Generated/Managed How It Links to EDMS (Section 12)
1 Finance & Accounting (5) Invoices, payment vouchers, journal entries, financial reports, tax returns, ICS schedules, SF1034/SF1035, audit workpapers Auto-filed to Document Register; transmittals for external audit document requests; retention per FAR 4.703
2 Human Resources (6) Employment contracts, offer letters, performance reviews, training certificates, policy documents, I-9 forms, clearance documents HR documents in restricted folder; confidential classification auto-applied; retention per labor law requirements
3 Project Management (7) Project charters, schedules, progress reports, EVM reports (IPMR/IPMDAR), meeting minutes, risk registers, baseline documents Project-scoped document register; transmittals for client progress reports; workflows for report approval
4 Procurement (8) Purchase orders, RFQs, vendor evaluations, goods receipts, subcontract agreements, sole-source justifications PO documents transmittable to vendors; vendor correspondence via Mail module; package management for procurement sets
5 Proposal/Bid Management (9) Proposals, compliance matrices, past performances, teaming agreements, bid bond documentation Tender packages for bid document distribution; confidential proposals in restricted access; version-controlled proposal drafts
6 Estimation & Costing (10) Estimates, takeoff reports, BOQ documents, rate analyses, tender submissions, cash flow projections Estimation documents version-controlled; drawing sets linked for takeoff source tracking; tender transmittals
7 Field Management (11) Daily logs, RFIs, submittals, punch lists, T&M tickets, field photos, inspection reports, site instructions RFIs/submittals managed via Correspondence module; drawings via Drawing Register; field photos auto-uploaded to register
8 QMS (13) Quality plans, ITPs, inspection reports, NCRs, CAPA reports, audit reports, calibration certificates, test reports Quality documents under controlled document numbering; workflows for quality document approval; transmittals for client quality submittals
9 HSE (14) Safety plans, JHA/AHAs, toolbox talks, incident reports, OSHA logs, permits to work, environmental monitoring reports HSE documents in compliance folder; incident reports auto-distributed; permit documents with expiry tracking
10 ITSM (15) Change requests, release notes, KB articles, service reports, SLA reports, audit logs IT documents auto-filed; change management documents workflow-approved; KB articles version-controlled
11 EAM (23) Asset registers, maintenance records, condition reports, warranty documents, disposal certificates Asset documents linked to asset records; warranty documents with expiry alerts; GFP documents per FAR 52.245-1
12 CRM (24) Client profiles, communication logs, proposals, satisfaction surveys, teaming agreements Client-facing documents transmittable; confidential CRM documents restricted; past performance packages
13 CLM (27) Contracts, amendments, change orders, obligation checklists, correspondence, completion certificates Contract documents version-controlled; amendment workflow-approved; correspondence via Mail module
14 Compliance & Risk (28) Risk registers, compliance reports, audit findings, policy documents, corrective action plans Compliance documents retention-managed; audit reports distributed via transmittal; policy documents workflow-approved
15 DoD Compliance (31) CDRLs, CDRL deliverables, DD Forms, security plans, SCRM assessments, counterfeit prevention logs CDRL packages managed in Packages module; classified documents per NISPOM handling; government property records per FAR

12.16 Tab 16: Document Processes Module (Review Matrix)

Source parity: Aconex "Document Processes" module — a structured alternative to ad-hoc workflows that uses a configurable review matrix to determine automatically which organizations/disciplines must review each document, eliminating manual reviewer assignment.

Page: Review Matrix Configuration

  • Fields Rule Name, Document Type(s), Discipline(s), Document Status Trigger, Reviewer Organization(s), Reviewer Role(s), Review Sequence (Serial/Parallel), Required/Optional, Response Due (days), Completion Rule (All Must Review/Minimum Quorum/First Response), Active (Y/N)
  • Buttons Create Rule Edit Rule Clone Rule Activate Deactivate Test Rule View Rule Usage Export Matrix Import Matrix
  • Features:
  • Review Matrix (Aconex Document Processes-Style): Define rules that automatically determine reviewers for a document based on its attributes (type, discipline, status) — no manual reviewer selection needed at time of review initiation
  • Rule-Based Auto-Assignment: When a document matches rule criteria, the system automatically assigns the correct organizations and roles to review without any manual configuration at runtime
  • Parallel vs. Serial Review: Configure whether all assigned reviewers review simultaneously or in a controlled sequence
  • Completion Rules: Define when the review process is considered complete (e.g., all required reviewers must respond; optional reviewers may skip)
  • Comment/Issue Register: All reviewer comments and issues raised during a Document Process are captured in a unified comment register (separate from general workflow comments) — tracked to resolution
  • Key Difference from Workflows: Workflows require manually selecting reviewers at the time of initiation; Document Processes auto-assign based on pre-configured matrix rules — ideal for high-volume document types with consistent review routing
  • Re-review Triggers: If a document is revised and re-submitted, the same matrix rules automatically re-assign the same reviewer set for the new revision
  • Active Processes Dashboard: Real-time view of all in-progress document reviews with status per reviewer, overdue indicators, comment counts, and % completion
  • Review Outcome Escalation: If a required reviewer does not respond within the SLA, auto-escalate to their manager
  • Integration with Transmittals: Receiving a transmittal can auto-trigger a Document Process if the document type matches a configured rule

Page: Active Document Processes Dashboard

  • Fields Process ID, Document(s), Rule Applied, Initiated Date, Reviewers Assigned, Responses Received, Outstanding Reviewers, Open Comments/Issues, Status (Active/Completed/Overdue/Cancelled), Due Date, Days Remaining/Overdue, Final Outcome
  • Buttons View Process Remind Overdue Reviewers Add Reviewer Close Process View Comment Register Export Filter by Rule/Status/Organization
  • Features:
  • Comment/Issue register per process — all raised issues tracked to resolution status
  • Bulk reminder capability for all overdue processes
  • Drill-down from process to individual reviewer responses and markups
  • Review cycle time analytics (average days per process type, per reviewer organization)

12.17 Tab 17: Inspection & Test Plans (ITP) — EDMS Document Role

Authoritative module for ITP process: §13.2 QMS — Inspection & Testing (Field Quality Control) contains the full ITP workflow specification including Hold Points, Witness Points, Review Points, activity sequencing, templates, mobile access, and audit-ready export.

EDMS role in ITP: This tab covers only the document management aspects of ITPs within the EDMS. The ITP process itself (creation, Hold Point enforcement, evidence workflows, event log, government sign-off) is fully specified in §13.2.

EDMS Services Supporting ITPs

  • Evidence Document Filing: All ITP evidence documents (test reports, inspection photos, certificates, measurement records) are filed directly into the EDMS Document Register §12.1 under document type "ITP Evidence" with linking to the originating ITP record in §13.2. Evidence is stored as controlled EDMS documents — version-controlled, accessible via transmittal, and included in closeout packages.
  • ITP PDF Archive: Completed ITP packages are exported as structured PDFs from §13.2 and filed into the EDMS Document Register as official project records — subject to the configured retention schedule §12.12 and included in project archive and handover packages §12.14.
  • Transmittal Distribution: Completed ITPs requiring distribution to Owner, Engineer, or Government Inspector are transmitted via the EDMS Transmittal Module §12.2 with full acknowledgment tracking and unalterable audit trail.
  • ITP Packages for Closeout: ITP records are included in closeout/handover document packages assembled in §12.14 — the EDMS Package function §12.6 groups all ITP PDFs, evidence documents, and test certificates for turnover.

→ Full ITP specification (templates, Hold Points, Witness Points, activity workflow, mobile access, government records): §13.2 QMS Inspection & Testing

12.18 Tab 18: Mobile EDMS — Field Access

Authoritative module for mobile/offline field access: §11.9 Field Management — Mobile & Offline contains the full mobile platform specification (offline-first architecture, IndexedDB sync, PWA capabilities, barcode/QR scanning, voice-to-text, conflict resolution, OneDrive offline sync).

EDMS role: The EDMS is fully accessible through the Field Management mobile platform §11.9. This tab describes the EDMS-specific mobile capabilities that extend the base field mobile platform.

EDMS-Specific Mobile Capabilities (extending §11.9 Field Mobile Platform)

  • EDMS Document Register — Mobile View: Browse and search the full EDMS Document Register from a mobile device; view, download, and annotate documents from the register; upload field-captured photos directly into the Document Register as official EDMS records with auto-assigned metadata (project, GPS, timestamp, uploader).
  • Offline Document & Drawing Access: Download specific document sets or drawing packages to device for offline field access; latest-revision drawings are automatically cached when project is synced; cached documents sync back to EDMS register on reconnect.
  • QR Code Document Lookup: QR codes generated by the EDMS (from §12.1 Document Register) can be printed and attached to physical equipment, locations, or submittals — field staff scan QR code to instantly navigate to that document record in EDMS, including revision history and linked correspondences.
  • Camera-to-Register Upload: Camera captures from the field (inspection photos, site conditions, deliveries, issues) are uploaded directly into the EDMS Document Register as classified documents, not as standalone attachments — maintaining the single-source document control principle.
  • Mail/Correspondence on Mobile: Full EDMS Correspondence & Mail module §12.3 accessible on mobile — create, reply, forward, and acknowledge mail; push notifications for new mail, overdue items, and Ball-in-Court assignments.
  • Transmittal Acknowledgment: Acknowledge received transmittals from mobile; field teams can confirm receipt via mobile without returning to office.

→ Full mobile platform specification (offline architecture, sync, PWA, GPS, barcode scanning, push notifications, supported platforms): §11.9 Field Management — Mobile & Offline

  • M365 Azure AD SSO on mobile (no separate credentials); SharePoint document sync backend; Teams notifications trigger mobile push alerts.

§13. Module 9: Quality Management System (QMS) — Enterprise Quality Platform (Procore Quality + ISO 9001 + AS9100)

Purpose: Comprehensive enterprise quality management platform integrating Procore's construction quality workflows with ISO 9001:2015, AS9100D (aerospace/defense), and ISO 14001 quality standards. Manages inspection & test plans (ITP), non-conformance reports, corrective/preventive actions (CAPA), quality audits, material testing, supplier quality, calibration, and document control. Built for a DoD Prime Contractor self-performing construction globally with requirements for USACE 3-phase inspection (Preparatory/Initial/Follow-up), government source inspection, and First Article Testing.

M365 SharePoint for quality documents (ITPs, specs, test reports, certificates). Teams for quality review meetings, NCR war rooms, and audit collaboration channels. Power BI for quality KPI dashboards (COPQ, defect rates, audit findings). Power Apps for mobile inspection forms (offline capable). Outlook for NCR notifications, audit reminders, and quality alert distribution. Planner for CAPA task tracking.

13.1 Tab 1: Quality Policy, Planning & Standards

Page: Quality Management System (QMS) Framework

  • Fields QMS Policy Name, Version, Effective Date, Scope, Quality Objectives, Management Representative, Review Frequency, Certification Body, Certificate Number, Expiry Date
  • Buttons Create Policy Review Approve Publish Archive Generate Policy Document Map to Standard
  • Features:
  • Quality Management System governance aligned to ISO 9001:2015 clause structure
  • AS9100D aerospace/defense quality requirements (additional clauses 8.1.1 Operational Risk, 8.1.2 Configuration Management, 8.1.3 Product Safety, 8.1.4 Counterfeit Parts Prevention)
  • ISO 14001:2015 Environmental Quality System integration
  • Quality objectives with measurable KPIs linked to organizational goals
  • Management Review scheduling and agenda generation (clause 9.3)
  • Process-based approach with SIPOC diagrams (Supplier-Input-Process-Output-Customer)
  • Context of the Organization documentation (clause 4.1/4.2 — internal/external issues, interested parties)
  • Risk-based thinking integration (clause 6.1 — risks and opportunities register)
  • Quality manual auto-generation from configured QMS settings

Page: Quality Plans & Inspection Test Plans (ITP)

  • Fields Plan ID, Project, Contract Reference, Specification, Discipline (Civil/Structural/MEP/Electrical), Activity, Inspection Type (Hold Point/Witness Point/Review/Monitor), Acceptance Criteria, Inspection Agency (Self/Third Party/Government), Test Method, Frequency, Responsible Party, Status
  • Buttons Create ITP Import Template Copy from Previous Assign Inspector Submit for Approval Revise Lock Export to PDF
  • Features:
  • USACE 3-Phase Inspection System:
    • Preparatory Phase: Pre-activity meeting, material/equipment verification, work procedure review, hazard analysis
    • Initial Phase: First production inspection, check conformance to plans/specs, document results
    • Follow-up Phase: Ongoing inspections, daily/periodic checks, document compliance
  • Hold Point / Witness Point / Review Point management with mandatory sign-off gates
  • Government inspection coordination (DCMA Quality Assurance Representative notifications)
  • Linked to project WBS — each WBS activity can have associated quality inspection requirements
  • ITP template library organized by discipline and construction type
  • Automatic notification to inspectors when activity is ready for inspection (linked to scheduling)
  • AI
  • AI ITP Generator — Analyzes contract specifications and automatically generates draft Inspection & Test Plans with appropriate hold/witness/review points based on specification requirements and project risk profile
  • AI Spec Analyzer — Reads contract specifications (PDF upload) and extracts all quality/testing requirements, acceptance criteria, and compliance obligations into structured checklist format

  • AI Recurrence Predictor — Identifies patterns across NCRs and predicts which types of non-conformances are likely to recur, recommending targeted preventive actions

§14. Module 10: Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) — Expanded (Procore Safety + OSHA + EM385-1-1)

Purpose: Comprehensive HSE management platform incorporating Procore's full safety capabilities — incident management with OSHA recordkeeping, observations, inspections, toolbox talks, safety orientations, JHAs, permits to work, and environmental compliance. Mandatory for all U.S. contractors (OSHA 29 CFR 1926, USACE EM385-1-1). Supports ISO 45001 and ISO 14001 frameworks.

M365 Power Apps for mobile safety inspection forms (offline capable). Teams for safety channels and incident alert war rooms. SharePoint for safety documents (AHAs, JHAs, SOPs, SDSs). Power BI for HSE metrics (TRIR, DART, EMR dashboards). Outlook for safety alerts and toolbox talk distribution.

Key Personas: HSE Director, Site Safety Officers, Safety Managers, Project Managers, Superintendents, Workers (self-reporting)

§15. Module 11: IT Service Management (ITSM) — Expanded

Purpose: Comprehensive ITIL-aligned IT Service Management: incident management, problem management, change management, request fulfillment, service catalog, SLA management, knowledge management, CMDB, capacity management, availability management, release management, service level reporting, and continuous improvement. This module is the operational backbone for all IT operations across every MVL location globally.

M365 Teams for real-time incident alerts and war rooms. Outlook for ticket notifications with actionable Approve/Reject/Acknowledge buttons via Graph API. Power BI for SLA dashboards, trend analytics, and executive reports. Power Apps for self-service portal and mobile ticket creation. SharePoint for knowledge base articles and runbook storage. Power Automate for escalation workflows, SLA breach alerts, and auto-routing. Microsoft Copilot for natural language ticket creation and KB search.

Key Personas: IT Service Manager, Help Desk Agents (L1/L2/L3), Infrastructure Engineers, Application Support, Security Operations, End Users (self-service), CIO/IT Director

Tech Azure App Service, Azure Functions for automation, Azure Logic Apps for workflow orchestration, Azure SQL for ticket store, Azure Cognitive Search for KB, Azure OpenAI for ticket classification and resolution suggestion, SignalR for real-time updates, Azure Service Bus for event-driven architecture

15.1 Tab 1: Service Desk & Incident Management

Page: Ticketing System Configuration

  • Fields Ticket Types (Incident/Request/Problem/Change/Task), Priority Levels (P1-Critical/P2-High/P3-Medium/P4-Low), SLA Definitions per priority, Routing Rules, Escalation Paths, Categories & Sub-Categories, Working Hours per location, Holiday Calendars per entity, Business Hours SLA vs 24x7 SLA
  • Buttons Configure Add Category Set SLA Define Routing Set Business Hours Configure Escalation Matrix Test Rules Import Categories Export Configuration
  • Agentic AI Automation:
  • AI auto-suggests optimal category tree structure based on historical ticket data
  • AI recommends SLA targets based on industry benchmarks and past performance
  • AI validates routing rules for coverage gaps (no team assigned for certain categories)

  • Fields Ticket ID (auto-generated with prefix INC-), Category, Sub-Category, Priority (P1-P4), Urgency, Impact, Summary, Description (rich text with screenshots), Reporter (auto-populated from AD), Reporter's Location, Reporter's Department, Assigned Group, Assigned To, Status (New/Acknowledged/In Progress/Pending User/Pending Vendor/Resolved/Closed), SLA Clock (response SLA + resolution SLA), Resolution Notes, Root Cause Category, Closure Code, Satisfaction Rating (1-5), Related CIs (from CMDB), Related Incidents, Parent Incident (for major incidents), Affected Users Count, Attachments, Communication Log
  • Buttons Create Ticket Quick Create via Template Assign Reassign Escalate to L2 Escalate to L3 Update Add Work Note Add Customer Note Link to CI Link to Problem Resolve Close Reopen Merge Duplicate Clone Convert to Problem Convert to Change Email User Call User View SLA Timer Print Ticket

  • Color-coded SLA indicators (Green = on track, Amber = approaching breach, Red = breached)
  • Ticket Escalation & Priority management (automatic and manual)
  • Alert-to-ticket engine with severity-to-priority mapping (from monitoring/SIEM)
  • On-call technician auto-assignment from rotation schedule
  • Major Incident Management — auto-create war room in Teams, bridge call, executive notifications
  • Child ticket creation for tasks under major incidents
  • Affected user tracking with mass communication capability
  • Auto-routing based on category + location + shift
  • Collision detection (warn if another agent is viewing same ticket)
  • Time tracking per work note (auto and manual)
  • AI
  • AI Ticket Classifier — Automatically classifies incoming tickets by category, sub-category, priority, and urgency using NLP analysis of the ticket description
  • AI Resolution Suggester — Searches knowledge base and historical resolved tickets to suggest resolution steps to the agent in real-time
  • AI Auto-Resolver — For known, repetitive issues (password reset, access request, printer issue), AI fully resolves the ticket without human intervention and notifies the user
  • AI Sentiment Analyzer — Analyzes user communication tone; flags frustrated users for priority handling and manager notification
  • AI Duplicate Detector — Scans new tickets against open tickets; auto-merges duplicates or links related incidents
  • AI Summary Generator — Generates a one-paragraph summary of all work notes and communications for handoff between shifts
  • AI Escalation Predictor — Predicts which tickets are likely to breach SLA or require escalation, alerting supervisors proactively
  • AI Response Drafter — Drafts customer-facing email responses based on resolution notes, using professional tone and including relevant KB links
  • M365
  • Actionable email notifications with Approve/Reject/Acknowledge buttons via Graph API
  • Teams notification to assigned group channel on new P1/P2 tickets
  • Auto-create Teams war room for Major Incidents
  • Outlook calendar integration for on-call schedules
  • Copilot integration: users can create tickets by chatting in Teams ("Hey Copilot, my VPN is not working")

  • AI Approval Optimizer — Learns approval patterns; auto-approves low-risk standard requests (e.g., software install for approved list items)
  • AI Catalog Recommender — Suggests relevant catalog items based on user role, department, and what peers have requested

  • License reclamation (identify unused licenses and reclaim them)
  • Software usage analytics (frequency, last used date)
  • Vendor license portal integration
  • True-up and compliance reporting
  • AI
  • AI License Optimizer — Analyzes actual usage patterns and recommends license right-sizing (downgrade, cancel unused, switch to cheaper tier)
  • AI Spend Forecaster — Predicts future license costs based on headcount growth, project pipeline, and historical consumption
  • AI Compliance Risk Scorer — Identifies software audit risk areas and prepares audit-ready documentation

  • Buttons Add CI Edit Map Dependencies View Impact Analysis Run Discovery View Dependency Map View History Decommission Link to Asset Link to Service Export Bulk Import
  • Features:
  • Configuration Item Management with auto-discovery

  • Dependency mapping with visual graph view
  • Impact analysis (what breaks if this CI goes down?)
  • CMDB health scoring (coverage %, accuracy %, freshness %)
  • Service mapping (CIs → Services → Business Processes)

15.10 Tab 10: Alert Management & On-Call (Freshservice-Style)

Page: Alert Management Console

  • Fields Alert ID, Source (Monitoring Tool/SIEM/Cloud/Application/Network/Custom), Severity (Critical/Warning/Info/OK), Alert Title, Description, Affected CI, Metric/Threshold, Current Value, Triggered At, Acknowledged By, Status (Triggered/Acknowledged/Suppressed/Resolved/Auto-Closed), Linked Incident, Correlation Group
  • Buttons View Alerts Acknowledge Suppress Create Incident Link to CI View History Configure Rules Set Suppression Window Filter by Source Filter by Severity Bulk Acknowledge Export
  • Features:
  • Alert-to-Incident Engine:
    • Automatic incident creation from critical alerts
    • Severity-to-priority mapping (Critical Alert → P1 Incident, Warning → P3, etc.)
    • Alert deduplication (same alert within window = single incident)
    • Alert correlation (group related alerts into single major incident)
  • Alert Rules:
    • Configurable alert rules per monitoring source
    • Threshold-based alerts (CPU > 90%, Disk > 85%, Memory > 95%)
    • Pattern-based alerts (X failures in Y minutes)
    • Anomaly-based alerts (deviation from baseline)
    • Maintenance window suppression (suppress during planned changes)
  • Alert Routing:
    • Route to on-call technician based on CI category and time of day
    • Escalation chain if not acknowledged within threshold
    • Multi-channel notification (Teams, Email, SMS, Phone)
  • Alert dashboard with real-time status
  • Alert history and trend analysis
  • Integration with Infrastructure Monitoring module
  • Integration with SIEM module for security alerts
  • AI AI Alert Correlator — Automatically groups related alerts from different sources into a single incident; identifies root cause alert vs symptom alerts

  • Buttons Create Schedule Edit Rotation Add Member Remove Member Swap Shifts Add Override Set Escalation View Calendar Export Schedule Send Schedule to Team
  • Features:
  • On-call rotation management (automatic rotation)
  • Primary and secondary on-call designation
  • Shift swaps and temporary overrides
  • Holiday and PTO coverage management
  • Escalation chain (Primary → Secondary → Manager) with configurable timeout
  • On-call calendar view (who is on-call when)
  • On-call notifications (remind technician of upcoming shift)

  • On-call compensation tracking (link to HR/Payroll for on-call premium pay)
  • M365 Outlook calendar sync for on-call schedules; Teams notification for on-call alerts

    • Action nodes: Update fields, send notifications, create records, API calls, scripts

    • Approval nodes (single/multi-level)

  • Orchestration:
    • Cross-module workflow execution (ITSM → HR → Procurement)
    • External system webhooks and API integration
    • Script execution (PowerShell, Python) for complex automations
    • Event-driven architecture (Azure Service Bus triggers)
  • Workflow analytics (execution count, success rate, average duration)
  • Workflow version control
  • Workflow testing/sandbox mode
  • AI AI Workflow Recommender — Analyzes repetitive manual agent actions and suggests new automation workflows to create

Tech Azure Sentinel (GCC High), Log Analytics workspace, KQL queries, Azure Logic Apps for auto-response

  • Buttons Configure Source Enable/Disable Set Retention Test View Sample
  • Features:
  • Real-time audit log streaming (CEF format) from all ERP modules
  • Audit Logging (90+ days retention)
  • Immutable audit storage (cannot be modified post-streaming)
  • Log Analytics Workspace

Page: Correlation Rules

  • Features:
  • Correlation rules for threat detection across modules
  • Behavioral baseline per user/role for anomaly detection
  • User activity analysis (bulk downloads, after-hours access)
  • Privilege escalation monitoring
  • Suspicious login detection with auto-MFA re-authentication
  • Data exfiltration attempt detection

  • Buttons View Alert Investigate Contain Escalate Close False Positive

  • Security alert ingestion (malware, suspicious process, policy violation)

  • Mandatory CISO notification for High/Critical severity
  • AI AI Behavior Baseline establishes per-user patterns and detects anomalies; AI Threat Responder auto-executes containment (lock account, force MFA), reducing mean-time-to-contain from hours to seconds

16.4 Module Compliance Specification (BG-5: IT & Security)

Compliance Header Specification
Business Group BG-5 — IT & Security
Data Classification Audit logs: CUI-SP-OPSEC; Alert records: CUI-SP; Configuration: Internal
Primary Roles CISO (full access), Security Analyst (read+investigate), ITSM Admin (alert create), IT Admin (config), Auditor (read-only)
SoD Requirement Alert investigation and alert closure must be different personnel
Approval Gates Critical/High alerts: CISO acknowledgment required within 4 hours; Auto-containment actions logged with CISO post-review within 24 hours
Key Audit Events Alert created, Alert investigated, Containment action taken, False positive marked, Log source added/removed, Retention period changed, Export of audit trail
Audit Immutability All CEF log streams are write-once; no Analyst or Admin role can modify; CISO can suppress (logged) but not delete
Retention Security audit logs: 7 years minimum; Breach-related events: 10 years — NIST AU-11, FAR 4.703
Required Reports CMMC Continuous Monitoring Report (monthly), POA&M Status (quarterly), Incident Response Summary (per incident), Annual Audit Log Review Certificate
NIST 800-171 Controls 3.3.1, 3.3.2 (audit log creation), 3.3.4 (alert on failure), 3.3.5 (audit reduction), 3.3.6 (log reduction), 3.13.1, 3.14.6, 3.14.7
CMMC Practices AU.L2-3.3.1, AU.L2-3.3.2, IR.L2-3.6.1, IR.L2-3.6.2, SI.L2-3.14.6, SI.L2-3.14.7
Export Controls Audit trail exports: CISO-only + dual approval; CEF streams: GCC High Sentinel only — never external SIEM
FedRAMP Boundary ✅ All event data processed and stored within GCC High; Azure Sentinel (GCC High) only

17.4 Module Compliance Specification (BG-5: IT & Security)

Compliance Header Specification
Business Group BG-5 — IT & Security
Data Classification Device compliance records: Internal; Vulnerability scan results: CUI-SP; Patch status: Internal
Primary Roles CISO (full access), IT Admin (device manage + patch), Security Analyst (vuln read), Help Desk (device view), Auditor (read-only)
SoD Requirement Vulnerability discovery and patch approval must be different personnel
Approval Gates Critical CVE (CVSS ≥9.0): emergency change ticket auto-created; CISA KEV items: 24-hour remediation SLA with CISO override required

CMMC Practices CM.L2-3.4.1, CM.L2-3.4.2, SI.L2-3.14.1, SI.L2-3.14.4, SI.L2-3.14.5, RA.L2-3.11.2, RA.L2-3.11.3
Export Controls Vulnerability scan results: IT Admin + CISO only; no export to unencrypted destinations
FedRAMP Boundary ✅ All MDM operations through Microsoft Intune GCC High; Defender for Endpoint GCC High

18.4 Module Compliance Specification (BG-5: IT & Security)

Compliance Header Specification
Business Group BG-5 — IT & Security
Data Classification Backup job logs: Internal; DR plans: Internal; COOP plans: CUI (if government operational data included)
Primary Roles IT Admin (full backup ops), CISO (DR plan approval), BC Manager (COOP), Auditor (read-only), Executives (BCP review)
SoD Requirement Backup configuration and backup verification must be different personnel
Approval Gates DR plan changes: CISO + VP approval; COOP plan activation: Executive + CISO; Restore from backup: IT Admin + CISO dual-authorization for production systems
Key Audit Events Backup job completed/failed, Restore initiated, DR test scheduled/executed/result, COOP plan updated, RPO/RTO threshold breached, Backup retention period changed
Audit Immutability Backup job logs immutable; restore events streamed to SIEM §16; retention change events require CISO acknowledgment
Retention Backup logs: 3 years; DR test results: 5 years; COOP plans: perpetual (version-controlled) — NIST CP-9, CP-10, FedRAMP CP
Required Reports Daily Backup Status Report (auto-email to IT Admin + CISO), Monthly RPO/RTO Compliance Report, Annual DR Test Certificate, NIST CP-9/CP-10 Evidence Package (annual)
NIST 800-171 Controls 3.6.1 (incident capability), 3.6.2 (incident tracking) (via backup failure incidents), 3.7.1 (maintenance controls); Primary: FedRAMP CP-9, CP-10
CMMC Practices RE.L2-3.6.1 (backup requirement mapped), IR.L2-3.6.1, IR.L2-3.6.2
Export Controls DR plans: Internal distribution only; COOP plans with government operational data: CUI handling
FedRAMP Boundary ✅ All backups to Azure Backup / Azure SQL backup (GCC High); Azure Site Recovery within GCC High

§21. Module 17: Enterprise E-Signature & Agreement Platform (Replaces DocuSign)

Purpose: Full DocuSign-equivalent e-signature and agreement platform built natively within the ERP. Provides envelope-based signing workflows with multi-party orchestration, advanced recipient roles, conditional fields, identity verification, bulk send, templates, PowerForms, remote notarization, payment collection, and complete audit trail. Legal validity across all MVL jurisdictions. No external DocuSign dependency.

M365 Outlook for signature request delivery and notifications (Mail.Send). SharePoint for signed document storage (Sites.ReadWrite.All). Teams for signature status updates and urgent signing alerts (ChannelMessage.Send). Power Automate for auto-trigger signing workflows from any module. OneDrive for personal signing queue.

Tech Web Crypto API, Azure Key Vault HSM, X.509 certificate management, RFC 3161 timestamping, PAdES/XAdES/CAdES signature standards, PDF.js for in-browser signing experience

21.1 Tab 1: Envelope Creation & Sending (DocuSign-Style)

Page: Create Signing Envelope

  • Fields Envelope Name, Documents (upload or select from EDMS), Recipients (ordered list), Signing Order Type (Sequential/Parallel/Mixed), Email Subject, Email Message, Expiration Date (days), Reminder Schedule (days after send, repeat interval), Brand/Template, Priority (Standard/Urgent), Access Code Protection (Y/N), Language
  • Buttons Add Document Add from EDMS Add from Template Add Recipient Set Signing Order Add Fields/Tabs Preview Send Save as Draft Save as Template Bulk Send Schedule Send Void Correct
  • Features:
  • Recipient Roles (DocuSign-Style):
    • Signer — Must sign the document (required fields: signature, initials, date)
    • Carbon Copy (CC) — Receives a copy when complete (no action required)
    • Needs to View — Must open and confirm viewing (acknowledgment tracked)
    • In-Person Signer — Signs on the sender's device (in-person ceremonies)
    • Editor — Can modify recipient list and fields before forwarding for signing
    • Agent — Signs on behalf of another person (delegation)
    • Intermediary — Receives, reviews, and routes to next signer
    • Certified Delivery — Must confirm receipt (tracked delivery)
    • Witness — Signs as witness after primary signer completes
    • Approver — Approves document without signing (approve/reject decision)
    • Notary — Remote Online Notarization (RON) role
  • Signing Order Configuration:
    • Sequential (signer 1 → signer 2 → signer 3)
    • Parallel (all signers simultaneously)
    • Mixed (group 1 parallel → group 2 sequential → group 3 parallel)
    • Routing order numbers (1, 2, 3, etc.) with same-number recipients signing in parallel
  • Envelope Lifecycle: Draft → Sent → Delivered → Signed → Completed → Archived
  • Envelope Correction: Modify recipients, fields, or documents after sending (before all sign)
  • Void & Resend: Void incomplete envelopes with reason; resend to recipients who haven't signed
  • Envelope Expiration: Configurable expiration with automatic void and notification
  • Reminders: Automatic reminders to pending signers on configurable schedule

Page: Field/Tab Placement Designer (DocuSign-Style)

  • Fields Document Page View, Recipient Assignment (per field), Field Properties (required/optional, read-only, conditional, validation, tooltip)
  • Buttons Add Signature Tab Add Initial Tab Add Date Signed Tab Add Text Tab Add Checkbox Tab Add Dropdown Tab Add Radio Button Tab Add Formula Tab Add Attachment Tab Add Payment Tab Add Approval Tab Add Decline Tab Add Note Tab Add Company Tab Add Title Tab Add Full Name Tab Add Email Tab Add Number Tab Auto-Place Delete Tab Copy Tab Set Conditional Logic Preview
  • Features:
  • Signing Fields/Tabs (Full DocuSign Parity):
    • Signature (draw, type, upload, or adopt signature)
    • Initials (draw, type, or adopt)
    • Date Signed (auto-populated)
    • Text (free-form text entry)
    • Checkbox (single or grouped)
    • Radio Button (mutually exclusive selection)
    • Dropdown/Select List (configurable options)
    • Number (numeric input with validation)
    • Formula/Calculated Field (references other fields, auto-calculate)
    • Attachment (recipient uploads supporting document)
    • Payment (collect payment during signing — credit card, bank transfer)
    • Approve/Decline (binary decision without signature)
    • Note (add note visible only to sender)
    • Company Name (auto-populated from profile)
    • Title (auto-populated from profile)
    • Full Name (auto-populated from profile)
    • Email Address (auto-populated from profile)
    • SSN/Tax ID (masked input)
    • Stamp/Seal (for notarized documents)
  • Conditional Logic (DocuSign Smart Sections):
    • Show/hide fields based on other field values
    • Show/hide document sections based on recipient selections
    • Conditional routing (different signing path based on approval/decline)
    • Field validation rules (format, range, required conditions)
  • Collaborative Fields: Multiple recipients can fill the same field (last edit wins or merge)
  • Supplemental Documents: Attach additional documents that don't require signing (terms, disclosures)
  • Auto-Place: AI-based automatic field placement using anchor text strings in document
  • Drag-and-drop field placement on document pages
  • Responsive Signing: Fields adapt for mobile signing experience

21.2 Tab 2: Templates & Bulk Operations

Page: Envelope Template Manager

  • Fields Template Name, Description, Documents, Recipients (roles, not specific people), Fields/Tabs, Default Email Subject/Message, Folder, Shared (Y/N), Last Modified, Usage Count
  • Buttons Create Template Edit Clone Delete Share Use Template Preview Organize in Folder Export Import
  • Features:
  • Reusable envelope templates with pre-placed fields
  • Role-based recipients (e.g., "Client Signer", "PM Approver") — specific people assigned at send time
  • Template folders for organization (by module, by document type, by entity)
  • Shared templates across organization
  • Template lock (prevent modification by non-admins)
  • Template usage analytics (most used, average completion time)

Page: Bulk Send

  • Fields Template, Recipient List (CSV upload or manual), Personalization Fields (merge data per recipient), Send Date, Status
  • Buttons Select Template Upload Recipient CSV Map Fields Preview Sample Send All Schedule View Progress Cancel Remaining
  • Features:
  • Send same document to hundreds of recipients simultaneously
  • CSV-based recipient import with field personalization (name, title, amount, etc.)
  • Merge fields populated from CSV data or ERP data
  • Progress tracking dashboard (sent, delivered, signed, declined)
  • Bulk void/resend capability
  • Use cases: annual policy acknowledgments, NDA distribution, benefit enrollment, safety certifications

Page: PowerForms (Self-Service Signing)

  • Fields PowerForm Name, Template, URL, Active (Y/N), Max Signers, Signer Authentication, Redirect URL, Branding
  • Buttons Create PowerForm Generate URL Activate Deactivate View Submissions Set Authentication Configure Redirect
  • Features:
  • Public-facing self-service signing URLs (no account required)
  • Signer fills in their details and signs without sender initiation
  • Use cases: vendor registration, NDA signing, safety acknowledgment, visitor agreements
  • Configurable authentication (email verification, access code, phone SMS)
  • Redirect to custom URL after signing completion
  • Submission tracking and analytics

21.3 Tab 3: Identity Verification & Authentication

Page: Signer Authentication Configuration

  • Fields Authentication Method, Required Level, Configuration, Fallback Method, Cost per Verification
  • Buttons Configure Methods Set Default Level Test Verification View Usage Report
  • Features:
  • Authentication Methods (DocuSign ID Verification):
    • Email access verification (default — signer must access email to get link)
    • Access code (sender-defined PIN sent via separate channel)
    • SMS/Phone verification (one-time code sent via SMS or voice call)
    • Knowledge-Based Authentication (KBA) — identity quiz from public records
    • Government ID Check — photo ID upload + selfie match (AI-powered facial recognition)
    • Video verification — live video identity confirmation
    • eNotarization — full notary verification workflow
  • Configurable authentication levels per document type (higher value = stronger verification)
  • Multi-factor authentication chaining (e.g., email + SMS + ID check for high-value contracts)
  • Authentication audit trail (which method used, timestamp, result)

21.4 Tab 4: Digital Certificate & PKI Management

Page: Certificate Authority Management

  • Fields Certificate ID, Owner, Type (X.509), Issuer (Internal CA/External CA), Issue Date, Expiry Date, Status (Active/Revoked/Expired/Suspended), Key Size, Algorithm, Serial Number, Thumbprint
  • Buttons Issue Certificate Renew Revoke Suspend View Chain Download Import External Export View CRL
  • Features:
  • PKI-based digital signatures with X.509 certificates for non-repudiation
  • Internal Certificate Authority (CA) management
  • External CA integration (DigiCert, GlobalSign, Entrust)
  • Certificate lifecycle management (issue, renew, revoke, suspend)
  • HSM storage for private keys (Azure Key Vault HSM, FIPS 140-2 Level 2+)
  • Trusted Timestamping Authority (TSA) per RFC 3161
  • Certificate Revocation List (CRL) management
  • PAdES (PDF Advanced Electronic Signatures) for long-term validation
  • XAdES/CAdES for XML/CMS-based signatures
  • Qualified Electronic Signature (QES) support for eIDAS compliance

21.5 Tab 5: Signing Experience & Branding

Page: Signing Experience

  • Features:
  • In-browser signing (no app/plugin required)
  • Signature methods: Draw (mouse/touch/stylus), Type (select font), Upload (image), Adopt (saved signature)
  • Mobile-responsive signing experience (optimized for phone/tablet)
  • In-person signing mode (signer signs on sender's device, hand-off between signers)
  • Guided signing (next-field highlighting, required field enforcement, progress indicator)
  • Decline to sign (with required reason)
  • Assign to another (redirect to different signer)
  • Print & Sign option (print, sign physically, upload scanned copy)
  • Offline signing (download, sign, upload)
  • Multi-language signing experience (Arabic, English, Japanese, Greek, Italian, Hindi, French)

Page: Brand & Email Customization

  • Fields Brand Name, Logo, Color Scheme, Email Header/Footer, Signing Page Header, Button Colors, Disclaimer Text, Active (Y/N)
  • Buttons Create Brand Edit Preview Set Default Assign to Entity Clone
  • Features:
  • Custom branding per entity (logo, colors, fonts)
  • Custom email templates (signing request, reminder, completion)
  • Custom signing page branding
  • Disclaimer/legal text per jurisdiction
  • Multi-brand support (different brands for different entities/projects)

21.6 Tab 6: Remote Online Notarization (RON)

21.7 Tab 7: Audit Trail & Compliance

Page: Certificate of Completion

  • Fields Envelope ID, Document Title, Sender, Recipients, Events (chronological list), Timestamps, IP Addresses, Authentication Methods, Signature Images, Tamper Seal Status
  • Buttons View Certificate Download Certificate Verify Tamper Seal Export Audit Trail View Full History
  • Features:
  • Certificate of Completion (DocuSign-Style):
    • Every envelope generates a tamper-evident Certificate of Completion
    • Chronological event log: created, sent, delivered, viewed, signed, completed
    • Per-signer details: name, email, IP address, timestamp, authentication method, signature image
    • Digital hash (SHA-256) tamper seal — any modification invalidates the certificate
    • Downloadable as PDF attached to signed document
  • Legal Compliance:
    • UAE Federal Law 46/2021 (Electronic Transactions and Trust Services)
    • US ESIGN Act and UETA
    • EU eIDAS Regulation (Simple/Advanced/Qualified Electronic Signatures)
    • Japan Act on Electronic Signatures and Authentication Business
    • UK Electronic Communications Act 2000
    • FedRAMP compliance for government contracts
    • HIPAA compliance for healthcare documents
    • SOC 2 Type II audit compliance
  • Retention: signed documents + audit trail stored per EDMS retention policies (Section 12.12)

§22. Module 18: PDF Engine & Document Generation — Full Bluebeam Revu-Style Platform

Purpose: Enterprise PDF creation, markup, measurement, real-time collaboration, batch processing, quantity takeoff, document comparison, and punch list management across all ERP modules. Replicates the complete Bluebeam Revu feature set natively within the ERP — providing construction-grade PDF tools purpose-built for AEC workflows while also serving as the PDF generation backbone for every module. This module eliminates the need for external PDF markup tools (Bluebeam Revu, Adobe Acrobat Pro, Foxit PhantomPDF) by providing calibrated measurement, Studio-style collaboration sessions, batch automation, and quantity takeoff with direct BOQ integration.

M365 SharePoint for PDF storage and version control. OneDrive for personal markup libraries. Outlook for PDF distribution and markup notifications. Teams for Studio session invitations and markup review meetings. Power BI for document analytics, markup statistics, and quantity takeoff dashboards. Power Automate for batch processing triggers and approval workflows.

Key Personas: Project Managers, Architects, Engineers, Quantity Surveyors, Field Inspectors, Estimators, Superintendents, Document Controllers, Punch List Managers, Review Coordinators

Tech PDF.js + WebGL for high-performance rendering, PDFLib for generation, Canvas 2D/WebGL for markup layers, Geometry engine (area/linear/volume/count calculations), SignalR for real-time collaboration, Azure Blob for archival storage, React template designer, Azure Computer Vision for OCR/AI features, IndexedDB for offline markup cache, Web Workers for batch processing

    • Subject (category for filtering/sorting)
    • Label (custom display text)
    • Color (full color picker with 16 preset colors)
    • Opacity (0-100%)
    • Line Width (1-20 pt)
    • Line Style (solid, dashed, dotted, dash-dot)
    • Fill Color and Fill Opacity
    • Font Family, Size, Bold, Italic
    • Layer assignment
    • Locked/Unlocked status
    • Custom data fields (key-value pairs)
    • Author and timestamp (auto-populated)
  • Markup Management:
    • Markups List panel (sortable table of all markups with columns: Subject, Label, Author, Date, Status, Page, Color, Layer, Comments, Checked)
    • Filter markups by: Author, Subject, Color, Status, Date Range, Page, Layer, Type
    • Sort markups by any column
    • Group by: Subject, Author, Page, Status, Color
    • Bulk operations: Select All, Delete Selected, Change Status, Change Color, Lock/Unlock
    • Markup count summary by type/author/status
    • Export Markups List to CSV/Excel with all properties and coordinates
    • Import markups from XFDF (Adobe/Bluebeam compatibility format)
    • Export markups as XFDF for interoperability
    • Copy/Paste markups between documents
    • Markup recovery (undo history preserved per session, auto-save every 60 seconds)
  • Markup Sets:
    • Create named markup sets (e.g., "Structural Review," "MEP Comments," "Punch List Items")
    • Toggle visibility per markup set
    • Lock entire markup set to prevent edits
    • Merge markup sets from multiple reviewers
    • Snapshot markup set (freeze as image layer)
    • Markup set permissions (per-user edit/view/none)

Page: Tool Chest & Profiles (Replaces Bluebeam Tool Chest)

  • Fields Profile Name, Description, Tool Set Name, Tool Count, Category, Shared (Y/N), Created By, Last Modified
  • Buttons Create Profile Edit Profile Clone Import Profile Export Profile Set as Default Create Tool Set Share Profile Manage Tool Chest
  • Features:
  • Tool Chest (Reusable Markup Library):
    • Save any markup as a reusable tool in the Tool Chest
    • Organize tools into named Tool Sets (e.g., "Electrical Symbols," "Structural Comments," "Punch List Items," "Fire Protection")
    • Tool properties saved: markup type, color, size, line style, text content, subject, custom data
    • Drag-and-drop tools from Tool Chest onto document
    • Shared Tool Chests (organization-wide standard tools)
    • Personal Tool Chests (individual user tools)
    • Import/Export Tool Chest as .btx files (Bluebeam compatibility) or JSON
    • Tool Chest synchronization across devices
  • Profiles (Workspace Configurations):
    • Save complete workspace layout as Profile: toolbar arrangement, panel positions, default tools, shortcuts
    • Pre-built profiles: Construction, Estimation, Punch List, Design Review, Submittal Review, Field Inspection
    • Switch between profiles with single click
    • Profile includes: visible toolbars, panel layout, default markup properties, measurement settings, keyboard shortcuts
    • Organization-managed profiles pushed to all users
  • Recent Tools Panel:
    • Last 20 used markup tools for quick access
    • Pinned favorite tools (always visible)
    • Quick-apply last used tool (keyboard shortcut: Space)
  • Hatch Patterns & Fill Library:
    • 50+ standard architectural hatch patterns (concrete, earth, steel, wood, insulation, brick, stone, glass, etc.)
    • Custom hatch pattern creation
    • Hatch scale and rotation controls
    • Apply hatch fill to any closed shape markup

22.3 Tab 3: Calibrated Measurement Tools

Page: Measurement & Calibration Workspace

  • Fields Calibration Scale, Unit System (Imperial/Metric), Drawing Scale (1:50, 1:100, 1/4"=1'-0", etc.), Precision (decimal places), Active Measurement Type, Snap Settings, Measurement Count
  • Buttons Calibrate Set Scale Reset Calibration Switch Units Measurement Summary Export Measurements Link to BOQ Verify Calibration
  • Features:
  • Scale Calibration:
    • Two-point calibration (click two points, enter known distance)
    • Multi-page calibration (set different scales per page for multi-scale drawings)
    • Auto-detect scale from drawing title block (AI-powered)
    • Calibration verification tool (measure known dimension to confirm accuracy)
    • Scale groups (group pages with same scale for batch calibration)
    • Calibration templates (save and apply common scales: 1/4"=1'-0", 1/8"=1'-0", 1:50, 1:100, 1:200)
    • Warning indicator when page is not calibrated
  • Linear Measurement Tools:
    • Distance — Point-to-point straight line measurement
    • Perimeter — Multi-segment path measurement (sum of all segments)
    • Polyline Length — Continuous multi-point length measurement
    • Diameter — Circle/pipe diameter measurement
    • Radius — Arc/circle radius measurement
    • Arc Length — Measurement along curved path
    • Display: Individual segment lengths + total length
    • Snap to endpoints, midpoints, intersections
    • Measurement label auto-placement with leader lines
  • Area Measurement Tools:
    • Rectangular Area — Click-and-drag rectangle area
    • Polygonal Area — Multi-point polygon with auto-close
    • Elliptical Area — Oval/circular area measurement
    • Freehand Area — Freehand traced area boundary
    • Cutout/Void Support — Subtract inner shapes from outer area (e.g., room area minus columns)
    • Area displayed in: SF, SM, SY, acres, hectares
    • Fill color/hatch for measured areas (visual differentiation by material/trade)
  • Volume Measurement Tools:
    • Area × Depth calculation for concrete pours, excavation, fill
    • Depth/height entry per measurement
    • Volume displayed in: CF, CM, CY, gallons, liters
    • Automatic waste factor application (user-configurable %)
  • Count Measurement Tools:
    • Count Tool — Click to place numbered markers for counting items
    • Count by category (doors, windows, fixtures, outlets, sprinkler heads)
    • Color-coded count groups
    • Auto-increment numbering
    • Count summary table by category
    • Symbol recognition assist (AI identifies similar symbols on drawing)
  • Angle Measurement:
    • Three-point angle measurement
    • Display in degrees, radians, or slope ratio
  • Measurement Display & Formatting:
    • Dynamic measurement labels attached to markup
    • Configurable label format: value only, value + unit, value + description
    • Leader line with measurement callout
    • Measurement color coding by trade/category
    • Font size and style for measurement labels
    • Show/hide individual measurement labels
  • Measurement Summary & Export:
    • Measurement Summary panel (table of all measurements with: Description, Type, Value, Unit, Page, Category, Cost Link)
    • Filter measurements by type, page, category, author
    • Group by page, category, or type
    • Export to Excel/CSV with all columns
    • Direct BOQ Link — Push measurements to Estimation module (Section 10) as quantity takeoff line items
    • Cost Column — Optional unit cost and total cost calculation per measurement
    • Running totals by category (e.g., total linear feet of conduit, total SF of drywall)
  • Snap & Precision Settings:
    • Snap to Markup (snap to existing markup endpoints)
    • Snap to Content (snap to detected lines/corners in PDF content)
    • Snap to Grid (configurable grid overlay)
    • Ortho mode (constrain to horizontal/vertical/45° angles)
    • Precision override per measurement (temporary decimal place change)
  • AI
  • AI Auto-Count — Automatically detect and count symbols on construction drawings (doors, windows, fixtures, outlets, sprinkler heads) using computer vision
  • AI Scale Detector — Read title block and auto-detect drawing scale
  • AI Measurement Validator — Flag measurements that seem unreasonable based on drawing context

22.4 Tab 4: Studio Sessions — Real-Time Collaboration (Replaces Bluebeam Studio)

Page: Studio Session Management

  • Fields Session Name, Session ID, Host, Status (Active/Paused/Closed/Archived), Created Date, Document Count, Participant Count, Deadline, Description, Permissions Template, Auto-Flatten (Y/N), Notification Settings
  • Buttons Create Session Join Session Invite Participants Add Documents Start Session Pause Session End Session Archive Session View Session Report Export All Markups Session Settings
  • Features:
  • Studio Sessions (Real-Time Collaboration):
    • Host creates session and uploads one or more PDFs
    • Invite internal users (ERP users) and external participants (via email link)
    • Real-time multi-user markup on shared documents
    • See other users' cursors and active markups in real-time (SignalR WebSocket)
    • Markup appears instantly on all connected clients
    • Per-document permissions: Markup & View / View Only / No Access
    • Per-user markup colors (auto-assigned or user-selected)
    • Session chat panel (real-time text chat alongside document)
    • Session activity log (who did what, when)
    • Session deadline with countdown timer
    • Automatic session summary email on close
    • Session recordings (timeline of all markup activity)
  • Session Permissions Model:
    • Host (full control: manage participants, documents, settings)
    • Editor (add/edit own markups, view all markups)
    • Viewer (view-only, can add comments but not markups)
    • External Guest (limited access via secure link, no ERP account needed)
    • Permission templates: Design Review, Punch List Walkthrough, Submittal Review, QA Inspection
  • Studio Projects (Persistent Collaboration):
    • Long-running collaboration spaces (project lifecycle)
    • Folder structure within Studio Project
    • Document check-in/check-out (prevents simultaneous editing conflicts)
    • Version control with markup history per version
    • Automatic file sync when documents are updated in EDMS (Section 12)
    • Role-based folder permissions
  • Session Workflow Integration:
    • Link Studio Session to ERP workflow (e.g., submittal review, RFI response, change order review)
    • Session completion triggers next workflow step
    • Markup status rollup (all markups resolved → session auto-complete)
    • Reviewers must mark all comments as "Resolved" or "Accepted" before session can close
  • Markup Conflict Resolution:
    • Visual indicators when multiple users markup same area
    • Markup threading (reply to specific markup with comments)
    • Status workflow per markup: Open → In Review → Resolved → Verified → Closed
    • Markup assignments (assign markup to specific user for action)
    • Due dates on individual markups
  • Offline Session Support:
    • Download session documents for offline markup (PWA)
    • Sync markups when back online
    • Conflict resolution for concurrent offline edits
  • M365 Session invitations via Outlook; Teams channel notification for session activity; SharePoint sync for session documents; Power Automate for session lifecycle triggers

Page: Markup Review & Status Tracking

  • Fields Markup ID, Subject, Author, Assignee, Status (Open/In Review/Resolved/Verified/Closed/Rejected), Priority (Critical/Major/Minor/Informational), Due Date, Response, Resolution Notes, Linked Record
  • Buttons Filter Assign Change Status Bulk Update Add Response Link to RFI Link to Change Order Export Status Report Send Reminders
  • Features:
  • Comprehensive markup status dashboard with KPIs: Total, Open, Resolved, Overdue
  • Markup aging report (days open by priority)
  • Assignee workload view (markups per person)
  • Markup-to-RFI conversion (create RFI from markup with screenshot and coordinates)
  • Markup-to-Change-Order linking
  • Markup-to-Punch-List conversion
  • Email notifications on status changes
  • Escalation rules (auto-escalate if overdue by X days)

22.5 Tab 5: Document Comparison & Overlay

Page: Document Comparison Workspace

  • Fields Document A (Base), Document B (Revised), Comparison Type, Alignment Mode, Sensitivity, Difference Count, Page Mapping
  • Buttons Select Documents Start Comparison Align Pages Set Sensitivity Toggle Differences Export Comparison Next Difference Previous Difference Create Markup from Difference Save Comparison
  • Features:
  • Overlay Comparison (Replaces Bluebeam Overlay):
    • Two documents overlaid with transparency controls
    • Color coding: Document A in one color, Document B in another, common content in third color
    • Transparency slider for each document (0-100%)
    • Pan/zoom synchronized between documents
    • Alignment tools: Auto-align (by content matching), manual alignment (pick 2-3 reference points), page-by-page mapping for documents with different page counts
    • Blink compare mode (rapidly toggle between A and B)
  • Cloud Comparison:
    • Automatic detection of differences between two document versions
    • Differences highlighted with revision clouds (auto-generated)
    • Difference categories: Added content (green), Removed content (red), Modified content (yellow)
    • Difference summary count by page
    • Navigate between differences with Next/Previous buttons
    • Filter differences by type (text changes, graphic changes, dimension changes)
    • Sensitivity control (ignore minor rendering differences)
  • Side-by-Side Comparison:
    • Two documents displayed side by side with synchronized navigation
    • Linked zoom and pan (move one document, other follows)
    • Independent zoom option for different scale documents
    • Difference highlighting in both views
  • Multi-Version Comparison:
    • Compare 3+ versions of same document
    • Version timeline with thumbnail previews
    • Cumulative difference tracking across versions
  • Comparison Report:
    • PDF report summarizing all detected differences
    • Screenshot of each difference with page number and coordinates
    • Comparison statistics (total pages compared, differences found, categories)
    • Export comparison results to EDMS (Section 12) as a transmittal attachment
  • AI
  • AI Difference Classifier — Categorizes differences as: dimensional change, text change, added element, removed element, moved element, scaled element
  • AI Critical Change Detector — Flags differences in critical areas (structural, fire safety, egress) with high-priority alerts

22.6 Tab 6: Batch Processing & Automation

Page: Batch Processing Manager

  • Fields Batch Name, Process Type, Input Files (list), Output Location, Settings, Status (Queued/Processing/Complete/Failed), Progress (%), Start Time, End Time, File Count, Success/Failure Count
  • Buttons Create Batch Add Files Configure Settings Start Pause Resume Cancel View Log Retry Failed Download Results Schedule
  • Features:
  • Batch Link (Hyperlink Automation):
    • Auto-create hyperlinks between drawing sheets based on reference callouts
    • Detect callout bubbles (e.g., "See Detail A/S2.03") and auto-link to target sheet/page
    • Batch process entire drawing set (hundreds of sheets) in single operation
    • Link report showing all created/broken links
  • Batch Flatten:
    • Flatten all markups into PDF content (makes markups permanent)
    • Selective flatten: by markup set, by author, by status (resolved only)
    • Archive original markup data before flattening
    • Flatten for distribution (keep original for internal use)
  • Batch Stamp:
    • Apply stamps to multiple documents simultaneously
    • Stamp placement: header, footer, center, custom coordinates
    • Dynamic stamp content: date, user, document number, revision
    • Stamp on specific pages: all, first, last, odd, even, page range
    • Classification stamps for CUI/ITAR documents
  • Batch OCR (Optical Character Recognition):
    • Convert scanned PDFs to searchable/selectable text
    • Language support: English, Arabic, Japanese, Greek, Italian
    • OCR quality settings: Speed / Balanced / Accuracy
    • Auto-deskew and image cleanup before OCR
    • Batch process hundreds of scanned documents
  • Batch Print:
    • Print multiple documents with consistent settings
    • Print set management (group related sheets for printing)
    • Paper size mapping (auto-detect from PDF page size)
    • Scale-to-fit or actual size options
    • Print queue management with priority
  • Batch Combine/Split:
    • Merge multiple PDFs into single document
    • Split PDF by page range, bookmarks, or file size
    • Reorder pages across multiple documents
    • Insert pages from one document into another at specific position
  • Batch Reduce File Size:
    • Optimize PDF file size (downsample images, remove metadata, compress streams)
    • Quality presets: Web (smallest), Print (medium), Archive (high quality)
    • Batch optimize entire project document set
  • Batch Headers/Footers:
    • Add consistent headers/footers to multiple documents
    • Dynamic content: filename, date, page number, project number, classification
    • Position and formatting controls
  • Batch Watermark:
    • Apply watermarks to multiple documents
    • Text or image watermarks
    • Classification-based automatic watermarking (CUI documents get CUI watermark)
  • Batch Export:
    • Export markups from multiple documents to single summary
    • Export measurement data from multiple sheets to single Excel/CSV
    • Export images from PDFs
  • Scheduled Batch Jobs:
    • Schedule recurring batch operations (nightly flatten, weekly optimization)
    • Trigger-based batches (on document upload to EDMS, on status change)
    • Batch job templates (save and reuse common batch configurations)
  • M365 Batch output filed to SharePoint; Power Automate triggers for batch jobs; Notification via Outlook on completion/failure

22.7 Tab 7: Quantity Takeoff & Estimation Link

Page: Quantity Takeoff Workspace

  • Fields Takeoff Name, Project, Drawing Set, Status (In Progress/Submitted/Approved), Estimator, Date, Total Line Items, Linked Estimate ID, Drawing Count
  • Buttons Create Takeoff Open Drawings Calibrate Start Measuring View Summary Export to Estimation Export to Excel Submit for Review Approve Link to BOQ
  • Features:
  • Integrated Takeoff Workflow:
    • Open construction drawings directly in measurement workspace
    • Calibrate scale per sheet (or use auto-detected scale)
    • Measure quantities using all measurement tools from 22.3
    • Assign measurements to cost codes (MasterFormat CSI from Section 10.1)
    • Color-code measurements by trade/division
    • Running quantity summary panel (live totals as you measure)
  • Takeoff Categories & Organization:
    • Organize takeoff by: CSI Division, Trade, Location/Zone, Phase, Bid Item
    • Custom category hierarchies
    • Multi-level grouping (Division → Section → Sub-section)
    • Takeoff templates (pre-configured categories for common project types)
  • Takeoff Conditions (Replaces Bluebeam Quantity Link):
    • Define "conditions" (measurement presets with name, type, color, cost code)
    • Example conditions: "4" Concrete Slab" (area, gray fill, 03 30 00), "3/4" EMT Conduit" (linear, blue, 26 05 33)
    • Switch between conditions while measuring (no reconfiguration needed)
    • Condition library saved per project or organization-wide
    • Bi-directional sync: condition quantities flow to BOQ, BOQ updates reflect in takeoff view
  • Drawing Set Management:
    • Upload entire drawing set (hundreds of sheets)
    • Organize by discipline: Architectural, Structural, Mechanical, Electrical, Plumbing, Fire Protection, Civil, Landscape
    • Drawing index with sheet number, title, discipline, scale, revision
    • Hyperlinked drawing navigation (click callout → jump to referenced sheet)
    • Revision tracking (highlight changed areas between drawing revisions)
  • Quantity Summary & Export:
    • Detailed quantity summary table with: Condition, Description, Quantity, Unit, Page(s), Cost Code, Unit Cost, Total Cost
    • Summary by division, trade, floor, zone, phase
    • Push to Estimation Module — Direct integration with Section 10 (Estimation & Costing):
    • Auto-create BOQ line items from takeoff measurements
    • Match conditions to cost database line items
    • Sync quantities bi-directionally
    • Export to Excel with formatting and formulas
    • Export to CSV for import into external estimating tools
    • Audit trail of all quantity changes with timestamps
  • Multi-User Takeoff:
    • Multiple estimators can work on different sheets simultaneously
    • Real-time quantity totals updated across all users
    • Conflict detection when two users measure same area
    • Takeoff locking by sheet (prevent overlapping work)
  • AI
  • AI Auto-Measure — Detect and auto-measure repetitive elements (rooms, ductwork runs, pipe lengths) using drawing recognition
  • AI Quantity Validator — Compare takeoff quantities against historical project data and flag outliers
  • AI Drawing Classifier — Auto-classify uploaded drawings by discipline (Architectural/Structural/MEP) and assign to correct category

22.8 Tab 8: Punch List Management

Page: Punch List Dashboard

  • Fields Punch List Name, Project, Phase (Substantial Completion/Final/Warranty), Status (Open/In Progress/Complete), Created Date, Due Date, Total Items, Open Items, Resolved Items, Verified Items, Responsible Party, Inspector
  • Buttons Create Punch List Open on Drawing Add Items Assign Send Notifications Generate Report Export Close Punch List Archive Warranty Items
  • Features:
  • Drawing-Based Punch List Creation:
    • Open as-built or construction drawings in PDF viewer
    • Click on drawing location to create punch item (auto-captures coordinates and screenshot)
    • Numbered pin markers on drawing showing all punch items
    • Filter pin visibility by: status, trade, priority, assignee
    • Photo/video attachment per punch item (field camera integration via PWA)
    • Voice note recording per punch item (transcribed by AI)
  • Punch Item Details:
    • Item Number (auto-increment per punch list)
    • Location (Building/Floor/Room/Area — selected from drawing or typed)
    • Drawing Reference (sheet number + coordinates)
    • Category (Architectural/Structural/Mechanical/Electrical/Plumbing/Fire/Civil/Landscape/General)
    • Description (text with photo and markup)
    • Priority (Critical/Major/Minor/Cosmetic)
    • Responsible Party (Subcontractor/Trade)
    • Assigned To (specific person)
    • Due Date
    • Status Workflow: Open → Assigned → In Progress → Completed → Verified → Closed / Rejected
    • Response/Resolution notes
    • Before/After photos (side-by-side comparison)
    • Cost Impact (if punch item requires additional work/materials)
    • Linked RFI / Change Order / NCR (Non-Conformance Report)
  • Punch List Workflow:
    • Inspector creates items during walkthrough (mobile/tablet PWA)
    • Items auto-assigned to responsible subcontractor
    • Subcontractor receives email/mobile notification
    • Subcontractor completes work and uploads completion photo
    • Inspector verifies and marks as Verified or Rejected with reason
    • Back-charge tracking for punch items not completed by deadline
    • Escalation rules (auto-notify superintendent if overdue)
  • Punch List Reports:
    • Summary by status, trade, priority, location
    • Aging report (days open)
    • Trend chart (items opened vs. closed over time)
    • Subcontractor performance scorecard (completion rate, average response time)
    • Print-ready punch list report with drawing excerpts and photos
    • Executive summary (% complete, critical items remaining)
  • Integration with Project Module (Section 7):
    • Punch list completion percentage drives project closeout milestone
    • Substantial completion certificate requires zero critical punch items
    • Final completion certificate requires zero open punch items
    • Warranty punch items tracked separately with warranty period dates
  • M365 Punch items assigned via Outlook; Status updates in Teams channel; Power BI punch list dashboards; Photos stored in SharePoint project folders

22.11 Tab 11: PDF Security & Compliance

Page: PDF Security Management

  • Fields Document, Security Level (Public/Internal/Confidential/CUI/ITAR/Classified), Encryption (None/128-bit AES/256-bit AES), Password Protection (Open/Permissions), Digital Certificate, Redaction Status, Retention Policy
  • Buttons Set Security Encrypt Redact Sanitize Apply DRM Verify Integrity Audit Access Set Retention
  • Features:
  • Encryption & Password Protection:
    • Document open password (prevent unauthorized access)
    • Permission password (control print, copy, edit, form fill)
    • AES-256 encryption for CUI/ITAR documents
    • Certificate-based encryption (X.509 certificate required to open)
  • Redaction Tools:
    • Visual redaction (black box over sensitive content)
    • Search-and-redact (find all instances of SSN pattern, account numbers, etc.)
    • Redaction verification (ensure no hidden text remains under redaction marks)
    • Redaction log (audit trail of what was redacted, by whom, when)
    • FOIA redaction workflow with exemption codes (b)(1) through (b)(9)
    • Batch redaction across multiple documents
  • Document Sanitization:
    • Remove hidden metadata (author, creation date, software, GPS coordinates)
    • Remove embedded scripts, links, and attachments
    • Remove hidden layers and optional content
    • Flatten all interactive elements
    • Sanitization report listing all removed elements
  • Digital Rights Management (DRM):
    • View-only mode (prevent print, copy, download)
    • Time-limited access (PDF expires after date/time)
    • Device-limited access (authorized devices only)
    • Watermark with viewer's identity (forensic watermark)
    • Print count limit
    • Screen capture prevention (deterrent watermark)
  • Compliance Integration:
    • CUI marking automation (banners, footers, portion marking)
    • ITAR document controls with access logging
    • CMMC Level 2 document handling compliance
    • FAR/DFARS document retention enforcement
    • Microsoft Purview sensitivity labels applied to PDFs
  • Document Integrity:
    • SHA-256 hash verification (detect tampering)
    • Digital signature verification (confirm signer identity)
    • Certificate chain validation
    • Timestamp verification (prove document existed at specific time)

22.12 Cross-Module PDF Engine Integration

The PDF Engine serves as the central document generation and markup platform for all ERP modules:

Module PDF Engine Integration
Finance (Section 5) Invoice PDF, credit note, payment voucher, financial statement generation with branded templates
HR (Section 6) Offer letter, employment contract, salary certificate, NOC, payslip, training certificate batch generation
Projects (Section 7) PSR, S-Curve, payment certificate, transmittal cover sheets, monthly reports with charts
Procurement (Section 8) Purchase order, RFQ, GRN, contract PDFs with terms and conditions
Proposals (Section 9) Technical/cost proposal compilation, compliance matrix, past performance volumes
Estimation (Section 10) Quantity takeoff integration, estimate report generation, BOQ export
Field Operations (Section 11) Inspection reports, daily logs, safety checklists, RFI responses with drawing markups
EDMS (Section 12) Document viewing, markup, transmittal attachments, review workflow documents
QMS (Section 13) NCR reports, CAPA documents, audit reports, calibration certificates
Contracts (Section 14) Contract documents, modifications, CLINs, CDRL deliverable formatting
ITSM (Section 15) Ticket report PDFs, SLA performance reports, change request documents
HSE (Section 16) Incident reports, safety inspection forms, training records, compliance certificates
Inventory (Section 20) Stock reports, receiving documents, inventory valuation reports
Signatures (Section 21) Signed document PDFs with certificate chain, Certificate of Completion
EAM (Section 23) Asset register reports, maintenance work orders, inspection certificates
CRM (Section 24) Customer reports, proposal summaries, service agreements

22.13 PDF Engine — AI Features Complete Catalog

AI Feature Description
AI Auto-Count Automatically detect and count symbols on construction drawings using computer vision
AI Scale Detector Read title block and auto-detect drawing scale for calibration
AI Measurement Validator Flag measurements that seem unreasonable based on drawing context and historical data
AI Auto-Measure Detect and auto-measure repetitive elements (rooms, ductwork, pipes)
AI Quantity Validator Compare takeoff quantities against historical project data and flag outliers
AI Drawing Classifier Auto-classify uploaded drawings by discipline (Architectural/Structural/MEP)
AI Difference Classifier Categorize document comparison differences by type and significance
AI Critical Change Detector Flag changes in critical areas (structural, fire safety, egress) with priority alerts
AI OCR Engine Convert scanned documents to searchable text with high accuracy
AI Template Optimizer Analyze template usage patterns and suggest layout improvements
AI Redaction Assistant Detect and suggest PII/sensitive data for redaction in documents
AI Punch List Voice-to-Text Transcribe field audio notes to structured punch list items
AI Form Auto-Fill Pre-populate form fields based on context and historical submissions
AI Document Summarizer Generate executive summaries of long PDF documents
