§23. Module 19: Enterprise Asset Management (EAM) — ALL ASSETS

Purpose: Complete lifecycle management for ALL MVL assets — not just IT equipment. This includes heavy construction equipment, vehicles/fleet, tools & instruments, office furniture, government-furnished property, leased equipment, site trailers, temporary facilities, and assets across ALL global locations. As a DoD Prime Contractor self-performing in various locations, MVL requires a unified asset management system that tracks every physical asset from procurement to disposal, including maintenance, calibration, certifications, insurance, depreciation, location transfers, and government property compliance (FAR 45 / DFARS 245).

M365 Power Apps for mobile asset scanning in the field. Power BI for asset dashboards per location, category, and depreciation. SharePoint for asset documentation (manuals, warranties, insurance certificates). Outlook for maintenance reminders and warranty expiry alerts. Teams for asset transfer approvals. Power Automate for automated maintenance scheduling and compliance alerts.

Key Personas: Asset Manager, Equipment Manager, Facility Managers, Site Superintendents, Finance (depreciation), Government Property Administrator, Fleet Manager, Warehouse/Tool Room Attendant

Tech Azure SQL for asset register, Azure IoT Hub for telemetry-connected assets, Azure Blob Storage for photos/documents, Barcode/QR/RFID scanning via Power Apps, Azure Maps for location tracking, Azure ML for predictive maintenance

23.1 Tab 1: Enterprise Asset Register (Master)

Page: Asset Master Data

  • Fields Asset ID (auto-generated with category prefix: HE- Heavy Equipment, VH- Vehicle, TL- Tool, FN- Furniture, IT- IT Asset, GF- Govt Furnished, SE- Safety Equipment, TE- Temp Equipment), Asset Name, Description, Category (Heavy Equipment/Vehicle/Power Tool/Hand Tool/Measuring Instrument/Office Furniture/IT Equipment/Safety Equipment/Temp Facility/Site Trailer/Generator/Crane/Scaffold/Formwork), Sub-Category, Make, Model, Serial Number, Year of Manufacture, Purchase Date, Purchase Cost, Purchase PO Number, Vendor/Supplier, Entity, Current Location (Country/City/Site/Building/Floor/Room/Zone), Department, Custodian, Assigned Project, Ownership Type (Company Owned/Leased/Rented/Government Furnished/Contractor Acquired), Lease/Rental Contract Reference, Insurance Policy Number, Insurance Expiry, Registration Number (for vehicles), License Plate, Certification Status, Next Calibration Date, Condition (New/Excellent/Good/Fair/Poor/Unserviceable), Operational Status (Operational/Under Maintenance/In Transit/In Storage/Decommissioned/Disposed/Lost/Stolen), Depreciation Method, Useful Life (years), Salvage Value, Current Book Value, Replacement Cost, Photo(s), QR/Barcode, GPS/IoT Tracker ID, Tags, Notes, Custom Attributes (configurable per category)
  • Buttons Add Asset Edit Assign to Project/Site Transfer Location Transfer Custodian Schedule Maintenance Schedule Calibration Update Condition Update Photo Generate QR Label Print Asset Label Send for Repair Mark Decommissioned Initiate Disposal Mark Lost/Stolen View Full History View Maintenance History View Transfer History View Depreciation Schedule Link to PO Link to Insurance Link to Certification Scan QR/Barcode Bulk Import Bulk Update Export Register View on Map Attach Document Clone Asset View Related Assets (sets)
  • Features:
  • Universal asset register across ALL categories and ALL locations
  • Multi-entity asset management (assets owned by different MVL entities)
  • Asset hierarchy (parent-child relationships: crane → attachments, vehicle → accessories)
  • Asset sets/kits (group related assets that travel together)
  • Unique QR/barcode per asset with mobile scanning
  • Photo documentation with timestamped GPS-tagged images
  • Custom attribute fields per category (e.g., engine hours for equipment, calibration range for instruments)
  • FAR 45 / DFARS 245 government property tracking integrated
  • Asset insurance tracking with expiry alerts
  • Multi-currency asset valuation (purchased in different countries)
  • AI
  • AI Asset Classifier — Auto-categorizes new assets from PO descriptions and vendor data
  • AI Duplicate Detector — Detects potential duplicate asset entries (same serial number, similar description)
  • AI Data Enricher — Auto-populates asset specifications (weight, dimensions, capacity) from manufacturer databases
  • AI Photo Condition Assessor — Analyzes uploaded asset photos using computer vision to auto-suggest condition rating (Good/Fair/Poor)
  • AI Valuation Estimator — Estimates current market value and replacement cost using market data and depreciation curves

  • AI PM Schedule Optimizer — Optimizes preventive maintenance schedules to minimize downtime during critical project periods; batches maintenance for efficiency
  • AI Maintenance Cost Analyzer — Tracks total cost of ownership per asset and identifies when repair costs exceed replacement threshold (repair-vs-replace decision support)
  • AI Technician Recommender — Suggests the best available technician based on skillset, location, workload, and past performance on similar asset types
  • AI Parts Predictor — Predicts which spare parts will be needed for upcoming PMs and auto-generates procurement requests with lead time factored in
  • AI Work Order Generator — From a simple description ("crane boom is making noise"), AI generates a complete work order with suspected cause, required parts, estimated labor hours, and priority

25.8 Module Compliance Specification (BG-4: People, Assets & Operations)

Compliance Header Specification
Business Group BG-4 — People, Assets & Operations
Data Classification Vehicle records: Internal; Driver license/medical: CUI-PRVCY + PII; GPS/telematics: Internal; Insurance docs: Internal
Primary Roles Fleet Manager (full), Driver (own vehicle + fuel log), Project Manager (fleet assignment view), Finance (cost data), Auditor (read-only), HR (driver qualification records)
SoD Requirement Vehicle assignment approval and vehicle dispatch must be different personnel for GFP or leased vehicles
Approval Gates Vehicle acquisition: Fleet Manager + Finance approval; Vehicle disposal: Fleet Manager + Finance + fixed asset write-off workflow; Driver license suspension: auto-removes assignment, HR notified
Key Audit Events Vehicle added/disposed, Driver assigned/unassigned, License expiry alert triggered, Fuel log entry created, Geofence violation detected, Insurance/registration renewal logged, GPS tracking activated/deactivated
Audit Immutability All GPS telematics events immutable; fuel anomaly flags immutable post-detection
Retention Vehicle records: asset life + 7 years post-disposal; Driver records (PII): employment + 7 years; Fuel logs: 7 years (FAR 4.703 if government project vehicles); GPS logs: 1 year rolling
Required Reports Fleet Utilization Report (monthly), Driver License Compliance Report (monthly), Fuel Cost vs Budget (monthly), Insurance & Registration Expiry Report (30/60/90-day lookahead)
NIST 800-171 Controls 3.1.1 (access control — driver data), 3.9.1 (personnel security for drivers with cleared access), 3.8.3 (media sanitation for GPS devices)
CMMC Practices AC.L2-3.1.1, PS.L2-3.9.1, MP.L1-3.8.3
Export Controls Driver PII records: HR only; GPS location history: Fleet Manager + CISO for legal discovery; No external sharing
FedRAMP Boundary ✅ GPS/IoT telemetry processed through Azure IoT Hub (GCC High); Azure Maps (GCC High)

  • AI Cost Reduction Advisor — Analyzes carrying costs and recommends: consolidation of stock, alternative materials, bulk purchasing opportunities

§33. AI & Automation Strategy — Generative AI, Agentic AI, RPA

Goal: Intelligent automation and AI-powered insights for operational excellence. Every module, every page, every workflow must incorporate automation opportunities. Three tiers of AI are deployed: Generative AI (content creation, drafting, summarization), Agentic AI (autonomous multi-step task execution), and Machine Learning / RPA (pattern recognition, predictions, robotic process automation).

Expected Outcomes: 20,000+ hours/year savings | 30% faster decisions | 95% anomaly detection | 75% of L0/L1 tickets auto-resolved | 50% reduction in manual data entry | 80% document processing automation | 165+ AI features deployed across all 36 modules

33.1 AI Architecture & Technology Stack

Layer Technology Capabilities
Generative AI Azure OpenAI Service (Government, GPT-4o) Document drafting, email composition, report narratives, proposal sections, KB article generation, contract clause drafting, meeting summaries, code documentation
Agentic AI Azure AI Agent Service + LangChain on Azure Multi-step autonomous workflows: new user provisioning (AD+Intune+Teams+Email), auto-resolution of known IT issues, end-to-end procurement workflows, automated compliance assessments, auto-generating and submitting reports
ML / Predictive Azure Machine Learning Predictive maintenance, demand forecasting, attrition prediction, risk scoring, anomaly detection, classification, regression, time-series forecasting
Computer Vision Azure Computer Vision + Custom Vision Photo-to-progress estimation, asset condition assessment, drawing change detection, receipt OCR, counterfeit part detection, safety violation detection
Document AI Azure Document Intelligence OCR, form recognition, invoice extraction, contract clause extraction, resume parsing, receipt digitization
Conversational AI Power Virtual Agents + Azure Bot Service ERP chatbot in Teams, self-service portal virtual agent, voice-enabled field queries
RPA Power Automate + Azure Logic Apps Workflow automation, data synchronization, scheduled tasks, approval routing, notification chains, legacy system integration
Copilot Integration Microsoft 365 Copilot + Graph Connectors Natural language ERP queries ("What's the SPI for Project Alpha?"), document summarization, email drafting, meeting action items
Search AI Azure Cognitive Search + Semantic Ranking Semantic search across KB, contracts, proposals, documents — understands intent, not just keywords

33.2 AI Automation Principles

  1. Every manual activity must be assessed for automation — If a human is doing it repetitively, AI should do it or assist
  2. Three automation tiers per activity: - Tier 1 — Full Automation (Agentic): AI completes the task end-to-end without human intervention (e.g., auto-resolve password resets, auto-provision new users, auto-approve standard purchases under $500) - Tier 2 — AI-Assisted (Copilot): AI drafts/suggests, human reviews and approves (e.g., AI drafts proposal section, human edits and approves; AI suggests risk score, human validates) - Tier 3 — AI-Monitored (ML): AI watches patterns and alerts humans to anomalies or predictions (e.g., AI predicts equipment failure, alerts maintenance team; AI detects fraud pattern, alerts finance)
  3. Every approval workflow gets AI Smart Digest — AI batches routine approvals, highlights exceptions
  4. Every data entry field gets AI pre-fill — Historical data, contextual data, and OCR populate fields
  5. Every report gets AI narrative — Numbers plus AI-generated insights and recommendations
  6. Every search gets semantic understanding — Natural language queries across all modules

33.4 AI Phased Deployment Roadmap

Phase 1: Quick Wins — RPA & OCR (0-3 months)

  • Deploy high-impact, low-complexity automations to generate immediate value
  • Receipt OCR and auto-expense categorization
  • AI Email Classifier for structured data extraction
  • AI Smart Digest for approval batching
  • Automated Journal Entry Creation from sub-modules
  • Power Automate workflows for all approval chains
  • AI Ticket Classifier for ITSM
  • Auto-routing rules for all modules
  • Target: 2,000+ hours/year saved

Phase 2: AI Foundation — ML Models (3-9 months)

  • Build data foundation and deploy machine learning models
  • AI Budget Advisor, AI Rate Anomaly Detector, AI Hedging Advisor
  • AI Opportunity Matcher, AI Win Probability Scorer
  • Payment fraud detection, AI Fuel Anomaly Detector
  • AI Compliance Predictor, AI Demand Forecaster
  • AI Predictive Maintenance for equipment
  • Attrition Prediction, AI Escalation Predictor
  • Target: 4,000+ hours/year saved, 25% faster decisions

Phase 3: Generative AI — Content Creation (9-15 months)

  • Deploy Generative AI for document drafting and summarization
  • AI Proposal Writer, AI Contract Drafter
  • AI KB Article Generator, AI Report Narrator
  • AI Financial Narrator, AI Progress Narrator
  • AI Work Order Generator, AI Communication Drafter
  • AI Implementation Plan Generator
  • M365 Copilot integration for NL ERP queries
  • Target: 7,000+ hours/year saved, 40% reduction in manual data entry

Phase 4: Agentic AI — Autonomous Operations (15-24 months)

  • Deploy fully autonomous AI agents for end-to-end task execution
  • AI Auto-Resolver for ITSM (70% of L0/L1 tickets)
  • AI Auto-Provisioner for new user setup
  • AI Invoice Processor (end-to-end AP automation)
  • AI Onboarding Orchestrator
  • AI Threat Responder with auto-containment
  • AI Obligation Tracker for contracts
  • AI Risk Scanner for continuous monitoring
  • AI CMDB Auditor for continuous validation
  • Target: 9,000+ hours/year saved, 70% L0/L1 auto-resolution, 95% anomaly detection

§34. Implementation Roadmap

34.1 Phased Deployment

Phase 1: Critical Compliance (0-6 months)

  • Deploy modules required for immediate DoD compliance and audit readiness
  • Modules: Finance (DCAA), Security (CMMC/NIST), User & Access Management, Audit & Compliance, Document Control
  • Key Deliverables:
  • DCAA accounting system compliance
  • NIST 800-171 control implementation
  • CMMC V2 Level 2 readiness
  • Audit logging and trail
  • FedRAMP security boundary establishment

Phase 2: Quality & Safety (6-12 months)

  • Implement quality and safety systems required for operations
  • Modules: QMS (ISO 9001/AS9100), HSE (OSHA/EM385-1-1), Government Property, Counterfeit Parts Prevention
  • Key Deliverables:
  • ISO 9001/AS9100 QMS implementation
  • OSHA compliance and EM385-1-1 adherence
  • FAR 45 government property tracking
  • DFARS counterfeit parts prevention

Phase 3: Risk & Resilience (12-18 months)

  • Deploy risk management and business continuity frameworks
  • Modules: SCRM, Facility Security (NISPOM), Backup & DR, Business Continuity, Small Business Compliance
  • Key Deliverables:
  • NIST 800-161 SCRM implementation
  • NISPOM facility security
  • BC/COOP planning and testing
  • DR compliance (NIST CP-9/CP-10)

§35. External System Replacement Matrix

Principle: Every capability previously served by external tools is built natively within the MVL ERP. This eliminates integration complexity, reduces security surface area, ensures FedRAMP boundary consistency, and provides a unified user experience across all functions.

This document contains 8,500+ lines of detailed specifications covering 26 core modules + 10 DoD modules = 36 total modules, 36 native capability engines, 1,100+ activities/functions, 220+ AI features (Generative AI, Agentic AI, ML, Computer Vision, RPA), 550+ pages/views, 4,500+ fields, 4,000+ buttons/actions, complete M365 Graph API integration strategy, and per-page/per-button/per-field detail. USG Compliance Additions (2026-02): §4.5 Data Classification & Retention Registry (master record classification for all 26 modules); Business Group TOC restructure (6 groups: Finance & Contracts, BD & Capture, Project Delivery, People/Assets/Operations, IT & Security, Platform & Governance); USG Module Compliance Specification blocks added to §16 SIEM, §17 MDM, §18 Backup, §19 Infra, §20 DevOps, §25 Fleet, §26 Warehouse, §28 Compliance, §29 Travel, §30 Facilities — each covering: Business Group, Data Classification, Role Matrix, SoD Rules, Approval Gates, Audit Events, Retention Rules, NIST 800-171 Controls, CMMC Practices, Export Controls, FedRAMP Boundary confirmation. It replicates the full capabilities of 13 industry-leading tools natively: Freshservice ITSM (including Self-Service Portal, Virtual Agent, Gamification), Procore (including Safety & Quality), Deltek CostPoint (including EVM, DCAA, 22+ Revenue Formulas), Oracle Primavera P6 EPPM, RIB CANDY/CCS, PlanSwift 11 Pro, RSMeans (built as native cost database, NOT API connection), Oracle Aconex (full EDMS with document register, transmittals, correspondence/mail, review workflows, drawing management, packages, BIM coordination, closeout/handover, 16 AI features), DocuSign (envelope-based signing, 11 recipient roles, PowerForms, bulk send, RON, identity verification, PKI certificates, 6 AI features), Bluebeam Revu (35+ markup types, calibrated measurements, Studio collaboration, batch processing, quantity takeoff, punch list, document comparison, 14 AI features), GovWin IQ (pre-RFP intelligence, agency/competitor/incumbent analysis, FPDS/USASpending data, market intelligence, capture management, 14 AI features), Rippling (unified HR+IT+Finance, employee graph, automatic provisioning/deprovisioning, MDM, app management, spend management, workflow automation, 14 AI features), and Gordian/eGordian (Job Order Contracting with UPB management, Facility Condition Assessment, capital planning, deferred maintenance, cooperative procurement, 7 AI features). All modules communicate through the centralized EDMS as the Common Data Environment (CDE). It serves as the definitive agent instruction set for building the MVL Group ERP platform.
